  return {
    plugins: [react(), tailwindcss()],
    resolve: {
      alias: {
        '@': path.resolve(__dirname, '.'),
      },
    },
    server: {
      // HMR is disabled in AI Studio via DISABLE_HMR env var.
      // Do not modifyâfile watching is disabled to prevent flickering during agent edits.
      hmr: process.env.DISABLE_HMR !== 'true',

=== FILE: server.ts ===
import express from 'express';
import path from 'path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
import { createServer as createViteServer } from 'vite';
import { GoogleGenAI, Type } from '@google/genai';
import * as dotenv from 'dotenv';

dotenv.config();

const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);

async function startServer() {
  const app = express();
  const PORT = 3000;

  app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));

  // Initialize Gemini Client safely
  const apiKey = process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY;
  const ai = new GoogleGenAI({
    apiKey: apiKey || '',
    httpOptions: {
      headers: {
        'User-Agent': 'aistudio-build',
      },
    },
  });

  // Robust retry helper with multi-model fallback to deal with transient 503 errors and high-demand rate limiting gracefully
  const callGeminiWithRetry = async (
    contents: any, 
    systemInstruction?: string, 
    responseSchema?: any, 
    retries = 5, 
    delayMs = 1000
  ) => {
    const modelsToTry = ['gemini-3.5-flash', 'gemini-2.5-flash', 'gemini-1.5-flash'];
    let lastError: any = null;

    for (const modelName of modelsToTry) {
      let currentDelay = delayMs;
      for (let i = 0; i < retries; i++) {
        try {
          console.log(`Calling Gemini using model: ${modelName} (attempt ${i + 1}/${retries})...`);
          
          const reqConfig: any = {};
          if (systemInstruction) {
            reqConfig.systemInstruction = systemInstruction;
          }
          if (responseSchema) {
            reqConfig.responseMimeType = 'application/json';
            reqConfig.responseSchema = responseSchema;
          }

          return await ai.models.generateContent({
            model: modelName,
            contents: contents,
            config: reqConfig
          });
        } catch (err: any) {
          lastError = err;
          const errMsg = err?.message || String(err);
          const isTransient = errMsg.includes('503') || 
                              errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('temporarily') || 
                              errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('high demand') || 
                              errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('unavailable') || 
                              errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('rate limit') ||
                              errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('resource exhausted') ||
                              errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('overloaded');
          if (isTransient && i < retries - 1) {
            console.warn(`Gemini call failed with transient error: "${errMsg}". Retrying in ${currentDelay}ms (attempt ${i + 1}/${retries})...`);
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, currentDelay));
            currentDelay *= 2; // exponential backoff
            continue;
          }
          console.warn(`Model ${modelName} failed. Error: "${errMsg}".`);
          break; // break retry loop to try the fallback model immediately
        }
      }
    }
    throw lastError;
  };

  // API: AI generate screenplay script from storyboard slides
  app.post('/api/gemini/generate-script', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const { slides, folderName } = req.body;
      if (!slides || !Array.isArray(slides)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid slides payload' });
      }

      if (!apiKey) {
        return res.status(500).json({ 
          error: 'GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable is not configured. Please configure it in Settings > Secrets.' 
        });
      }

      const prompt = `You are an expert Hollywood screenplay writer. 
Write a highly polished, professional, standard-format Screenplay Script based on this storyboard sequence titled "${folderName || 'My Storyboard'}".

The storyboard slides are:
${JSON.stringify(slides, null, 2)}

Format Instructions:
1. Write in standard professional screenplay format:
   - Scene Headings: e.g., "INT. COFFEE SHOP - DAY" (All Caps, bold, spaced)
   - Action Descriptions: Normal descriptive text.
   - Character Names: ALL CAPS on their own line (e.g., "HERO") before their dialogue.
   - Dialogue: Spoken words, indented.
   - Parenthetical cues: e.g. "(nervously)"
2. Correlate and integrate the storyboard frames. For EACH slide, insert a clear marker tag in the script on its own line:
   "[Frame: Scene X, Shot Y]"
   where X is the scene number and Y is the shot number. Place this marker exactly at the beat where the slide's visual direction should occur.
3. Be descriptive, cinematic, and dramatic. Ensure the screenplay reads beautifully and maintains the exact visual details, action directions, and audio cues provided in the slides.
4. CRITICAL INSTRUCTION: If any slide has a "subjects" list (representing Identified Subjects/Objects in that frame), you MUST base your screenplay descriptions, character actions, and scene narrative on these identified subjects/objects first. Prioritize naming, describing, and interacting with these identified entities in the action lines of the script.
5. Output only the plain script content, no wrapping markdown blocks (like \`\`\`fountain or \`\`\`text) or conversational text.`;

      const response = await callGeminiWithRetry(prompt);

      res.json({ script: response.text });
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error('Gemini generate script error:', err);
      const errMsg = err.message || String(err);
      if (errMsg.includes('503') || errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('high demand') || errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('unavailable')) {
        return res.status(503).json({ error: 'The AI model is currently experiencing extremely high demand. Please wait a brief moment and try again.' });
      }
      res.status(500).json({ error: errMsg || 'Failed to generate screenplay script' });
    }
  });

  // API: AI extract storyboard frames from screenplay text
  app.post('/api/gemini/extract-frames', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const { scriptText, complexity } = req.body;
      if (!scriptText || typeof scriptText !== 'string') {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No script text provided' });
      }

      if (!apiKey) {
        return res.status(500).json({ 
          error: 'GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable is not configured. Please configure it in Settings > Secrets.' 
        });
      }

      let complexityInstruction = "";
      if (complexity === 'quick') {
        complexityInstruction = "Format the shot description with a 'quick' style: In the 'action' field, provide a very brief, punchy description of the camera angle and the immediate visual framing (e.g., 'Close-up of the protagonist staring at the screen in disbelief.'). Keep the 'notes' extremely short (1-5 words).";
      } else if (complexity === 'objects') {
        complexityInstruction = "Format the shot description with a 'main objects only' style: In the 'action' field, focus heavily on identifying and describing the central physical objects, key props, characters, and visible elements present in the camera frame (e.g., 'A vintage pocket watch with cracked glass resting on a mahogany desk next to an open fountain pen. Protagonist's hand enters the frame.'). Keep 'notes' focused on key props.";
      } else {
        // 'full'
        complexityInstruction = "Format the shot description with a 'full' style: Provide a comprehensive, highly detailed, and cinematic description of the entire shot in the 'action' field. Include character staging, facial expressions, camera movement, composition, lighting, and environment (e.g., 'High-angle wide shot. The protagonist sits hunched over the mahogany desk, illuminated only by a warm, dusty desk lamp. Behind them, shadows stretch across the bookshelf. The camera slowly dollies in as their hand trembles while picking up a cracked vintage pocket watch.'). Keep 'notes' rich in director cues, lighting, lens types, and emotional tone.";
      }

      const prompt = `You are an expert film director and storyboard artist. 
Analyze the following screenplay script and break it down into a sequence of individual storyboard slides/frames.

Script:
${scriptText}

${complexityInstruction}

Extract up to 10 sequential cinematic frames from this script. For each frame, provide:
- sceneNo: number (the scene number from the script, starting at 1)
- shotNo: number (the sequential shot number within that scene, starting at 1)
- shotType: string (one of: 'WS', 'MS', 'CU', 'ECU', 'OTS', 'POV', 'INSERT', 'EST', 'TWO')
- duration: number (estimated screen duration in milliseconds, e.g. 3000 for 3 seconds)
- action: string (detailed camera direction, character movement, framing, or visual action)
- dialogue: string (the character dialogue or voiceover or crucial audio cue spoken in this shot)
- notes: string (notes about lighting, lens choice, emotional tone, or camera movement)

Output your response strictly as a JSON array of objects with the exact schema. Do not wrap the JSON in markdown code blocks like \`\`\`json. Output nothing else but the pure parsable JSON array.
Each object must have the fields: "sceneNo", "shotNo", "shotType", "duration", "action", "dialogue", "notes".`;

      const schema = {
        type: Type.ARRAY,
        description: "An array of extracted storyboard frames based on the screenplay",
        items: {
          type: Type.OBJECT,
          properties: {
            sceneNo: {
              type: Type.INTEGER,
              description: "The scene number from the script, starting at 1"
            },
            shotNo: {
              type: Type.INTEGER,
              description: "The sequential shot number within that scene, starting at 1"
            },
            shotType: {
              type: Type.STRING,
              description: "Cinematic shot type. One of: WS, MS, CU, ECU, OTS, POV, INSERT, EST, TWO"
            },
            duration: {
              type: Type.INTEGER,
              description: "Estimated screen duration in milliseconds"
            },
            action: {
              type: Type.STRING,
              description: "Detailed camera direction, character movement, framing, or visual action based on the requested detail level"
            },
            dialogue: {
              type: Type.STRING,
              description: "The character dialogue, voiceover, or crucial audio cue spoken in this shot"
            },
            notes: {
              type: Type.STRING,
              description: "Notes about lighting, lens choice, emotional tone, or camera movement based on the requested detail level"
            }
          },
          required: ["sceneNo", "shotNo", "shotType", "duration", "action", "dialogue", "notes"]
        }
      };

      const response = await callGeminiWithRetry(prompt, undefined, schema);

      let cleanText = response.text || '';
      // Strip markdown code blocks if any
      cleanText = cleanText.replace(/^```json\s*/i, '').replace(/```\s*$/, '').trim();

      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(cleanText);
        res.json({ frames: parsed });
      } catch (parseErr) {
        console.error('Failed to parse JSON response from Gemini:', cleanText);
        res.status(500).json({ 
          error: 'Failed to parse extracted frames from AI response.', 
          rawResponse: cleanText 
        });
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error('Gemini extract frames error:', err);
      const errMsg = err.message || String(err);
      if (errMsg.includes('503') || errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('high demand') || errMsg.toLowerCase().includes('unavailable')) {
        return res.status(503).json({ error: 'The AI model is currently experiencing extremely high demand. Please wait a brief moment and try again.' });
      }
      res.status(500).json({ error: errMsg || 'Failed to extract storyboard frames' });
    }
  });

  app.post("/api/gemini/describe-frame", async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const { base64Data, mimeType } = req.body;
      if (!base64Data || !mimeType) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: "Image data missing" });
      }
      const prompt = "Analyze this images subject, environment, style, lighting, and composition. Provide a detailed description. In your description, explicitly number the key items, objects, and people in the scene using brackets (e.g., [1] a tall man, [2] a red car, [3] a small dog).";
      const contents = [
        {
          inlineData: {
            data: base64Data,
            mimeType: mimeType
          }
        },
        { text: prompt }
      ];
      const response = await callGeminiWithRetry(contents);
      res.json({ description: response.text });
    } catch (err: any) {
      res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
    }
  });


  app.post("/api/gemini/enhance-image", async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const { base64Data: bodyBase64, image, mimeType, style, scaleSize } = req.body;
      const base64Data = bodyBase64 || image;
      if (!base64Data || !mimeType) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: "Image data missing" });
      }

      if (!apiKey) {
        return res.status(500).json({ 
          error: 'GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable is not configured. Please configure it in Settings > Secrets.' 
        });
      }

      const stylePrompts: Record<string, string> = {
        photorealistic: "Apply an ultra-realistic, photorealistic style with fine details, realistic lighting, and natural textures.",
        cinematic: "Apply a stunning cinematic film style with dramatic lighting, rich color grading, shallow depth of field, and movie-grade composition.",
        anime: "Apply a high-quality modern anime/manga illustration style with vibrant colors, clean line art, and beautiful stylized shading.",
        details_booster: "Boost overall details, fine textures, surface resolution, and micro-contrast to make elements pop.",
        oil_painting: "Apply a classical oil painting style with visible brush strokes, rich canvas texture, and painterly color blending.",
        vintage_comic: "Apply a vintage hand-drawn comic book aesthetic with ink outlines, retro halftone pattern dots, and muted color washes."
      };

      const selectedStylePrompt = stylePrompts[style] || stylePrompts['photorealistic'];
      const targetSize = scaleSize || "1K";

      const prompt = `Enhance and upscale this image. ${selectedStylePrompt} Maintain the original subject matter, layout, elements, and core composition precisely, but dramatically improve the details, sharpness, clarity, and visual appeal. Scale this up to high resolution.`;

      console.log(`Enhancing image with style "${style}" and size "${targetSize}"...`);

      const response = await ai.models.generateContent({
        model: 'gemini-3.1-flash-image',
        contents: {
          parts: [
            {
              inlineData: {
                data: base64Data,
                mimeType: mimeType
              }
            },
            {
              text: prompt
            }
          ]
        },
        config: {
          imageConfig: {
            aspectRatio: "1:1",
            imageSize: targetSize
          }
        }
      });

      let resultImageBase64 = "";
      if (response.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts) {
        for (const part of response.candidates[0].content.parts) {
          if (part.inlineData?.data) {
            resultImageBase64 = part.inlineData.data;
            break;
          }
        }
      }

      if (!resultImageBase64) {
        // Fallback to flash-lite-image
        console.log("Attempting fallback with gemini-3.1-flash-lite-image...");
        const fallbackResponse = await ai.models.generateContent({
          model: 'gemini-3.1-flash-lite-image',
          contents: {
            parts: [
              {
                inlineData: {
                  data: base64Data,
                  mimeType: mimeType
                }
              },
              {
                text: prompt
              }
            ]
          }
        });
        if (fallbackResponse.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts) {
          for (const part of fallbackResponse.candidates[0].content.parts) {
            if (part.inlineData?.data) {
              resultImageBase64 = part.inlineData.data;
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }

      if (!resultImageBase64) {
        return res.status(500).json({ error: "Could not extract generated/enhanced image from AI response." });
      }

      res.json({ imageUrl: `data:image/png;base64,${resultImageBase64}` });
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error("Image enhancement error:", err);
      res.status(500).json({ error: err.message || "Failed to enhance image" });
    }
  });

  app.post("/api/gemini/text-to-image", async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const { prompt, aspectRatio, imageSize } = req.body;
      if (!prompt) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: "Prompt is required" });
      }

      if (!apiKey) {
        return res.status(500).json({ 
          error: 'GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable is not configured. Please configure it in Settings > Secrets.' 
        });
      }

      const targetSize = imageSize || "1K";
      const ratio = aspectRatio || "1:1";

      console.log(`Generating image for prompt "${prompt}" with size "${targetSize}" and ratio "${ratio}"...`);

      const response = await ai.models.generateContent({
        model: 'gemini-3.1-flash-image',
        contents: prompt,
        config: {
          imageConfig: {
            aspectRatio: ratio,
            imageSize: targetSize
          }
        }
      });

      let resultImageBase64 = "";
      if (response.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts) {
        for (const part of response.candidates[0].content.parts) {
          if (part.inlineData?.data) {
            resultImageBase64 = part.inlineData.data;
            break;
          }
        }
      }

      if (!resultImageBase64) {
        // Fallback to flash-lite-image
        console.log("Attempting fallback with gemini-3.1-flash-lite-image...");
        const fallbackResponse = await ai.models.generateContent({
          model: 'gemini-3.1-flash-lite-image',
          contents: prompt
        });
        if (fallbackResponse.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts) {
          for (const part of fallbackResponse.candidates[0].content.parts) {
            if (part.inlineData?.data) {
              resultImageBase64 = part.inlineData.data;
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }

      if (!resultImageBase64) {
        return res.status(500).json({ error: "Could not extract generated image from AI response." });
      }

      res.json({ imageUrl: `data:image/png;base64,${resultImageBase64}` });
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error("Text to image error:", err);
      res.status(500).json({ error: err.message || "Failed to generate image" });
    }
  });

  app.post("/api/gemini/image-to-sequence", async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const { base64Data: bodyBase64, image, mimeType, movementType } = req.body;
      const base64Data = bodyBase64 || image;
      if (!base64Data || !mimeType) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: "Image data missing" });
      }

      if (!apiKey) {
        return res.status(500).json({ 
          error: 'GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable is not configured. Please configure it in Settings > Secrets.' 
        });
      }

      const movementLabels: Record<string, string> = {
        pan_right: "Cinematic Slow Pan Right",
        pan_left: "Cinematic Slow Pan Left",
        dolly_in: "Dramatic Dolly In (Camera moves closer to subject)",
        zoom_out: "Revealing Slow Zoom Out",
        tilt_up: "Majestic Tilt Up (Camera tilts upwards)",
        tilt_down: "Descending Tilt Down",
        orbit: "360-Degree Circular Orbit Shot",
        whip_pan: "Fast whip-pan transition"
      };

      const selectedMovement = movementLabels[movementType] || movementLabels['dolly_in'];

      const prompt = `You are an expert film director and cinematic visual artist. 
We have an initial frame (Frame 1) of a storyboard scene, which is provided in the uploaded image. We want to extend this into a continuous 4-frame storyboard sequence showcasing a fluid camera movement: "${selectedMovement}".

First, analyze this initial image's subjects, mood, layout, lighting, and composition.
Then, suggest the next 3 sequential frames (Frame 2, Frame 3, Frame 4) that perfectly continue the camera motion.
The entire sequence must represent a single, uninterrupted cinematic shot.

Provide suggestions for movement between the frames.
Return a structured JSON list of 4 objects. The first object represents Frame 1 itself (describe what's in the image), and the remaining 3 describe the progression.

Each object in the array must have these fields:
- shotNo: number (1 to 4)
- shotType: string (cinematic shot type, e.g. 'WS', 'MS', 'CU', 'OTS', 'POV')
- duration: number (estimated frame duration in milliseconds, e.g. 2000)
- action: string (highly detailed visual description of what is visible in the camera viewfinder for this frame. Make it clear and descriptively rich, so it can be used for text-to-image prompt generation later!)
- dialogue: string (optional dialogue line or voiceover text, or key sound effect)
- notes: string (notes about the camera movement, transition, emotional tone, or lighting)
- movementSuggestion: string (a short 1-sentence description of the camera movement/transition from the PREVIOUS frame to this one. For Frame 1, write "Starting frame")

Output your response strictly as a JSON array of objects. Do not wrap the JSON in markdown code blocks. Output nothing else but the pure, parsable JSON array.`;

      const schema = {
        type: Type.ARRAY,
        description: "An array of 4 sequential storyboard frames showing camera movement",
        items: {
          type: Type.OBJECT,
          properties: {
            shotNo: { type: Type.INTEGER },
            shotType: { type: Type.STRING },
            duration: { type: Type.INTEGER },
            action: { type: Type.STRING },
            dialogue: { type: Type.STRING },
            notes: { type: Type.STRING },
            movementSuggestion: { type: Type.STRING }
          },
          required: ["shotNo", "shotType", "duration", "action", "dialogue", "notes", "movementSuggestion"]
        }
      };

      const response = await callGeminiWithRetry(
        [
          {
            inlineData: {
              data: base64Data,
              mimeType: mimeType
            }
          },
          { text: prompt }
        ],
        undefined,
        schema
      );

      let cleanText = response.text || '';
      cleanText = cleanText.replace(/^```json\s*/i, '').replace(/```\s*$/, '').trim();

      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(cleanText);
        res.json({ frames: parsed });
      } catch (parseErr) {
        console.error('Failed to parse JSON response from Gemini:', cleanText);
        res.status(500).json({ 
          error: 'Failed to parse camera movement sequence from AI response.', 
          rawResponse: cleanText 
        });
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error("Image-to-sequence error:", err);
      res.status(500).json({ error: err.message || "Failed to generate sequence" });
    }
  });

  // Serve static assets or mount Vite
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    const vite = await createViteServer({
      server: { middlewareMode: true },
      appType: 'spa',
    });
    app.use(vite.middlewares);
  } else {
    const distPath = path.join(process.cwd(), 'dist');
    app.use(express.static(distPath));
    app.get('*', (req, res) => {
      res.sendFile(path.join(distPath, 'index.html'));
    });
  }

  app.listen(PORT, '0.0.0.0', () => {
    console.log(`Server running on port ${PORT}`);
  });
}

startServer();
-e

import {StrictMode} from 'react';
import {createRoot} from 'react-dom/client';
import App from './App.tsx';
import './index.css';

createRoot(document.getElementById('root')!).render(
  <StrictMode>
    <App />
  </StrictMode>,
);

=== FILE: src/index.css ===
@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Cinzel:wght@400;700&family=Creepster&family=Pacifico&display=swap');
@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/icon?family=Material+Icons');
@import "tailwindcss";

@layer base {
  body {
    background-color: #0A0A0B;

=== FILE: src/useAudio.ts ===
import { useCallback } from 'react';

export function useAudio() {
  const triggerAudioBeep = useCallback((freq: number, type: OscillatorType, duration: number) => {
    try {
      const ctx = new (window.AudioContext || (window as any).webkitAudioContext)();
      const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
      const gain = ctx.createGain();
      osc.type = type;
      osc.frequency.value = freq;
      gain.gain.value = 0.15;
      gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, ctx.currentTime + duration);
      osc.connect(gain);
      gain.connect(ctx.destination);
      osc.start();
      osc.stop(ctx.currentTime + duration);
    } catch {
      // Audio not supported or blocked by browser policies
    }
  }, []);

  return { triggerAudioBeep };
}

=== FILE: src/utils/image.ts ===
export function resizeImage(dataUrl: string, maxWidth: number = 1024, maxHeight: number = 720, quality: number = 0.75): Promise<string> {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const img = new Image();
    img.onload = () => {
      let width = img.width;
      let height = img.height;

      if (width > maxWidth || height > maxHeight) {
        const ratio = Math.min(maxWidth / width, maxHeight / height);
        width = Math.round(width * ratio);
        height = Math.round(height * ratio);
      }

      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      canvas.width = width;
      canvas.height = height;

      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      if (ctx) {
        ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, width, height);
        // Convert to JPEG for maximum compression
        resolve(canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', quality));
      } else {
        resolve(dataUrl);
      }
    };
    img.onerror = () => {
      resolve(dataUrl);
    };
    img.src = dataUrl;
  });
}

=== FILE: src/lib/firebase.ts ===
import { initializeApp } from 'firebase/app';
import { getAuth } from 'firebase/auth';
import { getFirestore } from 'firebase/firestore';
import firebaseConfig from '../../firebase-applet-config.json';

const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
export const db = getFirestore(app, (firebaseConfig as any).firestoreDatabaseId);
export const auth = getAuth();

export enum OperationType {
  CREATE = 'create',
  UPDATE = 'update',
  DELETE = 'delete',
  LIST = 'list',
  GET = 'get',
  WRITE = 'write',
}

export interface FirestoreErrorInfo {
  error: string;
  operationType: OperationType;
  path: string | null;
  authInfo: {
    userId?: string | null;
    email?: string | null;
    emailVerified?: boolean | null;
    isAnonymous?: boolean | null;
    tenantId?: string | null;
    providerInfo?: {
      providerId?: string | null;
      email?: string | null;
    }[];
  }
}

export function handleFirestoreError(error: unknown, operationType: OperationType, path: string | null) {
  const errInfo: FirestoreErrorInfo = {
    error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
    authInfo: {
      userId: auth.currentUser?.uid || null,
      email: auth.currentUser?.email || null,
      emailVerified: auth.currentUser?.emailVerified || null,
      isAnonymous: auth.currentUser?.isAnonymous || null,
      tenantId: auth.currentUser?.tenantId || null,
      providerInfo: auth.currentUser?.providerData?.map(provider => ({
        providerId: provider.providerId,
        email: provider.email,
      })) || []
    },
    operationType,
    path
  };
  console.error('Firestore Error: ', JSON.stringify(errInfo));
  throw new Error(JSON.stringify(errInfo));
}

=== FILE: src/components/UploadModal.tsx ===
import React, { useState, useRef, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react';
import {
  Upload, X, Trash2, CheckSquare, Square,
  Image, FileImage, Loader2, FolderTree, ArrowDownToLine
} from 'lucide-react';
import { resizeImage } from '../utils/image';

export interface UploadedFile {
  id: string;
  file: File;
  name: string;
  size: number;
  type: string;
  relativePath: string;
  folder: string;
  dataUrl: string;
  width: number;
  height: number;
  selected: boolean;
  status: 'loading' | 'ready' | 'error';
}

interface UploadModalProps {
  onClose: () => void;
  onImport: (files: UploadedFile[], folderName?: string) => void;
  autoTriggerFolder?: boolean;
}

const ACCEPTED_TYPES = ['image/png', 'image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/gif', 'image/webp', 'image/svg+xml', 'image/bmp'];
const MAX_FILE_SIZE = 50 * 1024 * 1024;

function generateId() {
  return Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10);
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes < 1024) return bytes + ' B';
  if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) return (bytes / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' KB';
  return (bytes / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(1) + ' MB';
}

function extractFolder(path: string): string {
  const parts = path.split('/');
  if (parts.length <= 1) return '';
  return parts.slice(0, -1).join('/');
}

export default function UploadModal({ onClose, onImport, autoTriggerFolder = false }: UploadModalProps) {
  const [uploadedFiles, setUploadedFiles] = useState<UploadedFile[]>([]);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [detectedFolderName, setDetectedFolderName] = useState('');
  const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false);
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<'grid' | 'list'>('grid');
  const [sortBy] = useState<'name' | 'size' | 'folder'>('name');
  const [sortAsc] = useState(true);
  const [filterFolder] = useState<string>('all');

  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const folderInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const dropZoneRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const processFile = useCallback((file: File, relativePath: string): Promise<UploadedFile> => {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      const id = generateId();
      const folder = extractFolder(relativePath);

      if (!ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) {
        resolve({
          id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
          relativePath, folder, dataUrl: '', width: 0, height: 0,
          selected: false, status: 'error',
        });
        return;
      }

      if (file.size > MAX_FILE_SIZE) {
        resolve({
          id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
          relativePath, folder, dataUrl: '', width: 0, height: 0,
          selected: false, status: 'error',
        });
        return;
      }

      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = (e) => {
        const rawDataUrl = e.target?.result as string;
        // Resize image to keep Firestore payload lightweight & robust
        resizeImage(rawDataUrl, 800, 450, 0.55).then((dataUrl) => {
          const img = new window.Image();
          img.onload = () => {
            resolve({
              id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
              relativePath, folder, dataUrl,
              width: img.naturalWidth, height: img.naturalHeight,
              selected: true, status: 'ready',
            });
          };
          img.onerror = () => {
            resolve({
              id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
              relativePath, folder, dataUrl,
              width: 0, height: 0,
              selected: true, status: 'ready',
            });
          };
          img.src = dataUrl;
        }).catch(() => {
          resolve({
            id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
            relativePath, folder, dataUrl: rawDataUrl, width: 0, height: 0,
            selected: true, status: 'ready',
          });
        });
      };
      reader.onerror = () => {
        resolve({
          id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
          relativePath, folder, dataUrl: '', width: 0, height: 0,
          selected: false, status: 'error',
        });
      };
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
  }, []);

  const processFiles = useCallback(async (fileList: File[], paths?: string[]) => {
    setIsProcessing(true);
    const results: UploadedFile[] = [];

    for (let i = 0; i < fileList.length; i++) {
      const file = fileList[i];
      const relativePath = paths ? paths[i] : file.name;
      if (!ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) continue;
      const processed = await processFile(file, relativePath);
      results.push(processed);
    }

    setUploadedFiles(prev => [...prev, ...results]);
    setIsProcessing(false);
  }, [processFile]);

  const handleFileSelect = useCallback((e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const files = e.target.files;
    if (!files || files.length === 0) return;
    const fileArray = Array.from(files) as File[];
    const paths = fileArray.map(f => f.name);
    processFiles(fileArray, paths);
    e.target.value = '';
  }, [processFiles]);

  const handleFolderSelect = useCallback(async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const files = e.target.files;
    if (!files || files.length === 0) return;

    const fileArray = Array.from(files) as File[];
    const paths = fileArray.map(f => (f as File & { webkitRelativePath?: string }).webkitRelativePath || f.name);

    let folderName = '';
    for (const p of paths) {
      const parts = p.split('/');
      if (parts.length > 1) { folderName = parts[0]; break; }
    }
    if (folderName) setDetectedFolderName(folderName);

    const results: UploadedFile[] = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < fileArray.length; i++) {
      const file = fileArray[i];
      if (!ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) continue;
      const processed = await processFile(file, paths[i]);
      results.push(processed);
    }

    if (results.length > 0) {
      const readyFiles = results.filter(f => f.status === 'ready');
      if (readyFiles.length > 0) {
        onImport(readyFiles, folderName || undefined);
        onClose();
      }
    }
    e.target.value = '';
  }, [processFile, onImport, onClose]);

  const handleDragEnter = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
    setIsDragging(true);
  }, []);

  const handleDragLeave = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
    const rect = dropZoneRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (rect) {
      const { clientX, clientY } = e;
      if (clientX < rect.left || clientX > rect.right || clientY < rect.top || clientY > rect.bottom) {
        setIsDragging(false);
      }
    }
  }, []);

  const handleDragOver = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
  }, []);

  const readDirectory = useCallback(async (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry): Promise<{file: File; path: string}[]> => {
    const results: {file: File; path: string}[] = [];

    const readEntries = (dirReader: FileSystemDirectoryReader): Promise<FileSystemEntry[]> => {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => dirReader.readEntries(resolve, reject));
    };

    const getFile = (fileEntry: FileSystemFileEntry): Promise<File> => {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => fileEntry.file(resolve, reject));
    };

    const processEntry = async (e: FileSystemEntry, path: string): Promise<void> => {
      if (e.isFile) {
        try {
          const file = await getFile(e as FileSystemFileEntry);
          if (ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) results.push({ file, path: path + e.name });
        } catch { /* skip */ }
      } else if (e.isDirectory) {
        const dirReader = (e as FileSystemDirectoryEntry).createReader();
        let entries: FileSystemEntry[] = [];
        let batch: FileSystemEntry[];
        do {
          batch = await readEntries(dirReader);
          entries = entries.concat(batch);
        } while (batch.length > 0);

        for (const child of entries) await processEntry(child, path + e.name + '/');
      }
    };

    await processEntry(entry, '');
    return results;
  }, []);

  const handleDrop = useCallback(async (e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
    setIsDragging(false); setIsProcessing(true);

    const items = e.dataTransfer.items;
    const allFiles: File[] = [];
    const allPaths: string[] = [];

    if (items) {
      const entries: FileSystemEntry[] = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
        const entry = items[i].webkitGetAsEntry?.();
        if (entry) entries.push(entry);
      }

      for (const entry of entries) {
        if (entry.isDirectory) {
          const dirFiles = await readDirectory(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
          for (const { file, path } of dirFiles) { allFiles.push(file); allPaths.push(path); }
        } else if (entry.isFile) {
          const file = await new Promise<File>((resolve, reject) =>
            (entry as FileSystemFileEntry).file(resolve, reject)
          );
          if (ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) { allFiles.push(file); allPaths.push(file.name); }
        }
      }
    } else {
      const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
      for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
        if (ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(files[i].type)) { allFiles.push(files[i]); allPaths.push(files[i].name); }
      }
    }

    if (allFiles.length > 0) await processFiles(allFiles, allPaths);
    setIsProcessing(false);
  }, [processFiles, readDirectory]);

  const toggleSelect = useCallback((id: string) => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.id === id ? { ...f, selected: !f.selected } : f));
  }, []);

  const selectAll = useCallback(() => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.status === 'ready' ? { ...f, selected: true } : f));
  }, []);

  const deselectAll = useCallback(() => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.map(f => ({ ...f, selected: false })));
  }, []);

  const removeFile = useCallback((id: string) => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.filter(f => f.id !== id));
  }, []);

  const removeAll = useCallback(() => setUploadedFiles([]), []);

  const removeSelected = useCallback(() => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.filter(f => !f.selected));
  }, []);

  const filteredFiles = uploadedFiles
    .filter(f => filterFolder === 'all' || f.folder === filterFolder || (filterFolder === '' && !f.folder))
    .sort((a, b) => {
      let cmp = 0;
      if (sortBy === 'name') cmp = a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
      else if (sortBy === 'size') cmp = a.size - b.size;
      else if (sortBy === 'folder') cmp = a.folder.localeCompare(b.folder);
      return sortAsc ? cmp : -cmp;
    });

  const selectedCount = uploadedFiles.filter(f => f.selected && f.status === 'ready').length;
  const readyCount = uploadedFiles.filter(f => f.status === 'ready').length;
  const totalSize = uploadedFiles.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size, 0);

  const handleImport = () => {
    const selected = uploadedFiles.filter(f => f.selected && f.status === 'ready');
    if (selected.length > 0) {
      onImport(selected, detectedFolderName || undefined);
      onClose();
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    if (autoTriggerFolder && folderInputRef.current) {
      folderInputRef.current.click();
    }
  }, [autoTriggerFolder]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = (e: KeyboardEvent) => { if (e.key === 'Escape') onClose(); };
    window.addEventListener('keydown', handler);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handler);
  }, [onClose]);

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-[#0A0A0B]/90 z-[150] flex items-center justify-center p-4 animate-fade-in backdrop-blur-sm">
      <div className="bg-[#0C0C0E] border border-neutral-800 rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-5xl max-h-[90vh] flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-4 border-b border-neutral-800 shrink-0">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="w-9 h-9 bg-indigo-600/20 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center"><Upload className="w-4.5 h-4.5 text-indigo-400" /></div>
            <div>
              <h2 className="text-sm font-extrabold text-white tracking-tight">Import Media Files</h2>
              <p className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 font-medium">Upload images or drag folders</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="p-2 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-400 hover:text-neutral-200 rounded-lg transition-colors"><X className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
        </div>

        <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden flex flex-col">
          <div className="px-5 py-4 border-b border-neutral-800/60 shrink-0">
            <div ref={dropZoneRef} onDragEnter={handleDragEnter} onDragLeave={handleDragLeave} onDragOver={handleDragOver} onDrop={handleDrop} onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}
              className={`relative border-2 border-dashed rounded-xl p-6 text-center transition-all cursor-pointer ${isDragging ? 'border-indigo-500 bg-indigo-500/10 scale-[1.01]' : 'border-neutral-700 bg-neutral-800/30 hover:border-neutral-600 hover:bg-neutral-800/50'}`}>
              {isProcessing ? (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2"><Loader2 className="w-8 h-8 text-indigo-400 animate-spin" /><p className="text-xs text-indigo-300 font-bold">Processing...</p></div>
              ) : isDragging ? (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2"><ArrowDownToLine className="w-8 h-8 text-indigo-400 animate-bounce" /><p className="text-xs text-indigo-300 font-bold">Drop here</p></div>
              ) : (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-neutral-800 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center border border-neutral-700"><FileImage className="w-5 h-5 text-neutral-400" /></div>
                    <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-neutral-800 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center border border-neutral-700"><FolderTree className="w-5 h-5 text-neutral-400" /></div>
                  </div>
                  <div><p className="text-xs text-neutral-300 font-bold">Drag & drop images or folders</p><p className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 mt-0.5">Supports PNG, JPG, GIF, WebP, SVG, BMP</p></div>
                </div>
              )}
              <input ref={fileInputRef} type="file" multiple accept="image/*" onChange={handleFileSelect} className="hidden" />
              <input ref={folderInputRef} type="file" {...({webkitdirectory: "true", directory: "true"} as React.InputHTMLAttributes<HTMLInputElement>)} multiple onChange={handleFolderSelect} className="hidden" />
            </div>

            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-3">
              <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); fileInputRef.current?.click(); }} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold transition-colors border border-neutral-700"><Image className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Files</button>
              <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); folderInputRef.current?.click(); }} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold transition-colors border border-neutral-700"><FolderTree className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Folder</button>

              {uploadedFiles.length > 0 && (
                <>
                  <div className="h-4 w-px bg-neutral-700 mx-1" />
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 font-mono">{uploadedFiles.length} files • {formatFileSize(totalSize)}</span>
                </>
              )}

              {uploadedFiles.length > 0 && (
                <div className="ml-auto flex items-center gap-2">
                  <div className="flex bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg border border-neutral-700 overflow-hidden">
                    <button onClick={() => setViewMode('grid')} className={`px-2 py-1 text-[10px] font-bold ${viewMode === 'grid' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400'}`}>Grid</button>
                    <button onClick={() => setViewMode('list')} className={`px-2 py-1 text-[10px] font-bold ${viewMode === 'list' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400'}`}>List</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-5 py-3">
            {uploadedFiles.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="flex-1">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3 sticky top-0 bg-[#0C0C0E] py-1.5 z-10">
                  <button onClick={selectedCount === readyCount ? deselectAll : selectAll} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 rounded text-[10px] font-bold border border-neutral-700">
                    {selectedCount === readyCount ? <CheckSquare className="w-3 h-3 text-indigo-400" /> : <Square className="w-3 h-3" />} {selectedCount === readyCount ? 'Deselect All' : 'Select All'}
                  </button>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <button onClick={removeSelected} disabled={selectedCount === 0} className="text-[10px] text-rose-400 font-bold disabled:opacity-30">Remove Selected</button>
                    <button onClick={removeAll} className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 font-bold">Clear All</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <FileGrid files={filteredFiles} viewMode={viewMode} onToggle={toggleSelect} onRemove={removeFile} />
              </div>
            ) : !isProcessing && (
              <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center py-12 text-center"><div><Upload className="w-10 h-10 text-neutral-700 mx-auto mb-3" /><p className="text-xs text-neutral-600">No files yet</p></div></div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-3 border-t border-neutral-800 bg-neutral-900/80 shrink-0">
          <span className="text-[10px] text-emerald-400 font-bold">{readyCount} ready</span>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <button onClick={onClose} className="px-4 py-2 bg-neutral-800 text-neutral-400 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold">Cancel</button>
            <button onClick={handleImport} disabled={selectedCount === 0} className="px-5 py-2 bg-indigo-600 text-white rounded-lg text-xs font-extrabold disabled:opacity-40">Import {selectedCount} Frames</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

interface FileGridProps { files: UploadedFile[]; viewMode: 'grid' | 'list'; onToggle: (id: string) => void; onRemove: (id: string) => void; }

function FileGrid({ files, viewMode, onToggle, onRemove }: FileGridProps) {
  if (viewMode === 'grid') {
    return (
      <div className="grid grid-cols-4 sm:grid-cols-5 md:grid-cols-6 lg:grid-cols-7 gap-2">
        {files.map(f => (
          <div key={f.id} onClick={() => f.status === 'ready' && onToggle(f.id)}
            className={`group relative rounded-lg border overflow-hidden cursor-pointer ${f.status === 'error' ? 'opacity-60 grayscale' : f.selected ? 'border-indigo-500 ring-1 ring-indigo-500/30' : 'border-neutral-700 bg-neutral-800/40'}`}>
            <div className="aspect-square bg-black flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
              {f.dataUrl ? <img src={f.dataUrl} alt={f.name} className="w-full h-full object-cover" /> : <FileImage className="w-6 h-6 text-neutral-700" />}
            </div>
            {f.selected && <div className="absolute top-1 left-1"><CheckSquare className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" /></div>}
            <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onRemove(f.id); }} className="absolute top-1 right-1 p-0.5 bg-black/70 rounded text-neutral-500 hover:text-rose-400 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"><X className="w-3 h-3" /></button>
            <div className="px-1.5 py-1 bg-neutral-900/90"><p className="text-[9px] text-neutral-300 truncate font-medium">{f.name}</p></div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    );
  }
  return (
    <div className="space-y-1">
      {files.map(f => (
        <div key={f.id} onClick={() => f.status === 'ready' && onToggle(f.id)}
          className={`flex items-center gap-3 p-2 rounded-lg cursor-pointer ${f.selected ? 'bg-indigo-500/10 border border-indigo-500/30' : 'bg-neutral-800/30 border border-transparent'}`}>
          {f.selected ? <CheckSquare className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" /> : <Square className="w-4 h-4 text-neutral-600" />}
          <div className="w-10 h-8 rounded bg-black border border-neutral-700 overflow-hidden shrink-0 flex items-center justify-center">
            {f.dataUrl ? <img src={f.dataUrl} alt={f.name} className="w-full h-full object-cover" /> : <FileImage className="w-4 h-4 text-neutral-700" />}
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-0"><p className="text-[11px] text-neutral-200 truncate font-medium">{f.name}</p></div>
          <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onRemove(f.id); }} className="p-1 text-neutral-600 hover:text-rose-400"><Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /></button>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
