          <path d="M40,55 L30,40" stroke="#312e81" stroke-width="6" stroke-linecap="round"/>
          <path d="M60,55 L70,40" stroke="#312e81" stroke-width="6" stroke-linecap="round"/>
        </svg>`
      },
      {
        name: "Target Sight",
        category: "prop",
        svg: `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 100 100" width="100" height="100">
          <circle cx="50" cy="50" r="35" fill="none" stroke="#22c55e" stroke-width="3"/>
          <circle cx="50" cy="50" r="15" fill="none" stroke="#22c55e" stroke-width="1.5"/>
          <line x1="50" y1="5" x2="50" y2="95" stroke="#22c55e" stroke-width="2"/>
          <line x1="5" y1="50" x2="95" y2="50" stroke="#22c55e" stroke-width="2"/>
        </svg>`
      }
    ];

    for (const asset of defaultAssets) {
      const assetId = generateId();
      const encodedSvg = encodeURIComponent(asset.svg);
      const dataUrl = `data:image/svg+xml;utf8,${encodedSvg}`;
      try {
        await setDoc(doc(db, 'collageAssets', assetId), {
          id: assetId,
          name: asset.name,
          imageUrl: dataUrl,
          category: asset.category,
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      } catch (err) {
        handleFirestoreError(err, OperationType.WRITE, `collageAssets/${assetId}`);
      }
    }
  };

  const filteredAssets = collageAssets.filter(asset => {
    const matchesSearch = asset.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
    const matchesCategory = selectedCategory === 'all' || asset.category === selectedCategory;
    return matchesSearch && matchesCategory;
  });

  // Responsive display dimensions
  const displayScale = Math.min(1, Math.min(780 / width, 440 / height));
  const displayW = Math.round(width * displayScale);
  const displayH = Math.round(height * displayScale);

  const pushHistory = useCallback((customTextLayers?: TextLayer[], customImageLayers?: ImageLayer[]) => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;
    const data = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    const textLayersToSave = customTextLayers !== undefined ? customTextLayers : textLayers;
    const imageLayersToSave = customImageLayers !== undefined ? customImageLayers : imageLayers;
    setHistory(prev => {
      const next = prev.slice(0, historyIndex + 1);
      next.push({ imageData: data, textLayers: textLayersToSave, imageLayers: imageLayersToSave });
      if (next.length > 40) next.shift();
      return next;
    });
    setHistoryIndex(prev => Math.min(prev + 1, 39));
  }, [historyIndex, textLayers, imageLayers]);

  const restoreHistory = useCallback((index: number) => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas || !history[index]) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    ctx.putImageData(history[index].imageData, 0, 0);
    setTextLayers(history[index].textLayers || []);
    setImageLayers(history[index].imageLayers || []);
    setHistoryIndex(index);
  }, [history]);

  const handleUndo = useCallback(() => {
    if (historyIndex > 0) restoreHistory(historyIndex - 1);
  }, [historyIndex, restoreHistory]);

  const handleRedo = useCallback(() => {
    if (historyIndex < history.length - 1) restoreHistory(historyIndex + 1);
  }, [historyIndex, history.length, restoreHistory]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    canvas.width = width;
    canvas.height = height;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);

    if (imageUrl) {
      const img = new window.Image();
      img.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
      img.onload = () => {
        ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, width, height);
        const data = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
        const startTextLayers = initialTextLayers || [];
        setHistory([{ imageData: data, textLayers: startTextLayers, imageLayers: [] }]);
        setHistoryIndex(0);
        setTextLayers(startTextLayers);
      };
      img.onerror = () => {
        ctx.fillStyle = '#0f172a';
        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
        const data = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
        const startTextLayers = initialTextLayers || [];
        setHistory([{ imageData: data, textLayers: startTextLayers, imageLayers: [] }]);
        setHistoryIndex(0);
        setTextLayers(startTextLayers);
      };
      img.src = imageUrl;
    } else {
      ctx.fillStyle = '#0f172a';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      const data = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
      const startTextLayers = initialTextLayers || [];
      setHistory([{ imageData: data, textLayers: startTextLayers, imageLayers: [] }]);
      setHistoryIndex(0);
      setTextLayers(startTextLayers);
    }
  }, [imageUrl, width, height, initialTextLayers]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const overlay = overlayRef.current;
    if (!overlay) return;
    overlay.width = width;
    overlay.height = height;
  }, [width, height]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (tool === 'crop' && cropRect) {
      drawPersistentCrop();
    } else {
      clearOverlay();
    }
  }, [tool, cropRect]);

  // Sync selected text layer settings to the toolbar
  useEffect(() => {
    if (selectedTextId) {
      const activeText = textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId);
      if (activeText) {
        setFontFamily(activeText.fontFamily);
        setFontSize(activeText.fontSize);
        setFontBold(activeText.isBold);
        setFontItalic(activeText.isItalic);
        setFontOutline(activeText.hasOutline);
        setColor(activeText.color);
        setTextRotation(activeText.rotation !== undefined ? activeText.rotation : 0);
        setTextScaleX(activeText.scaleX !== undefined ? activeText.scaleX : 1);
        setTextScaleY(activeText.scaleY !== undefined ? activeText.scaleY : 1);
      }
    }
  }, [selectedTextId, textLayers]);

  // Update selected text layer when settings change
  const updateSelectedTextProps = (patch: Partial<TextLayer>, shouldPushHistory = false) => {
    if (!selectedTextId) return;
    const nextLayers = textLayers.map(l => l.id === selectedTextId ? { ...l, ...patch } : l);
    setTextLayers(nextLayers);
    if (shouldPushHistory) {
      pushHistory(nextLayers, imageLayers);
    }
  };

  // Update selected image layer when settings change
  const updateSelectedImageProps = (patch: Partial<ImageLayer>, shouldPushHistory = false) => {
    if (!selectedImageId) return;
    const nextLayers = imageLayers.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, ...patch } : l);
    setImageLayers(nextLayers);
    if (shouldPushHistory) {
      pushHistory(textLayers, nextLayers);
    }
  };

  const getPos = (e: React.MouseEvent | React.TouchEvent | MouseEvent | TouchEvent) => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return { x: 0, y: 0 };
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    
    let clientX = 0;
    let clientY = 0;
    
    if ('touches' in e) {
      if (e.touches.length > 0) {
        clientX = e.touches[0].clientX;
        clientY = e.touches[0].clientY;
      } else if ('changedTouches' in e && e.changedTouches.length > 0) {
        clientX = e.changedTouches[0].clientX;
        clientY = e.changedTouches[0].clientY;
      }
    } else {
      clientX = e.clientX;
      clientY = e.clientY;
    }

    const scaleX = canvas.width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = canvas.height / rect.height;
    return {
      x: (clientX - rect.left) * scaleX,
      y: (clientY - rect.top) * scaleY,
    };
  };

  const clearOverlay = () => {
    const overlay = overlayRef.current;
    if (!overlay) return;
    const ctx = overlay.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, overlay.width, overlay.height);
  };

  const drawArrow = (ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, from: { x: number; y: number }, to: { x: number; y: number }) => {
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(from.x, from.y);
    ctx.lineTo(to.x, to.y);
    ctx.stroke();

    const angle = Math.atan2(to.y - from.y, to.x - from.x);
    const headLength = Math.max(12, lineWidth * 3);
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(to.x, to.y);
    ctx.lineTo(
      to.x - headLength * Math.cos(angle - Math.PI / 6),
      to.y - headLength * Math.sin(angle - Math.PI / 6)
    );
    ctx.lineTo(
      to.x - headLength * Math.cos(angle + Math.PI / 6),
      to.y - headLength * Math.sin(angle + Math.PI / 6)
    );
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fill();
  };

  const drawStar = (ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, cx: number, cy: number, spikes: number, outerRadius: number, innerRadius: number, fillShape: boolean) => {
    let rot = (Math.PI / 2) * 3;
    let x = cx;
    let y = cy;
    const step = Math.PI / spikes;

    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(cx, cy - outerRadius);
    for (let i = 0; i < spikes; i++) {
      x = cx + Math.cos(rot) * outerRadius;
      y = cy + Math.sin(rot) * outerRadius;
      ctx.lineTo(x, y);
      rot += step;

      x = cx + Math.cos(rot) * innerRadius;
      y = cy + Math.sin(rot) * innerRadius;
      ctx.lineTo(x, y);
      rot += step;
    }
    ctx.lineTo(cx, cy - outerRadius);
    ctx.closePath();
    if (fillShape) {
      ctx.fill();
    } else {
      ctx.stroke();
    }
  };

  const drawShapePreview = (from: { x: number; y: number }, to: { x: number; y: number }) => {
    const overlay = overlayRef.current;
    if (!overlay) return;
    const ctx = overlay.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, overlay.width, overlay.height);
    ctx.strokeStyle = color;
    ctx.fillStyle = color;
    ctx.lineWidth = lineWidth;
    ctx.lineCap = 'round';
    ctx.lineJoin = 'round';

    if (tool === 'line') {
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(from.x, from.y);
      ctx.lineTo(to.x, to.y);
      ctx.stroke();
    } else if (tool === 'arrow') {
      drawArrow(ctx, from, to);
    } else if (tool === 'rect') {
      const w = to.x - from.x;
      const h = to.y - from.y;
      if (fill) ctx.fillRect(from.x, from.y, w, h);
      else ctx.strokeRect(from.x, from.y, w, h);
    } else if (tool === 'ellipse') {
      const rx = Math.abs(to.x - from.x) / 2;
      const ry = Math.abs(to.y - from.y) / 2;
      const cx = (from.x + to.x) / 2;
      const cy = (from.y + to.y) / 2;
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.ellipse(cx, cy, rx, ry, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      if (fill) ctx.fill();
      else ctx.stroke();
    } else if (tool === 'star') {
      const rx = Math.abs(to.x - from.x) / 2;
      const ry = Math.abs(to.y - from.y) / 2;
      const cx = (from.x + to.x) / 2;
      const cy = (from.y + to.y) / 2;
      const outerRadius = Math.max(rx, ry);
      const innerRadius = outerRadius * 0.4;
      drawStar(ctx, cx, cy, 5, outerRadius, innerRadius, fill);
    } else if (tool === 'crop') {
      ctx.strokeStyle = '#c084fc';
      ctx.lineWidth = 2;
      ctx.setLineDash([6, 4]);
      const w = to.x - from.x;
      const h = to.y - from.y;
      ctx.strokeRect(from.x, from.y, w, h);
      
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, overlay.width, Math.min(from.y, to.y));
      ctx.fillRect(0, Math.max(from.y, to.y), overlay.width, overlay.height - Math.max(from.y, to.y));
      ctx.fillRect(0, Math.min(from.y, to.y), Math.min(from.x, to.x), Math.abs(h));
      ctx.fillRect(Math.max(from.x, to.x), Math.min(from.y, to.y), overlay.width - Math.max(from.x, to.x), Math.abs(h));
      ctx.setLineDash([]);
    }
  };

  const drawPersistentCrop = () => {
    if (!cropRect) return;
    const overlay = overlayRef.current;
    if (!overlay) return;
    const ctx = overlay.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, overlay.width, overlay.height);

    const { x, y, w, h } = cropRect;

    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.65)';
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, overlay.width, y);
    ctx.fillRect(0, y + h, overlay.width, overlay.height - y - h);
    ctx.fillRect(0, y, x, h);
    ctx.fillRect(x + w, y, overlay.width - x - w, h);

    ctx.strokeStyle = '#c084fc';
    ctx.lineWidth = 2.5;
    ctx.setLineDash([6, 4]);
    ctx.strokeRect(x, y, w, h);
    ctx.setLineDash([]);

    ctx.fillStyle = '#c084fc';
    const s = 8;
    ctx.fillRect(x - s/2, y - s/2, s, s);
    ctx.fillRect(x + w - s/2, y - s/2, s, s);
    ctx.fillRect(x - s/2, y + h - s/2, s, s);
    ctx.fillRect(x + w - s/2, y + h - s/2, s, s);
  };

  const commitShape = (from: { x: number; y: number }, to: { x: number; y: number }) => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    if (tool === 'crop') {
      const x = Math.min(from.x, to.x);
      const y = Math.min(from.y, to.y);
      const w = Math.abs(to.x - from.x);
      const h = Math.abs(to.y - from.y);
      if (w > 10 && h > 10) {
        setCropRect({ x, y, w, h });
        setIsCropping(true);
      }
      return;
    }

    ctx.strokeStyle = color;
    ctx.fillStyle = color;
    ctx.lineWidth = lineWidth;
    ctx.lineCap = 'round';
    ctx.lineJoin = 'round';

    if (tool === 'line') {
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(from.x, from.y);
      ctx.lineTo(to.x, to.y);
      ctx.stroke();
    } else if (tool === 'arrow') {
      drawArrow(ctx, from, to);
    } else if (tool === 'rect') {
      const w = to.x - from.x;
      const h = to.y - from.y;
      if (fill) ctx.fillRect(from.x, from.y, w, h);
      else ctx.strokeRect(from.x, from.y, w, h);
    } else if (tool === 'ellipse') {
      const rx = Math.abs(to.x - from.x) / 2;
      const ry = Math.abs(to.y - from.y) / 2;
      const cx = (from.x + to.x) / 2;
      const cy = (from.y + to.y) / 2;
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.ellipse(cx, cy, rx, ry, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      if (fill) ctx.fill();
      else ctx.stroke();
    } else if (tool === 'star') {
      const rx = Math.abs(to.x - from.x) / 2;
      const ry = Math.abs(to.y - from.y) / 2;
      const cx = (from.x + to.x) / 2;
      const cy = (from.y + to.y) / 2;
      const outerRadius = Math.max(rx, ry);
      const innerRadius = outerRadius * 0.4;
      drawStar(ctx, cx, cy, 5, outerRadius, innerRadius, fill);
    }

    clearOverlay();
    pushHistory();
  };

  const handlePointerDown = (e: React.MouseEvent | React.TouchEvent) => {
    const pos = getPos(e);

    if (tool === 'blur') {
      e.preventDefault();
      setIsDrawing(true);
      setStartPos(pos);
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (canvas) {
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        if (ctx) {
          const origData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
          blurOriginalImageDataRef.current = origData;

          const blurCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
          blurCanvas.width = canvas.width;
          blurCanvas.height = canvas.height;
          const bctx = blurCanvas.getContext('2d');
          if (bctx) {
            bctx.filter = 'blur(16px)';
            bctx.drawImage(canvas, 0, 0);
          }
          blurCanvasRef.current = blurCanvas;

          const maskCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
          maskCanvas.width = canvas.width;
          maskCanvas.height = canvas.height;
          maskCanvasRef.current = maskCanvas;

          lastBlurPosRef.current = pos;
        }
      }
      return;
    }

    if (tool === 'eyedropper') {
      e.preventDefault();
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      if (!ctx) return;
      const pixel = ctx.getImageData(Math.floor(pos.x), Math.floor(pos.y), 1, 1).data;
      if (pixel[3] === 0) {
        setColor('#ffffff');
      } else {
        const hex = '#' + [pixel[0], pixel[1], pixel[2]].map(v => v.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
        setColor(hex);
      }
      setTool('pen');
      return;
    }

    if (tool === 'text') {
      e.preventDefault();
      const newLayer: TextLayer = {
        id: generateId(),
        text: textValue || 'Storyboard Text',
        x: pos.x,
        y: pos.y,
        fontSize,
        fontFamily,
        color,
        isBold: fontBold,
        isItalic: fontItalic,
        hasOutline: fontOutline,
        rotation: 0,
        scaleX: 1,
        scaleY: 1
      };
      const nextLayers = [...textLayers, newLayer];
      setTextLayers(nextLayers);
      setSelectedTextId(newLayer.id);
      justAddedTextRef.current = true;
      setTool('select');
      pushHistory(nextLayers);
      return;
    }

    if (tool === 'move') {
      e.preventDefault();
      setIsPanning(true);
      setStartPos(pos);
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (canvas) {
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        if (ctx) {
          setPanStartImageData(ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height));
        }
      }
      return;
    }

    setIsDrawing(true);
    setStartPos(pos);

    if (tool === 'pen' || tool === 'eraser') {
      e.preventDefault();
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      if (!ctx) return;
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(pos.x, pos.y);
      
      if (tool === 'eraser') {
        ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'destination-out';
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,1)';
        ctx.lineWidth = lineWidth * 3.5;
      } else {
        ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
        ctx.strokeStyle = color;
        ctx.lineWidth = lineWidth;
      }
      ctx.lineCap = 'round';
      ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
    }
  };

  const handlePointerMove = (e: React.MouseEvent | React.TouchEvent) => {
    const pos = getPos(e);

    if (tool === 'move' && isPanning && startPos && panStartImageData) {
      e.preventDefault();
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      if (!ctx) return;
      
      const dx = Math.round(pos.x - startPos.x);
      const dy = Math.round(pos.y - startPos.y);
      
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
      ctx.putImageData(panStartImageData, dx, dy);
      return;
    }

    if (tool === 'blur' && isDrawing && lastBlurPosRef.current && blurCanvasRef.current && maskCanvasRef.current && blurOriginalImageDataRef.current) {
      e.preventDefault();
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      if (!ctx) return;
      
      const mctx = maskCanvasRef.current.getContext('2d');
      if (mctx) {
        mctx.beginPath();
        mctx.moveTo(lastBlurPosRef.current.x, lastBlurPosRef.current.y);
        mctx.lineTo(pos.x, pos.y);
        mctx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';
        mctx.lineWidth = lineWidth * 3.5;
        mctx.lineCap = 'round';
        mctx.lineJoin = 'round';
        mctx.stroke();
      }

      ctx.putImageData(blurOriginalImageDataRef.current, 0, 0);

      const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      tempCanvas.width = canvas.width;
      tempCanvas.height = canvas.height;
      const tctx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d');
      if (tctx) {
        tctx.drawImage(maskCanvasRef.current, 0, 0);
        tctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-in';
        tctx.drawImage(blurCanvasRef.current, 0, 0);
      }

      ctx.drawImage(tempCanvas, 0, 0);
      
      lastBlurPosRef.current = pos;
      return;
    }

    if (!isDrawing || !startPos) return;

    if (tool === 'pen' || tool === 'eraser') {
      e.preventDefault();
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      if (!ctx) return;
      ctx.lineTo(pos.x, pos.y);
      ctx.stroke();
    } else if (['line', 'arrow', 'rect', 'ellipse', 'star', 'crop'].includes(tool)) {
      e.preventDefault();
      drawShapePreview(startPos, pos);
    }
  };

  const handlePointerUp = (e: React.MouseEvent | React.TouchEvent) => {
    if (tool === 'blur') {
      setIsDrawing(false);
      setStartPos(null);
      lastBlurPosRef.current = null;
      blurCanvasRef.current = null;
      maskCanvasRef.current = null;
      blurOriginalImageDataRef.current = null;
      pushHistory();
      return;
    }

    if (tool === 'move' && isPanning) {
      e.preventDefault();
      setIsPanning(false);
      setStartPos(null);
      setPanStartImageData(null);
      pushHistory();
      return;
    }

    if (!isDrawing || !startPos) return;
    e.preventDefault();
    const pos = getPos(e);

    if (tool === 'pen' || tool === 'eraser') {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (canvas) {
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        if (ctx) ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
      }
      pushHistory();
    } else if (['line', 'arrow', 'rect', 'ellipse', 'star', 'crop'].includes(tool)) {
      commitShape(startPos, pos);
    }

    setIsDrawing(false);
    setStartPos(null);
  };

  const handleTextMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent, layer: TextLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setSelectedTextId(layer.id);
    setIsDraggingText(true);
    setTool('select');

    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;

    const clickX = (e.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
    const clickY = (e.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;

    setDragOffset({
      x: clickX - layer.x,
      y: clickY - layer.y
    });
  };

  const handleTextTouchStart = (e: React.TouchEvent, layer: TextLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setSelectedTextId(layer.id);
    setIsDraggingText(true);
    setTool('select');

    if (e.touches.length === 0) return;
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;

    const clickX = (touch.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
    const clickY = (touch.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;

    setDragOffset({
      x: clickX - layer.x,
      y: clickY - layer.y
    });
  };

  const handleResizeMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent, layer: TextLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    e.preventDefault();
    setSelectedTextId(layer.id);
    setIsResizingText(true);
    setResizeStartSize(layer.fontSize);
    
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;
    
    setResizeStartPos({
      x: e.clientX * scaleX,
      y: e.clientY * scaleY
    });
  };

  const handleResizeTouchStart = (e: React.TouchEvent, layer: TextLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    e.preventDefault();
    setSelectedTextId(layer.id);
    setIsResizingText(true);
    setResizeStartSize(layer.fontSize);
    
    if (e.touches.length === 0) return;
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;
    
    setResizeStartPos({
      x: touch.clientX * scaleX,
      y: touch.clientY * scaleY
    });
  };

  const handleBubbleResizeMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent, layer: TextLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    e.preventDefault();
    setSelectedTextId(layer.id);
    setIsResizingBubble(true);
    setResizeStartBubbleSize({
      w: layer.bubbleWidth || 250,
      h: layer.bubbleHeight || 120
    });
    
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;
    
    setResizeStartBubblePos({
      x: e.clientX * scaleX,
      y: e.clientY * scaleY
    });
  };

  const handleBubbleResizeTouchStart = (e: React.TouchEvent, layer: TextLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    e.preventDefault();
    setSelectedTextId(layer.id);
    setIsResizingBubble(true);
    setResizeStartBubbleSize({
      w: layer.bubbleWidth || 250,
      h: layer.bubbleHeight || 120
    });
    
    if (e.touches.length === 0) return;
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;
    
    setResizeStartBubblePos({
      x: touch.clientX * scaleX,
      y: touch.clientY * scaleY
    });
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleGlobalMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isDraggingText || !selectedTextId) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const currentX = (e.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
      const currentY = (e.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;

      const newX = Math.round(currentX - dragOffset.x);
      const newY = Math.round(currentY - dragOffset.y);

      setTextLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedTextId ? { ...l, x: newX, y: newY } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalTouchMove = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      if (!isDraggingText || !selectedTextId || e.touches.length === 0) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const touch = e.touches[0];
      const currentX = (touch.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
      const currentY = (touch.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;

      const newX = Math.round(currentX - dragOffset.x);
      const newY = Math.round(currentY - dragOffset.y);

      setTextLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedTextId ? { ...l, x: newX, y: newY } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalMouseUp = () => {
      if (isDraggingText) {
        pushHistory();
      }
      setIsDraggingText(false);
    };

    if (isDraggingText) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.addEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.removeEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isDraggingText, selectedTextId, dragOffset, width, height, pushHistory]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleGlobalMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isResizingText || !selectedTextId || !resizeStartPos) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const currentX = e.clientX * scaleX;
      const currentY = e.clientY * scaleY;

      const dx = currentX - resizeStartPos.x;
      const dy = currentY - resizeStartPos.y;
      
      const displacement = (dx + dy) / 2;
      const newSize = Math.max(10, Math.min(200, Math.round(resizeStartSize + displacement)));

      setTextLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedTextId ? { ...l, fontSize: newSize } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalTouchMove = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      if (!isResizingText || !selectedTextId || !resizeStartPos || e.touches.length === 0) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const touch = e.touches[0];
      const currentX = touch.clientX * scaleX;
      const currentY = touch.clientY * scaleY;

      const dx = currentX - resizeStartPos.x;
      const dy = currentY - resizeStartPos.y;
      
      const displacement = (dx + dy) / 2;
      const newSize = Math.max(10, Math.min(200, Math.round(resizeStartSize + displacement)));

      setTextLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedTextId ? { ...l, fontSize: newSize } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalMouseUp = () => {
      if (isResizingText) {
        pushHistory();
      }
      setIsResizingText(false);
    };

    if (isResizingText) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.addEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.removeEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isResizingText, selectedTextId, resizeStartPos, resizeStartSize, width, height, pushHistory]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleGlobalMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isResizingBubble || !selectedTextId || !resizeStartBubblePos) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const currentX = e.clientX * scaleX;
      const currentY = e.clientY * scaleY;

      const dx = currentX - resizeStartBubblePos.x;
      const dy = currentY - resizeStartBubblePos.y;
      
      const newW = Math.max(80, Math.min(600, Math.round(resizeStartBubbleSize.w + dx * 2)));
      const newH = Math.max(50, Math.min(500, Math.round(resizeStartBubbleSize.h + dy * 2)));

      setTextLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedTextId ? { ...l, bubbleWidth: newW, bubbleHeight: newH } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalTouchMove = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      if (!isResizingBubble || !selectedTextId || !resizeStartBubblePos || e.touches.length === 0) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const touch = e.touches[0];
      const currentX = touch.clientX * scaleX;
      const currentY = touch.clientY * scaleY;

      const dx = currentX - resizeStartBubblePos.x;
      const dy = currentY - resizeStartBubblePos.y;
      
      const newW = Math.max(80, Math.min(600, Math.round(resizeStartBubbleSize.w + dx * 2)));
      const newH = Math.max(50, Math.min(500, Math.round(resizeStartBubbleSize.h + dy * 2)));

      setTextLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedTextId ? { ...l, bubbleWidth: newW, bubbleHeight: newH } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalMouseUp = () => {
      if (isResizingBubble) {
        pushHistory();
      }
      setIsResizingBubble(false);
    };

    if (isResizingBubble) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.addEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.removeEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isResizingBubble, selectedTextId, resizeStartBubblePos, resizeStartBubbleSize, width, height, pushHistory]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleKeyDown = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      const activeEl = document.activeElement;
      const isTyping = activeEl && (activeEl.tagName === 'INPUT' || activeEl.tagName === 'TEXTAREA' || activeEl.getAttribute('contenteditable') === 'true');

      // Global Undo/Redo keyboard shortcuts
      if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key.toLowerCase() === 'z') {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (e.shiftKey) {
          handleRedo();
        } else {
          handleUndo();
        }
        return;
      }
      if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key.toLowerCase() === 'y') {
        e.preventDefault();
        handleRedo();
        return;
      }

      if (isTyping) return;

      if (selectedTextId) {
        if (e.key === 'Delete' || e.key === 'Backspace') {
          e.preventDefault();
          const nextLayers = textLayers.filter(l => l.id !== selectedTextId);
          setTextLayers(nextLayers);
          setSelectedTextId(null);
          pushHistory(nextLayers, imageLayers);
        } else if (['ArrowUp', 'ArrowDown', 'ArrowLeft', 'ArrowRight'].includes(e.key)) {
          e.preventDefault();
          const step = e.shiftKey ? 10 : 2;
          const dx = e.key === 'ArrowLeft' ? -step : e.key === 'ArrowRight' ? step : 0;
          const dy = e.key === 'ArrowUp' ? -step : e.key === 'ArrowDown' ? step : 0;
          const nextLayers = textLayers.map(l => l.id === selectedTextId ? { ...l, x: l.x + dx, y: l.y + dy } : l);
          setTextLayers(nextLayers);
        }
      }

      if (selectedImageId) {
        if (e.key === 'Delete' || e.key === 'Backspace') {
          e.preventDefault();
          const nextLayers = imageLayers.filter(l => l.id !== selectedImageId);
          setImageLayers(nextLayers);
          setSelectedImageId(null);
          pushHistory(textLayers, nextLayers);
        } else if (['ArrowUp', 'ArrowDown', 'ArrowLeft', 'ArrowRight'].includes(e.key)) {
          e.preventDefault();
          const step = e.shiftKey ? 10 : 2;
          const dx = e.key === 'ArrowLeft' ? -step : e.key === 'ArrowRight' ? step : 0;
          const dy = e.key === 'ArrowUp' ? -step : e.key === 'ArrowDown' ? step : 0;
          const nextLayers = imageLayers.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, x: l.x + dx, y: l.y + dy } : l);
          setImageLayers(nextLayers);
        }
      }
    };

    window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
  }, [selectedTextId, textLayers, selectedImageId, imageLayers, handleUndo, handleRedo, pushHistory]);

  const drawTextLayersToCtx = (ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D) => {
    if (hideAllTextLayers) return;
    textLayers.forEach(layer => {
      ctx.save();
      const weight = layer.isBold ? 'bold' : 'normal';
      const style = layer.isItalic ? 'italic' : 'normal';
      ctx.font = `${style} ${weight} ${layer.fontSize}px ${layer.fontFamily}`;
      ctx.fillStyle = layer.color;
      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      ctx.translate(layer.x, layer.y);
      if (layer.rotation) {
        ctx.rotate((layer.rotation * Math.PI) / 180);
      }
      const sx = layer.scaleX !== undefined ? layer.scaleX : 1;
      const sy = layer.scaleY !== undefined ? layer.scaleY : 1;
      if (sx !== 1 || sy !== 1) {
        ctx.scale(sx, sy);
      }

      // Apply advanced skew transformations for text
      const skewXRad = ((layer.skewX || 0) * Math.PI) / 180;
      const skewYRad = ((layer.skewY || 0) * Math.PI) / 180;
      if (skewXRad !== 0 || skewYRad !== 0) {
        ctx.transform(1, Math.tan(skewYRad), Math.tan(skewXRad), 1, 0, 0);
      }

      // Apply 3D perspective foreshortening approximation for text
      const rxRad = ((layer.rotateX || 0) * Math.PI) / 180;
      const ryRad = ((layer.rotateY || 0) * Math.PI) / 180;
      const simScaleX = Math.cos(ryRad);
      const simScaleY = Math.cos(rxRad);
      if (simScaleX !== 1 || simScaleY !== 1) {
        ctx.scale(simScaleX, simScaleY);
      }

      if (layer.isSpeechBubble) {
        const lines = getLinesForText(ctx, layer.text, layer.bubbleWidth || 250, `${style} ${weight} ${layer.fontSize}px ${layer.fontFamily}`);
        const lineHeight = layer.fontSize * 1.25;
        const textHeight = lines.length * lineHeight;
        const bubbleW = layer.bubbleWidth || 250;
        const bubbleH = layer.bubbleHeight || 120;
        const bType = layer.bubbleType || 'speech';

        ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
        ctx.lineWidth = 4;
        ctx.lineJoin = 'round';

        if (bType === 'narration') {
          // Beautiful pale warm cream yellow background
          ctx.fillStyle = layer.bubbleBgColor || '#fffdf2'; 
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.rect(-bubbleW / 2, -bubbleH / 2, bubbleW, bubbleH);
          ctx.fill();

          // Draw a beautiful vertical thick orange accent bar on the left edge inside the border
          ctx.fillStyle = '#f97316';
          ctx.fillRect(-bubbleW / 2, -bubbleH / 2, 10, bubbleH);

          // Outer black outline
          ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
          ctx.lineWidth = 4;
          ctx.stroke();
        } else if (bType === 'thought') {
          // Lavender-blueish elliptical thought bubble with double border (purple outer, black inner)
          ctx.fillStyle = layer.bubbleBgColor || '#e8ecfb';
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.ellipse(0, 0, bubbleW / 2, bubbleH / 2, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
          ctx.fill();

          // Double border: Draw outer purple border first (wider stroke), then inner black border (narrower stroke)
          ctx.strokeStyle = '#8b5cf6';
          ctx.lineWidth = 8;
          ctx.stroke();

          ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
          ctx.lineWidth = 4;
          ctx.stroke();

          // Thought bubble tail circles at the bottom, matching the double border style
          const tailOffset = layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'left' ? -bubbleW * 0.25 :
                             layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'right' ? bubbleW * 0.25 : 0;
          
          const drawThoughtCircle = (cx: number, cy: number, r: number) => {
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = layer.bubbleBgColor || '#e8ecfb';
            ctx.fill();
            
            ctx.strokeStyle = '#8b5cf6';
            ctx.lineWidth = 6;
            ctx.stroke();
            
            ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
            ctx.lineWidth = 3;
            ctx.stroke();
          };

          drawThoughtCircle(tailOffset, bubbleH / 2 + 10, 8);
          drawThoughtCircle(tailOffset + (layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'left' ? -8 : layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'right' ? 8 : 0), bubbleH / 2 + 22, 5);
          drawThoughtCircle(tailOffset + (layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'left' ? -16 : layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'right' ? 16 : 0), bubbleH / 2 + 32, 3);
        } else {
          // Speech Bubble: highly rounded/capsule shape, white background
          ctx.fillStyle = layer.bubbleBgColor || '#ffffff';
          ctx.beginPath();
          const radius = Math.min(bubbleW, bubbleH) / 2;
          if (typeof ctx.roundRect === 'function') {
            ctx.roundRect(-bubbleW / 2, -bubbleH / 2, bubbleW, bubbleH, radius);
          } else {
            ctx.rect(-bubbleW / 2, -bubbleH / 2, bubbleW, bubbleH);
          }
          ctx.fill();
          ctx.stroke();

          // Tail quote bar with 3 selectable lengths
          const tailStyle = layer.bubbleTailLength || 'medium';
          let tailH = 16;
          if (tailStyle === 'short') tailH = 8;
          else if (tailStyle === 'long') tailH = 28;

          const tailW = 20;
          const tailOffset = layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'left' ? -bubbleW * 0.25 :
                             layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'right' ? bubbleW * 0.25 : 0;

          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(tailOffset - tailW / 2, bubbleH / 2 - 2);
          ctx.lineTo(tailOffset, bubbleH / 2 + tailH);
          ctx.lineTo(tailOffset + tailW / 2, bubbleH / 2 - 2);
          ctx.closePath();
          ctx.fillStyle = layer.bubbleBgColor || '#ffffff';
          ctx.fill();
          ctx.stroke();

          // Cover the line intersecting the speech bubble and its tail beautifully
          ctx.fillStyle = layer.bubbleBgColor || '#ffffff';
          ctx.fillRect(tailOffset - tailW / 2 + 2, bubbleH / 2 - 3, tailW - 4, 6);
        }

        ctx.fillStyle = layer.color || '#000000';
        lines.forEach((lineText, lineIdx) => {
          const lineY = -textHeight / 2 + (lineIdx + 0.5) * lineHeight;
          ctx.fillText(lineText.trim(), 0, lineY);
        });
      } else {
        if (layer.hasOutline) {
          ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
          ctx.lineWidth = Math.max(3, layer.fontSize / 7);
          ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
          ctx.strokeText(layer.text, 0, 0);
        }
        ctx.fillText(layer.text, 0, 0);
      }
      
      ctx.restore();
    });
  };

  const drawImageLayersToCtx = (ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D): Promise<void> => {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      if (imageLayers.length === 0) {
        resolve();
        return;
      }
      
      let loadedCount = 0;
      imageLayers.forEach(layer => {
        const img = new window.Image();
        img.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
        img.onload = () => {
          ctx.save();
          ctx.translate(layer.x, layer.y);
          ctx.rotate(((layer.rotation || 0) * Math.PI) / 180);

          // Apply advanced skew transformations for image overlays
          const skewXRad = ((layer.skewX || 0) * Math.PI) / 180;
          const skewYRad = ((layer.skewY || 0) * Math.PI) / 180;
          if (skewXRad !== 0 || skewYRad !== 0) {
            ctx.transform(1, Math.tan(skewYRad), Math.tan(skewXRad), 1, 0, 0);
          }

          // Apply 3D perspective foreshortening approximation for image overlays
          const rxRad = ((layer.rotateX || 0) * Math.PI) / 180;
          const ryRad = ((layer.rotateY || 0) * Math.PI) / 180;
          const simScaleX = Math.cos(ryRad);
          const simScaleY = Math.cos(rxRad);
          if (simScaleX !== 1 || simScaleY !== 1) {
            ctx.scale(simScaleX, simScaleY);
          }

          ctx.drawImage(img, -layer.width / 2, -layer.height / 2, layer.width, layer.height);
          ctx.restore();
          
          loadedCount++;
          if (loadedCount === imageLayers.length) {
            resolve();
          }
        };
        img.onerror = () => {
          loadedCount++;
          if (loadedCount === imageLayers.length) {
            resolve();
          }
        };
        img.src = layer.src;
      });
    });
  };

  const applyCrop = () => {
    if (!cropRect) return;
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    const { x, y, w, h } = cropRect;
    const cropped = ctx.getImageData(x, y, w, h);

    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    const temp = document.createElement('canvas');
    temp.width = w;
    temp.height = h;
    const tctx = temp.getContext('2d');
    if (!tctx) return;
    tctx.putImageData(cropped, 0, 0);

    const scale = Math.min(canvas.width / w, canvas.height / h);
    const dw = w * scale;
    const dh = h * scale;
    const dx = (canvas.width - dw) / 2;
    const dy = (canvas.height - dh) / 2;
    
    ctx.drawImage(temp, dx, dy, dw, dh);

    setCropRect(null);
    setIsCropping(false);
    clearOverlay();
    pushHistory();
    setTool('pen');
  };

  const cancelCrop = () => {
    setCropRect(null);
    setIsCropping(false);
    clearOverlay();
  };

  const handleClear = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    setTextLayers([]);
    setImageLayers([]);
    setSelectedTextId(null);
    setSelectedImageId(null);
    pushHistory([], []);
  };

  const handleBakeLayers = async () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    // Draw all collage images, then draw all text overlays onto the pixel canvas
    await drawImageLayersToCtx(ctx);
    drawTextLayersToCtx(ctx);

    // Clear dynamic vector/image layers since they are now baked into the background canvas
    setTextLayers([]);
    setImageLayers([]);
    setSelectedTextId(null);
    setSelectedImageId(null);

    // Push state to canvas history
    pushHistory([], []);
  };

  const applyPixelFilter = (imageData: ImageData, filter: string) => {
    const data = imageData.data;
    const len = data.length;

    if (filter === 'grayscale') {
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i += 4) {
        const r = data[i];
        const g = data[i + 1];
        const b = data[i + 2];
        const gray = 0.299 * r + 0.587 * g + 0.114 * b;
        data[i] = gray;
        data[i + 1] = gray;
        data[i + 2] = gray;
      }
    } else if (filter === 'sepia') {
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i += 4) {
        const r = data[i];
        const g = data[i + 1];
        const b = data[i + 2];
        data[i] = Math.min(255, (r * 0.393) + (g * 0.769) + (b * 0.189));
        data[i + 1] = Math.min(255, (r * 0.349) + (g * 0.686) + (b * 0.168));
        data[i + 2] = Math.min(255, (r * 0.272) + (g * 0.534) + (b * 0.131));
      }
    } else if (filter === 'invert') {
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i += 4) {
        data[i] = 255 - data[i];
        data[i + 1] = 255 - data[i + 1];
        data[i + 2] = 255 - data[i + 2];
      }
    } else if (filter === 'cinematic') {
      const factor = 1.25; 
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i += 4) {
        let r = data[i];
        let g = data[i + 1];
        let b = data[i + 2];

        r *= 0.95;
        g *= 0.95;
        b *= 0.95;

        r = factor * (r - 128) + 128;
        g = factor * (g - 128) + 128;
        b = factor * (b - 128) + 128;

        const gray = 0.299 * r + 0.587 * g + 0.114 * b;
        r = gray + (r - gray) * 0.85;
        g = gray + (g - gray) * 0.85;
        b = gray + (b - gray) * 0.85;

        data[i] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, r));
        data[i + 1] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, g));
        data[i + 2] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, b));
      }
    } else if (filter === 'warm') {
      const factor = 1.1;
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i += 4) {
        let r = data[i];
        let g = data[i + 1];
        let b = data[i + 2];

        const sr = Math.min(255, (r * 0.393) + (g * 0.769) + (b * 0.189));
        const sg = Math.min(255, (r * 0.349) + (g * 0.686) + (b * 0.168));
        const sb = Math.min(255, (r * 0.272) + (g * 0.534) + (b * 0.131));
        r = r + (sr - r) * 0.3;
        g = g + (sg - g) * 0.3;
        b = b + (sb - b) * 0.3;

        r = factor * (r - 128) + 128;
        g = factor * (g - 128) + 128;
        b = factor * (b - 128) + 128;

        const gray = 0.299 * r + 0.587 * g + 0.114 * b;
        r = gray + (r - gray) * 1.4;
        g = gray + (g - gray) * 1.4;
        b = gray + (b - gray) * 1.4;

        data[i] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, r));
        data[i + 1] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, g));
        data[i + 2] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, b));
      }
    } else if (filter === 'cold') {
      const factor = 0.95;
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i += 4) {
        let r = data[i];
        let g = data[i + 1];
        let b = data[i + 2];

        r = r * 1.02;
        g = g * 1.04;
        b = b * 1.08;

        r = factor * (r - 128) + 128;
        g = factor * (g - 128) + 128;
        b = factor * (b - 128) + 128;

        const gray = 0.299 * r + 0.587 * g + 0.114 * b;
        r = gray + (r - gray) * 0.85;
        g = gray + (g - gray) * 0.85;
        b = gray + (b - gray) * 0.85;

        data[i] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, r));
        data[i + 1] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, g));
        data[i + 2] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, b));
      }
    } else if (filter === 'high-contrast') {
      const factor = 1.4;
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i += 4) {
        let r = data[i];
        let g = data[i + 1];
        let b = data[i + 2];

        r = factor * (r - 128) + 128;
        g = factor * (g - 128) + 128;
        b = factor * (b - 128) + 128;

        data[i] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, r));
        data[i + 1] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, g));
        data[i + 2] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, b));
      }
    }
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    const origData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    // Create a temporary canvas to bake the filter
    const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    tempCanvas.width = canvas.width;
    tempCanvas.height = canvas.height;
    const tempCtx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d');
    
    if (tempCtx) {
      tempCtx.drawImage(canvas, 0, 0);
      const tempImgData = tempCtx.getImageData(0, 0, tempCanvas.width, tempCanvas.height);
      applyPixelFilter(tempImgData, activeFilter);
      tempCtx.putImageData(tempImgData, 0, 0);
      await drawImageLayersToCtx(tempCtx);
      drawTextLayersToCtx(tempCtx);
      const dataUrl = tempCanvas.toDataURL('image/png');
      onSave(dataUrl);
    } else {
      await drawImageLayersToCtx(ctx);
      drawTextLayersToCtx(ctx);
      const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
      ctx.putImageData(origData, 0, 0);
      onSave(dataUrl);
    }
  };

  const handleSaveAsNew = async () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    const origData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    tempCanvas.width = canvas.width;
    tempCanvas.height = canvas.height;
    const tempCtx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d');

    if (tempCtx) {
      tempCtx.drawImage(canvas, 0, 0);
      const tempImgData = tempCtx.getImageData(0, 0, tempCanvas.width, tempCanvas.height);
      applyPixelFilter(tempImgData, activeFilter);
      tempCtx.putImageData(tempImgData, 0, 0);
      await drawImageLayersToCtx(tempCtx);
      drawTextLayersToCtx(tempCtx);
      const dataUrl = tempCanvas.toDataURL('image/png');
      if (onSaveAsNew) {
        onSaveAsNew(dataUrl);
      } else {
        onSave(dataUrl);
      }
    } else {
      await drawImageLayersToCtx(ctx);
      drawTextLayersToCtx(ctx);
      const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
      ctx.putImageData(origData, 0, 0);
      if (onSaveAsNew) {
        onSaveAsNew(dataUrl);
      } else {
        onSave(dataUrl);
      }
    }

    setShowSaveMessage(true);
    setTimeout(() => {
      setShowSaveMessage(false);
    }, 2000);
  };

  const handleNavigate = async (direction: 'prev' | 'next') => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    const origData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    // Create a temporary canvas to bake the filter
    const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    tempCanvas.width = canvas.width;
    tempCanvas.height = canvas.height;
    const tempCtx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d');

    let dataUrl = '';
    if (tempCtx) {
      tempCtx.drawImage(canvas, 0, 0);
      const tempImgData = tempCtx.getImageData(0, 0, tempCanvas.width, tempCanvas.height);
      applyPixelFilter(tempImgData, activeFilter);
      tempCtx.putImageData(tempImgData, 0, 0);
      await drawImageLayersToCtx(tempCtx);
      drawTextLayersToCtx(tempCtx);
      dataUrl = tempCanvas.toDataURL('image/png');
    } else {
      await drawImageLayersToCtx(ctx);
      drawTextLayersToCtx(ctx);
      dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
      ctx.putImageData(origData, 0, 0);
    }

    if (onNavigate && dataUrl) {
      onNavigate(direction, dataUrl);
    }
  };

  const handleDownload = async () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    const origData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    tempCanvas.width = canvas.width;
    tempCanvas.height = canvas.height;
    const tempCtx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d');

    let dataUrl = '';
    if (tempCtx) {
      tempCtx.drawImage(canvas, 0, 0);
      const tempImgData = tempCtx.getImageData(0, 0, tempCanvas.width, tempCanvas.height);
      applyPixelFilter(tempImgData, activeFilter);
      tempCtx.putImageData(tempImgData, 0, 0);
      await drawImageLayersToCtx(tempCtx);
      drawTextLayersToCtx(tempCtx);
      dataUrl = tempCanvas.toDataURL('image/png');
    } else {
      await drawImageLayersToCtx(ctx);
      drawTextLayersToCtx(ctx);
      dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
      ctx.putImageData(origData, 0, 0);
    }

    try {
      const filename = `frame-export-${Date.now()}.png`;
      const link = document.createElement('a');
      link.href = dataUrl;
      link.download = filename;
      document.body.appendChild(link);
      link.click();
      document.body.removeChild(link);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Export PNG failed:", err);
      alert("Failed to export PNG. Tainted canvas error might occur with external images.");
    }
  };

  const handleAddNewText = () => {
    const newLayer: TextLayer = {
      id: generateId(),
      text: textValue || 'Storyboard Text',
      x: width / 2,
      y: height / 2,
      fontSize,
      fontFamily,
      color,
      isBold: fontBold,
      isItalic: fontItalic,
      hasOutline: fontOutline,
      rotation: 0,
      scaleX: 1,
      scaleY: 1
    };
    const nextLayers = [...textLayers, newLayer];
    setTextLayers(nextLayers);
    setSelectedTextId(newLayer.id);
    setSelectedImageId(null);
    setTool('select');
    pushHistory(nextLayers, imageLayers);
  };

  const handleImageUpload = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (event) => {
      const dataUrl = event.target?.result as string;
      const img = new window.Image();
      img.onload = () => {
        const maxDim = 200;
        let w = img.naturalWidth;
        let h = img.naturalHeight;
        if (w > maxDim || h > maxDim) {
          const ratio = Math.min(maxDim / w, maxDim / h);
          w = Math.round(w * ratio);
          h = Math.round(h * ratio);
        }
        
        const newImgLayer: ImageLayer = {
          id: generateId(),
          src: dataUrl,
          x: width / 2,
          y: height / 2,
          width: w,
          height: h,
          rotation: 0
        };
        const nextLayers = [...imageLayers, newImgLayer];
        setImageLayers(nextLayers);
        setSelectedImageId(newImgLayer.id);
        setSelectedTextId(null);
        setTool('select');
        pushHistory(textLayers, nextLayers);
      };
      img.src = dataUrl;
    };
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    e.target.value = '';
  };

  const handleImageMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent, layer: ImageLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setSelectedImageId(layer.id);
    setSelectedTextId(null);
    setIsDraggingImage(true);
    setTool('select');

    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;

    const clickX = (e.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
    const clickY = (e.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;

    setDragImageOffset({
      x: clickX - layer.x,
      y: clickY - layer.y
    });
  };

  const handleImageTouchStart = (e: React.TouchEvent, layer: ImageLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setSelectedImageId(layer.id);
    setSelectedTextId(null);
    setIsDraggingImage(true);
    setTool('select');

    if (e.touches.length === 0) return;
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;

    const clickX = (touch.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
    const clickY = (touch.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;

    setDragImageOffset({
      x: clickX - layer.x,
      y: clickY - layer.y
    });
  };

  const handleImageResizeMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent, layer: ImageLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    e.preventDefault();
    setSelectedImageId(layer.id);
    setSelectedTextId(null);
    setIsResizingImage(true);
    setResizeImageStartSize({ w: layer.width, h: layer.height });
    
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;
    
    setResizeImageStartPos({
      x: e.clientX * scaleX,
      y: e.clientY * scaleY
    });
  };

  const handleImageResizeTouchStart = (e: React.TouchEvent, layer: ImageLayer) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    e.preventDefault();
    setSelectedImageId(layer.id);
    setSelectedTextId(null);
    setIsResizingImage(true);
    setResizeImageStartSize({ w: layer.width, h: layer.height });
    
    if (e.touches.length === 0) return;
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scaleX = width / rect.width;
    const scaleY = height / rect.height;
    
    setResizeImageStartPos({
      x: touch.clientX * scaleX,
      y: touch.clientY * scaleY
    });
  };

  // Image layer dragging useEffect
  useEffect(() => {
    const handleGlobalMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isDraggingImage || !selectedImageId) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const currentX = (e.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
      const currentY = (e.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;

      const newX = Math.round(currentX - dragImageOffset.x);
      const newY = Math.round(currentY - dragImageOffset.y);

      setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, x: newX, y: newY } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalTouchMove = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      if (!isDraggingImage || !selectedImageId || e.touches.length === 0) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const touch = e.touches[0];
      const currentX = (touch.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
      const currentY = (touch.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;

      const newX = Math.round(currentX - dragImageOffset.x);
      const newY = Math.round(currentY - dragImageOffset.y);

      setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, x: newX, y: newY } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalMouseUp = () => {
      if (isDraggingImage) {
        pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
      }
      setIsDraggingImage(false);
    };

    if (isDraggingImage) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.addEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.removeEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isDraggingImage, selectedImageId, dragImageOffset, width, height, textLayers, imageLayers, pushHistory]);

  // Image layer resizing useEffect
  useEffect(() => {
    const handleGlobalMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isResizingImage || !selectedImageId || !resizeImageStartPos) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const currentX = e.clientX * scaleX;
      const currentY = e.clientY * scaleY;

      const dx = currentX - resizeImageStartPos.x;
      const dy = currentY - resizeImageStartPos.y;
      
      const aspect = resizeImageStartSize.w / resizeImageStartSize.h;
      const delta = (dx + dy) / 2;
      const newW = Math.max(20, Math.min(width, Math.round(resizeImageStartSize.w + delta)));
      const newH = Math.max(20, Math.min(height, Math.round(newW / aspect)));

      setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, width: newW, height: newH } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalTouchMove = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      if (!isResizingImage || !selectedImageId || !resizeImageStartPos || e.touches.length === 0) return;
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      if (!canvas) return;
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const scaleX = width / rect.width;
      const scaleY = height / rect.height;

      const touch = e.touches[0];
      const currentX = touch.clientX * scaleX;
      const currentY = touch.clientY * scaleY;

      const dx = currentX - resizeImageStartPos.x;
      const dy = currentY - resizeImageStartPos.y;
      
      const aspect = resizeImageStartSize.w / resizeImageStartSize.h;
      const delta = (dx + dy) / 2;
      const newW = Math.max(20, Math.min(width, Math.round(resizeImageStartSize.w + delta)));
      const newH = Math.max(20, Math.min(height, Math.round(newW / aspect)));

      setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, width: newW, height: newH } : l));
    };

    const handleGlobalMouseUp = () => {
      if (isResizingImage) {
        pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
      }
      setIsResizingImage(false);
    };

    if (isResizingImage) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.addEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleGlobalMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleGlobalMouseUp);
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleGlobalTouchMove);
      window.removeEventListener('touchend', handleGlobalMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isResizingImage, selectedImageId, resizeImageStartPos, resizeImageStartSize, width, height, textLayers, imageLayers, pushHistory]);

  const handleShapeSelect = (shape: ShapeTool) => {
    setActiveShapeTool(shape);
    setTool(shape);
    setShowShapesFlyout(false);
    cancelCrop();
  };

  const resetColorPicker = () => {
    setColor('#ffffff');
    if (selectedTextId) {
      updateSelectedTextProps({ color: '#ffffff' });
    }
  };

  const isShapeActive = ['line', 'arrow', 'rect', 'ellipse', 'star'].includes(tool);

  const getShapeIcon = (shape: ShapeTool) => {
    switch (shape) {
      case 'line': return <Minus className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'arrow': return <ArrowUpRight className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'rect': return <Square className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'ellipse': return <Circle className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'star': return <Star className="w-4 h-4" />;
    }
  };

  const activeTextLayer = textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId);
  const activeImageLayer = imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId);

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-[#0A0A0B]/95 z-[160] flex flex-col animate-fade-in backdrop-blur-sm">
      {showSaveMessage && (
        <div className="absolute top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 bg-emerald-600 text-white font-extrabold text-xs px-4 py-2 rounded-full shadow-lg z-[200] flex items-center gap-2 animate-bounce">
          <Check className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          <span>Saved Copy as New Frame! Continue editing...</span>
        </div>
      )}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-neutral-800 bg-[#0C0C0E] shrink-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-indigo-600/20 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center">
            <ImageIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-sm font-extrabold text-white tracking-tight flex items-center gap-1.5">
              <span>FrameEditor Studio</span>
              <span className="px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-sky-500/10 text-sky-400 text-[9px] font-mono border border-sky-500/10">v007-pro</span>
            </h2>
            <p className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500">{width}×{height}px</p>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Transport Toggle */}
        {index !== undefined && totalFrames !== undefined && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5 bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-800 rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1 shadow-inner">
            <button
              onClick={() => handleNavigate('prev')}
              disabled={index <= 0}
              className="p-1 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 disabled:opacity-20 text-neutral-300 hover:text-white rounded-md transition-colors cursor-pointer disabled:cursor-not-allowed"
              title="Save & Go to Previous Frame"
            >
              <ChevronLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
            </button>
            <span className="text-[10px] font-mono font-black text-neutral-400 uppercase tracking-widest px-1">
              Frame {index + 1} / {totalFrames}
            </span>
            <button
              onClick={() => handleNavigate('next')}
              disabled={index >= totalFrames - 1}
              className="p-1 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 disabled:opacity-20 text-neutral-300 hover:text-white rounded-md transition-colors cursor-pointer disabled:cursor-not-allowed"
              title="Save & Go to Next Frame"
            >
              <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" />
            </button>
          </div>
        )}

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setShowToolbar(!showToolbar)} 
            className={cn(
              "flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold border transition-colors cursor-pointer",
              showToolbar 
                ? "bg-indigo-600 border-indigo-500 text-white" 
                : "bg-neutral-800 border-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 hover:bg-neutral-700"
            )}
            title={showToolbar ? "Hide Editing Tools" : "Show Editing Tools"}
          >
            {showToolbar ? <EyeOff className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> : <Eye className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />}
            <span>Toolbar</span>
          </button>

          <button 
            onClick={() => setShowTTPanel(!showTTPanel)} 
            className={cn(
              "flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold border transition-colors cursor-pointer",
              showTTPanel 
                ? "bg-purple-600 border-purple-500 text-white shadow-lg shadow-purple-900/20" 
                : "bg-neutral-800 border-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 hover:bg-neutral-700"
            )}
            title="Toggle Text & Dialogue Panel (TT)"
          >
            <Type className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-purple-400 animate-pulse" />
            <span>tt</span>
          </button>

          <button 
            onClick={handleDownload} 
            className="p-2 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 rounded-lg border border-neutral-700 transition-colors cursor-pointer flex items-center justify-center"
            title="Export PNG"
          >
            <Download className="w-4 h-4 text-sky-400" />
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={handleSaveAsNew} 
            className="p-2 bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-500 text-white rounded-lg transition-colors cursor-pointer flex items-center justify-center"
            title="Save as New Frame"
          >
            <Plus className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={handleSave} 
            className="p-2 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white rounded-lg transition-colors cursor-pointer flex items-center justify-center"
            title="Apply to Frame"
          >
            <Check className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={onClose} 
            className="p-2 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-400 hover:text-neutral-200 rounded-lg transition-colors cursor-pointer" 
            title="Close Editor"
          >
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-1 overflow-hidden relative">
        <div className="w-14 bg-[#0C0C0E] border-r border-neutral-800 flex flex-col items-center py-4 gap-1.5 shrink-0 z-20">
          <button onClick={() => { setTool('select'); setShowShapesFlyout(false); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', tool === 'select' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Pointer Selection Tool"><MousePointer className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          <button onClick={() => { setTool('pen'); setShowShapesFlyout(false); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', tool === 'pen' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Draw Pen"><Pencil className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          <button onClick={() => { setTool('eraser'); setShowShapesFlyout(false); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', tool === 'eraser' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Eraser"><Eraser className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          <button onClick={() => { setTool('blur'); setShowShapesFlyout(false); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', tool === 'blur' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Blur Pen"><Droplet className="w-4 h-4" /></button>

          <div className="relative">
            <button onClick={() => { setShowShapesFlyout(prev => !prev); setTool(activeShapeTool); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', isShapeActive ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Shapes Tool">{getShapeIcon(activeShapeTool)}</button>
            {showShapesFlyout && (
              <div className="absolute left-12 top-0 bg-[#0C0C0E] border border-neutral-700/80 p-1 rounded-xl shadow-xl flex flex-col gap-1 z-30 min-w-[130px]">
                <div className="px-2 py-1 border-b border-neutral-800 mb-1"><span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider block">Drawing Shapes</span></div>
                <button onClick={() => handleShapeSelect('line')} className={cn('flex items-center gap-2 px-2.5 py-1.5 text-left text-xs rounded-lg transition-colors w-full cursor-pointer', activeShapeTool === 'line' && tool === 'line' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white font-bold' : 'text-neutral-300 hover:bg-neutral-800')}><Minus className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 text-neutral-400" /><span>Line</span></button>
                <button onClick={() => handleShapeSelect('arrow')} className={cn('flex items-center gap-2 px-2.5 py-1.5 text-left text-xs rounded-lg transition-colors w-full cursor-pointer', activeShapeTool === 'arrow' && tool === 'arrow' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white font-bold' : 'text-neutral-300 hover:bg-neutral-800')}><ArrowUpRight className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 text-neutral-400" /><span>Arrow</span></button>
                <button onClick={() => handleShapeSelect('rect')} className={cn('flex items-center gap-2 px-2.5 py-1.5 text-left text-xs rounded-lg transition-colors w-full cursor-pointer', activeShapeTool === 'rect' && tool === 'rect' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white font-bold' : 'text-neutral-300 hover:bg-neutral-800')}><Square className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 text-neutral-400" /><span>Rectangle</span></button>
                <button onClick={() => handleShapeSelect('ellipse')} className={cn('flex items-center gap-2 px-2.5 py-1.5 text-left text-xs rounded-lg transition-colors w-full cursor-pointer', activeShapeTool === 'ellipse' && tool === 'ellipse' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white font-bold' : 'text-neutral-300 hover:bg-neutral-800')}><Circle className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 text-neutral-400" /><span>Ellipse</span></button>
                <button onClick={() => handleShapeSelect('star')} className={cn('flex items-center gap-2 px-2.5 py-1.5 text-left text-xs rounded-lg transition-colors w-full cursor-pointer', activeShapeTool === 'star' && tool === 'star' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white font-bold' : 'text-neutral-300 hover:bg-neutral-800')}><Star className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 text-neutral-400" /><span>Star</span></button>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          <button onClick={() => { setTool('text'); setShowShapesFlyout(false); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', tool === 'text' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Text tool overlay"><Type className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          <button onClick={() => { setTool('crop'); setShowShapesFlyout(false); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', tool === 'crop' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Crop canvas"><Crop className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          <button onClick={() => { setTool('eyedropper'); setShowShapesFlyout(false); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', tool === 'eyedropper' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Eyedropper color picker"><Pipette className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          <button onClick={() => { setTool('move'); setShowShapesFlyout(false); cancelCrop(); }} className={cn('w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all cursor-pointer', tool === 'move' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-neutral-200')} title="Pan / Move drawing layer"><Move className="w-4 h-4" /></button>

          <div className="h-px w-8 bg-neutral-800 my-2" />
          
          <button onClick={handleUndo} disabled={historyIndex <= 0} className="w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 disabled:opacity-30 cursor-pointer" title="Undo drawing/text layer (Ctrl+Z)"><Undo2 className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          <button onClick={handleRedo} disabled={historyIndex >= history.length - 1} className="w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 disabled:opacity-30 cursor-pointer" title="Redo (Ctrl+Y)"><Redo2 className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          <button onClick={handleClear} className="w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center text-rose-400 hover:bg-neutral-800 hover:text-rose-300 cursor-pointer" title="Reset drawing layer"><Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
        </div>

        {/* TT Pop Out Panel: between tool strip and frame viewer */}
        {showTTPanel && (
          <div className="w-52 bg-[#0C0C0E] border-r border-neutral-800 flex flex-col p-4 gap-4 shrink-0 z-10 overflow-y-auto">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-neutral-800 pb-2">
              <span className="text-[10px] text-purple-400 font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1.5">
                <Type className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-purple-400" />
                Text Studio
              </span>
              <button 
                onClick={() => setShowTTPanel(false)}
                className="text-neutral-500 hover:text-neutral-300 p-1 rounded hover:bg-neutral-800 transition-colors cursor-pointer"
                title="Close Panel"
              >
                <X className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
              <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Layer Controls</span>
              <button 
                onClick={handleAddNewText} 
                className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 bg-violet-600/20 hover:bg-violet-600/30 text-violet-300 border border-violet-500/30 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold cursor-pointer transition-all w-full animate-pulse"
                title="Add standard Text Layer overlay"
              >
                <Plus className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> 
                txtLayer
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
              <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Dialogue Bubbles</span>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-1">
                <button 
                  onClick={() => handleAddDialogueBubble('speech')} 
                  className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 p-1.5 bg-neutral-900 hover:bg-neutral-800 text-neutral-200 hover:text-white rounded-lg border border-neutral-800 text-[10px] font-bold cursor-pointer transition-all"
                  title="Create a standard dialogue Speech Bubble layer"
                >
                  <MessageSquare className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-sky-400 animate-pulse" />
                  <span>Talk</span>
                </button>
                <button 
                  onClick={() => handleAddDialogueBubble('thought')} 
                  className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 p-1.5 bg-neutral-900 hover:bg-neutral-800 text-neutral-200 hover:text-white rounded-lg border border-neutral-800 text-[10px] font-bold cursor-pointer transition-all"
                  title="Create a cloud-shaped Thought Bubble layer"
                >
                  <Cloud className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-pink-400 animate-pulse" />
                  <span>Think</span>
                </button>
                <button 
                  onClick={() => handleAddDialogueBubble('narration')} 
                  className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 p-1.5 bg-neutral-900 hover:bg-neutral-800 text-neutral-200 hover:text-white rounded-lg border border-neutral-800 text-[10px] font-bold cursor-pointer transition-all"
                  title="Create a Narration Box layer"
                >
                  <StickyNote className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-amber-400 animate-pulse" />
                  <span>Desc</span>
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Transform Tools section for the active text layer */}
            {activeTextLayer && (
              <>
                {/* Text Content Input box */}
