                <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 mt-1 border-t border-neutral-800 pt-3">
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-violet-400 font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1">
                    <Type className="w-3 h-3 text-violet-400" />
                    Edit Content
                  </span>
                  <textarea
                    rows={2}
                    value={activeTextLayer.text}
                    onChange={e => {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ text: e.target.value });
                    }}
                    onBlur={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    className="w-full bg-neutral-950 border border-neutral-800 rounded p-1.5 text-xs text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-violet-500 resize-none font-medium"
                    placeholder="Type dialogue/text..."
                  />
                </div>

                {/* Bubble Settings / Text Colors section */}
                <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 mt-1 border-t border-neutral-800 pt-3">
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-sky-400 font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1">
                    <MessageSquare className="w-3 h-3 text-sky-400" />
                    Bubble Studio
                  </span>
                  
                  <button
                    onClick={() => {
                      const isBubble = !activeTextLayer.isSpeechBubble;
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ 
                        isSpeechBubble: isBubble,
                        bubbleType: isBubble ? 'speech' : undefined,
                        bubbleWidth: isBubble ? 220 : undefined,
                        bubbleHeight: isBubble ? 100 : undefined,
                        bubbleTailAlign: isBubble ? 'center' : undefined,
                        color: isBubble ? '#000000' : activeTextLayer.color,
                        fontFamily: isBubble ? 'Comic Sans MS, cursive' : activeTextLayer.fontFamily
                      }, true);
                    }}
                    className={cn(
                      "w-full py-1.5 text-[11px] font-extrabold rounded-lg border cursor-pointer transition-all flex items-center justify-center gap-2",
                      activeTextLayer.isSpeechBubble
                        ? "bg-sky-600/20 border-sky-500/40 text-sky-300"
                        : "bg-neutral-900 border-neutral-800 text-neutral-400 hover:text-white"
                    )}
                  >
                    <span>{activeTextLayer.isSpeechBubble ? "Is Bubble Style" : "Convert to Bubble"}</span>
                  </button>

                  {activeTextLayer.isSpeechBubble && (
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2.5 bg-neutral-950/40 border border-neutral-900 rounded-lg p-2">
                      {/* Style / Type Selector */}
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                        <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-bold uppercase">Style</span>
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-1 bg-neutral-950 border border-neutral-800 rounded p-0.5">
                          {(['speech', 'thought', 'narration'] as const).map((bType) => {
                            const labelMap = {
                              speech: 'Talk',
                              thought: 'Think',
                              narration: 'Desc'
                            };
                            return (
                              <button
                                key={bType}
                                onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleType: bType, isBold: bType === 'narration' ? true : activeTextLayer.isBold, isItalic: bType === 'thought' ? true : activeTextLayer.isItalic }, true)}
                                className={cn(
                                  "py-1 text-[9px] font-extrabold uppercase rounded cursor-pointer transition-all",
                                  (activeTextLayer.bubbleType || 'speech') === bType 
                                    ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white" 
                                    : "text-neutral-500 hover:text-neutral-300"
                                )}
                              >
                                {labelMap[bType]}
                              </button>
                            );
                          })}
                        </div>
                      </div>

                      {/* Tail Alignment */}
                      {activeTextLayer.bubbleType !== 'narration' && (
                        <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                          <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-bold uppercase">Tail Alignment</span>
                          <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-1 bg-neutral-950 border border-neutral-800 rounded p-0.5">
                            {(['left', 'center', 'right'] as const).map((align) => (
                              <button
                                key={align}
                                onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleTailAlign: align }, true)}
                                className={cn(
                                  "py-1 text-[9px] font-extrabold uppercase rounded cursor-pointer transition-all",
                                  (activeTextLayer.bubbleTailAlign || 'center') === align 
                                    ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white" 
                                    : "text-neutral-500 hover:text-neutral-300"
                                )}
                              >
                                {align}
                              </button>
                            ))}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      )}

                      {/* Tail Length */}
                      {(activeTextLayer.bubbleTailLength !== undefined || (activeTextLayer.bubbleType || 'speech') === 'speech') && (activeTextLayer.bubbleType || 'speech') === 'speech' && (
                        <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                          <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-bold uppercase">Tail / Quote Length</span>
                          <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-1 bg-neutral-950 border border-neutral-800 rounded p-0.5">
                            {(['short', 'medium', 'long'] as const).map((len) => (
                              <button
                                key={len}
                                onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleTailLength: len }, true)}
                                className={cn(
                                  "py-1 text-[9px] font-extrabold uppercase rounded cursor-pointer transition-all",
                                  (activeTextLayer.bubbleTailLength || 'medium') === len 
                                    ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white" 
                                    : "text-neutral-500 hover:text-neutral-300"
                                )}
                              >
                                {len}
                              </button>
                            ))}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      )}

                      {/* Bubble Background Color */}
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1 mt-1 border-t border-neutral-900 pt-2">
                        <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-bold uppercase">Bubble Bg Color</span>
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                          <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-0.5 flex-1">
                            {[
                              { value: '#ffffff', name: 'Wht' },
                              { value: '#fffdf2', name: 'Crm' },
                              { value: '#fef08a', name: 'Yel' },
                              { value: '#bbf7d0', name: 'Grn' },
                              { value: '#bae6fd', name: 'Blu' },
                              { value: '#e9d5ff', name: 'Pur' },
                              { value: '#fbcfe8', name: 'Pnk' },
                            ].map((bgOpt) => (
                              <button
                                key={bgOpt.value}
                                onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleBgColor: bgOpt.value }, true)}
                                className={cn(
                                  "w-4.5 h-4.5 rounded border transition-all cursor-pointer",
                                  (activeTextLayer.bubbleBgColor || (activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'thought' ? '#e8ecfb' : activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'narration' ? '#fffdf2' : '#ffffff')) === bgOpt.value
                                    ? "border-violet-500 scale-110 ring-1 ring-violet-500/35" 
                                    : "border-neutral-800 hover:scale-105"
                                )}
                                style={{ backgroundColor: bgOpt.value }}
                                title={bgOpt.name}
                              />
                            ))}
                          </div>
                          <input 
                            type="color" 
                            value={activeTextLayer.bubbleBgColor || (activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'thought' ? '#e8ecfb' : activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'narration' ? '#fffdf2' : '#ffffff')} 
                            onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleBgColor: e.target.value }, true)} 
                            className="w-5 h-5 rounded cursor-pointer bg-transparent border-0 shrink-0" 
                          />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}

                  {/* Text Color / Swatches */}
                  <div className="flex flex-col gap-1 border-t border-neutral-800 pt-2">
                    <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-bold uppercase">Text Color</span>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-1 flex-1">
                        {['#ffffff', '#facc15', '#ef4444', '#000000'].map((qc) => (
                          <button
                            key={qc}
                            onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ color: qc }, true)}
                            className={cn(
                              "h-5 rounded border border-neutral-800 cursor-pointer transition-transform hover:scale-105",
                              activeTextLayer.color === qc ? "ring-1 ring-violet-500 border-violet-500" : ""
                            )}
                            style={{ backgroundColor: qc }}
                            title={`Set text to ${qc}`}
                          />
                        ))}
                      </div>
                      <input 
                        type="color" 
                        value={activeTextLayer.color} 
                        onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ color: e.target.value }, true)} 
                        className="w-5 h-5 rounded cursor-pointer bg-transparent border-0 shrink-0" 
                        title="Custom text color"
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 mt-1 border-t border-neutral-800 pt-3">
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-purple-400 font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1">
                    <Sliders className="w-3 h-3 text-purple-400" />
                    Transform Studio
                  </span>

                  {/* Resize Font Size */}
                  <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                    <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px]">
                      <span className="text-neutral-400 font-bold">Font Size</span>
                      <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono font-bold">{activeTextLayer.fontSize}px</span>
                    </div>
                    <input 
                      type="range" 
                      min={10} 
                      max={120} 
                      value={activeTextLayer.fontSize} 
                      onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ fontSize: Number(e.target.value) })}
                      onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                      onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                      className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                    />
                  </div>

                  {/* General Scaling multipliers */}
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                      <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                        <span className="text-neutral-500 font-bold">Scale X</span>
                        <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono">{(activeTextLayer.scaleX !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.scaleX : 1).toFixed(1)}x</span>
                      </div>
                      <input 
                        type="range" 
                        min={0.2} 
                        max={5} 
                        step={0.1}
                        value={activeTextLayer.scaleX !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.scaleX : 1} 
                        onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ scaleX: Number(e.target.value) })}
                        onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                        onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                        className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                      />
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                      <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                        <span className="text-neutral-500 font-bold">Scale Y</span>
                        <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono">{(activeTextLayer.scaleY !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.scaleY : 1).toFixed(1)}x</span>
                      </div>
                      <input 
                        type="range" 
                        min={0.2} 
                        max={5} 
                        step={0.1}
                        value={activeTextLayer.scaleY !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.scaleY : 1} 
                        onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ scaleY: Number(e.target.value) })}
                        onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                        onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                        className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Speech Bubble Width/Height (if applicable) */}
                  {activeTextLayer.isSpeechBubble && (
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 p-1.5 rounded-lg border border-neutral-900 bg-[#060608]">
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                          <span className="text-sky-400 font-bold">Bubble Width</span>
                          <span className="text-sky-400 font-mono">{activeTextLayer.bubbleWidth || 220}px</span>
                        </div>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={80} 
                          max={600} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.bubbleWidth || 220} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleWidth: Number(e.target.value) })}
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-sky-500"
                        />
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                          <span className="text-sky-400 font-bold">Bubble Height</span>
                          <span className="text-sky-400 font-mono">{activeTextLayer.bubbleHeight || 100}px</span>
                        </div>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={40} 
                          max={400} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.bubbleHeight || 100} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleHeight: Number(e.target.value) })}
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-sky-500"
                        />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}

                  {/* Rotate Angle */}
                  <div className="flex flex-col gap-1 border-t border-neutral-900 pt-2">
                    <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px]">
                      <span className="text-neutral-400 font-bold">Rotate Angle</span>
                      <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono font-bold">{activeTextLayer.rotation !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.rotation : 0}°</span>
                    </div>
                    <input 
                      type="range" 
                      min={-180} 
                      max={180} 
                      value={activeTextLayer.rotation !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.rotation : 0} 
                      onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ rotation: Number(e.target.value) })}
                      onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                      onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                      className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                    />
                  </div>

                  {/* Perspective & 3D Warp */}
                  <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 border-t border-neutral-900 pt-2">
                    <span className="text-[10px] text-neutral-400 font-bold">3D Perspective</span>
                    
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                      <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                        <span className="text-neutral-500">Perspective Depth</span>
                        <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono">{activeTextLayer.perspective || 1000}px</span>
                      </div>
                      <input 
                        type="range" 
                        min={100} 
                        max={2000} 
                        step={50}
                        value={activeTextLayer.perspective || 1000} 
                        onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ perspective: Number(e.target.value) })}
                        onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                        onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                        className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                      />
                    </div>

                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                          <span className="text-neutral-500">3D Tilt X</span>
                          <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono">{activeTextLayer.rotateX || 0}°</span>
                        </div>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-80} 
                          max={80} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.rotateX || 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ rotateX: Number(e.target.value) })}
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                        />
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                          <span className="text-neutral-500">3D Tilt Y</span>
                          <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono">{activeTextLayer.rotateY || 0}°</span>
                        </div>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-80} 
                          max={80} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.rotateY || 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ rotateY: Number(e.target.value) })}
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                        />
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* Skews for custom shear */}
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                          <span className="text-neutral-500">Skew X</span>
                          <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono">{activeTextLayer.skewX || 0}°</span>
                        </div>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-60} 
                          max={60} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.skewX || 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ skewX: Number(e.target.value) })}
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                        />
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px]">
                          <span className="text-neutral-500">Skew Y</span>
                          <span className="text-violet-400 font-mono">{activeTextLayer.skewY || 0}°</span>
                        </div>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-60} 
                          max={60} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.skewY || 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ skewY: Number(e.target.value) })}
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-full h-1 bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-ew-resize accent-violet-500"
                        />
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    <button
                      onClick={() => {
                        updateSelectedTextProps({
                          rotation: 0,
                          scaleX: 1,
                          scaleY: 1,
                          skewX: 0,
                          skewY: 0,
                          rotateX: 0,
                          rotateY: 0,
                          perspective: 1000
                        }, true);
                      }}
                      className="mt-1 py-1 px-2 bg-neutral-950 hover:bg-neutral-900 text-[9px] font-bold text-neutral-400 hover:text-white rounded border border-neutral-800 flex items-center justify-center gap-1 transition-all cursor-pointer"
                    >
                      <RotateCcw className="w-3 h-3" />
                      <span>Reset Transforms</span>
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </>
            )}

            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-2 border-t border-neutral-800 pt-3">
              <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Canvas Visibility</span>
              <button 
                onClick={() => setHideAllTextLayers(!hideAllTextLayers)}
                className={cn(
                  "flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold border transition-all cursor-pointer w-full",
                  !hideAllTextLayers 
                    ? "bg-indigo-600/15 border-indigo-500/30 text-indigo-300 hover:bg-indigo-600/25" 
                    : "bg-slate-900 border-slate-800 text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-400"
                )}
                title="Toggle visibility of dialogue/text layers on the canvas (defaults to hide)"
              >
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                  {!hideAllTextLayers ? <Eye className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-indigo-400" /> : <EyeOff className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-slate-500" />}
                  <span>Text Layers</span>
                </div>
                <span className="text-[9px] uppercase px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-neutral-800 rounded text-neutral-400 font-mono">
                  {hideAllTextLayers ? "hide" : "show"}
                </span>
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
          {showToolbar && (
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-2 border-b border-slate-800 bg-slate-900/50 flex-wrap shrink-0">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
              {COLORS.map(c => (
                <button key={c} onClick={() => { setColor(c); if (selectedTextId) updateSelectedTextProps({ color: c }, true); }} className={cn('w-5.5 h-5.5 rounded-full border transition-transform cursor-pointer', color === c ? 'border-white scale-110 shadow-lg' : 'border-slate-800 hover:scale-105')} style={{ backgroundColor: c }} />
              ))}
              <input type="color" value={color} onChange={e => { setColor(e.target.value); if (selectedTextId) updateSelectedTextProps({ color: e.target.value }, true); }} className="w-7 h-7 rounded cursor-pointer bg-transparent border-0 ml-1" />
              <button onClick={resetColorPicker} className="p-1 px-2 bg-slate-800 hover:bg-slate-700 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200 rounded text-[10px] font-bold border border-slate-700 flex items-center gap-1 cursor-pointer"><RotateCcw className="w-3 h-3" /><span>Reset</span></button>
            </div>

            <div className="h-5 w-px bg-slate-800" />

            <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
              <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-extrabold uppercase">Brush</span>
              <input type="range" min={1} max={30} value={lineWidth} onChange={e => setLineWidth(Number(e.target.value))} className="w-20 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" />
              <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-6">{lineWidth}px</span>
            </div>

            {(tool === 'rect' || tool === 'ellipse' || tool === 'star') && (
              <>
                <div className="h-5 w-px bg-slate-800" />
                <label className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-bold cursor-pointer select-none"><input type="checkbox" checked={fill} onChange={e => setFill(e.target.checked)} className="accent-violet-500 cursor-pointer" />Fill Shape</label>
              </>
            )}

            <div className="h-5 w-px bg-slate-800" />

            <button 
              onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()} 
              className="flex items-center gap-1 px-2.5 py-1 bg-sky-600/30 hover:bg-sky-600/50 text-sky-300 border border-sky-500/30 rounded text-[10px] font-bold cursor-pointer transition-all"
              title="Import an image to overlay and make a collage"
            >
              <Plus className="w-3 h-3" /> Collage
            </button>
            <input 
              type="file" 
              ref={fileInputRef} 
              onChange={handleImageUpload} 
              accept="image/*" 
              className="hidden" 
            />

            <button 
              onClick={() => setShowAssetLibrary(!showAssetLibrary)} 
              className={cn(
                "flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2.5 py-1 rounded text-[10px] font-extrabold cursor-pointer transition-all border",
                showAssetLibrary 
                  ? "bg-pink-600 border-pink-500 text-white shadow-lg shadow-pink-900/30" 
                  : "bg-pink-600/20 hover:bg-pink-600/30 text-pink-300 border-pink-500/20"
              )}
              title="Open database-driven collage asset library (Stickers, Props, Characters)"
            >
              <FolderHeart className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-pink-400" />
              <span>AssetLib</span>
            </button>

            {(textLayers.length > 0 || imageLayers.length > 0) && (
              <button 
                onClick={handleBakeLayers} 
                className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2.5 py-1 bg-amber-600/30 hover:bg-amber-600/50 text-amber-300 border border-amber-500/30 rounded text-[10px] font-extrabold cursor-pointer transition-all animate-pulse shadow-md shadow-amber-950/20"
                title="Bake/Flatten all text and collage layers into the background canvas permanently so you can paint over them or apply filters"
              >
                <Check className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-amber-400" /> Bake
              </button>
            )}

            <div className="h-5 w-px bg-slate-800" />

            {/* Cinematic FX Filters bar */}
            <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-slate-900/80 border border-slate-800 rounded px-2.5 py-1">
              <select
                value={activeFilter}
                onChange={e => {
                  setActiveFilter(e.target.value);
                }}
                className="bg-transparent border-0 text-slate-300 text-[10px] font-extrabold outline-none cursor-pointer max-w-[110px]"
              >
                <option value="none" className="bg-[#0C0C0E]">Normal Style</option>
                <option value="grayscale" className="bg-[#0C0C0E]">Noir (B&W)</option>
                <option value="sepia" className="bg-[#0C0C0E]">Vintage Sepia</option>
                <option value="cinematic" className="bg-[#0C0C0E]">Cinematic</option>
                <option value="warm" className="bg-[#0C0C0E]">Warm Golden</option>
                <option value="cold" className="bg-[#0C0C0E]">Cold Cinema</option>
                <option value="high-contrast" className="bg-[#0C0C0E]">High Contrast</option>
                <option value="invert" className="bg-[#0C0C0E]">Negative (Invert)</option>
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="h-5 w-px bg-slate-800" />

            {/* Text settings toolbar: STAYS OPEN AT ALL TIMES */}
            {showTextSettings && (
              <>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-slate-800/40 px-2 py-1 rounded border border-slate-700/60 shrink-0">
              <span className="text-[10px] text-purple-400 font-extrabold uppercase flex items-center gap-1">
                <Type className="w-3 h-3 text-purple-400" />
                <span>{activeImageLayer ? "Overlay Settings:" : ""}</span>
              </span>
              
              {/* Text input section also on the text editor toolbar! */}
              <input 
                type="text" 
                value={activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.text : textValue} 
                onChange={e => {
                  const val = e.target.value;
                  if (activeTextLayer) {
                    updateSelectedTextProps({ text: val });
                  } else {
                    setTextValue(val);
                  }
                }} 
                onBlur={() => {
                  if (activeTextLayer) {
                    pushHistory();
                  }
                }}
                disabled={!!activeImageLayer}
                placeholder={activeImageLayer ? "[Image Overlay Selected]" : "Type storyboard text..."} 
                className="bg-slate-900 border border-slate-700 text-white text-[10px] rounded px-1.5 py-1 w-36 focus:border-violet-500 outline-none placeholder:text-neutral-600 font-bold disabled:opacity-40" 
              />

              <select 
                value={activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.fontFamily : fontFamily} 
                onChange={e => {
                  const fam = e.target.value;
                  if (activeTextLayer) {
                    updateSelectedTextProps({ fontFamily: fam }, true);
                  } else {
                    setFontFamily(fam);
                  }
                }} 
                disabled={!!activeImageLayer}
                className="bg-slate-900 border border-slate-700 text-slate-300 text-[10px] rounded px-1.5 py-1 font-bold outline-none cursor-pointer disabled:opacity-40"
              >
                {FONT_FAMILIES.map(f => (
                  <option key={f} value={f}>{f.split(',')[0]}</option>
                ))}
              </select>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold">Size:</span>
                <input 
                  type="range" 
                  min={10} 
                  max={activeImageLayer ? 800 : 120} 
                  value={activeImageLayer ? activeImageLayer.width : (activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.fontSize : fontSize)} 
                  onChange={e => {
                    const sz = Number(e.target.value);
                    if (activeImageLayer) {
                      const aspect = activeImageLayer.width / activeImageLayer.height;
                      const nextH = Math.max(10, Math.round(sz / aspect));
                      setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, width: sz, height: nextH } : l));
                    } else if (activeTextLayer) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ fontSize: sz });
                    } else {
                      setFontSize(sz);
                    }
                  }} 
                  onMouseUp={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
                  }}
                  onTouchEnd={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
                  }}
                  className="w-16 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                />
                <input 
                  type="number" 
                  min={10} 
                  max={activeImageLayer ? 800 : 120} 
                  value={activeImageLayer ? activeImageLayer.width : (activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.fontSize : fontSize)} 
                  onChange={e => {
                    const sz = Number(e.target.value);
                    if (activeImageLayer) {
                      const aspect = activeImageLayer.width / activeImageLayer.height;
                      const nextH = Math.max(10, Math.round(sz / aspect));
                      setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, width: sz, height: nextH } : l));
                    } else if (activeTextLayer) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ fontSize: sz }, true);
                    } else {
                      setFontSize(sz);
                    }
                  }} 
                  className="w-10 bg-slate-900 border border-slate-700 text-slate-300 text-[10px] rounded px-1 text-center font-mono outline-none py-0.5" 
                />
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                <button 
                  onClick={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ isBold: !activeTextLayer.isBold }, true);
                    } else {
                      setFontBold(!fontBold);
                    }
                  }} 
                  disabled={!!activeImageLayer}
                  className={cn('p-1 rounded transition-all cursor-pointer disabled:opacity-30', (activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.isBold : fontBold) ? 'bg-violet-600 text-white' : 'bg-slate-900 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200')}
                  title="Bold text"
                >
                  <Bold className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                </button>
                <button 
                  onClick={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ isItalic: !activeTextLayer.isItalic }, true);
                    } else {
                      setFontItalic(!fontItalic);
                    }
                  }} 
                  disabled={!!activeImageLayer}
                  className={cn('p-1 rounded transition-all cursor-pointer disabled:opacity-30', (activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.isItalic : fontItalic) ? 'bg-violet-600 text-white' : 'bg-slate-900 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200')}
                  title="Italic text"
                >
                  <Italic className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                </button>
                <button 
                  onClick={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ hasOutline: !activeTextLayer.hasOutline }, true);
                    } else {
                      setFontOutline(!fontOutline);
                    }
                  }} 
                  disabled={!!activeImageLayer}
                  className={cn('px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[8px] font-extrabold transition-all cursor-pointer border disabled:opacity-30', (activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.hasOutline : fontOutline) ? 'bg-sky-600 border-sky-500 text-white' : 'bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-slate-400')}
                  title="Toggle Text Stroke Outline"
                >
                  OL
                </button>
              </div>

              {/* Directly accessible text color selection and quick-swatches */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 ml-1 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                <input 
                  type="color" 
                  value={activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.color : color} 
                  onChange={e => {
                    const col = e.target.value;
                    if (activeTextLayer) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ color: col }, true);
                    } else {
                      setColor(col);
                    }
                  }} 
                  disabled={!!activeImageLayer}
                  className="w-5 h-5 rounded cursor-pointer bg-transparent border-0 disabled:opacity-35"
                  title="Text Color Picker"
                />
                
                {/* Simple high-contrast quick-colors for storyboarding */}
                <div className="flex gap-1">
                  {['#ffffff', '#facc15', '#ef4444', '#000000'].map((qc) => (
                    <button
                      key={qc}
                      onClick={() => {
                        if (activeTextLayer) {
                          updateSelectedTextProps({ color: qc }, true);
                        } else {
                          setColor(qc);
                        }
                      }}
                      disabled={!!activeImageLayer}
                      className={cn(
                        "w-3.5 h-3.5 rounded-full border border-slate-600 cursor-pointer transition-transform hover:scale-110 disabled:opacity-20",
                        (activeTextLayer ? activeTextLayer.color : color) === qc ? "ring-1 ring-violet-500 scale-110" : "opacity-80 hover:opacity-100"
                      )}
                      style={{ backgroundColor: qc }}
                      title={`Set text to ${qc === '#ffffff' ? 'White' : qc === '#facc15' ? 'Yellow' : qc === '#ef4444' ? 'Red' : 'Black'}`}
                    />
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="h-4 w-px bg-slate-700" />

              {/* Convert to Bubble Button */}
              <button
                onClick={() => {
                  if (activeTextLayer) {
                    const isBubble = !activeTextLayer.isSpeechBubble;
                    updateSelectedTextProps({ 
                      isSpeechBubble: isBubble,
                      bubbleType: isBubble ? 'speech' : undefined,
                      bubbleWidth: isBubble ? 220 : undefined,
                      bubbleHeight: isBubble ? 100 : undefined,
                      bubbleTailAlign: isBubble ? 'center' : undefined,
                      color: isBubble ? '#000000' : activeTextLayer.color,
                      fontFamily: isBubble ? 'Comic Sans MS, cursive' : activeTextLayer.fontFamily
                    }, true);
                  }
                }}
                disabled={!activeTextLayer}
                className={cn(
                  "px-2 py-0.5 text-[8px] font-extrabold rounded cursor-pointer transition-all border disabled:opacity-35 shrink-0",
                  activeTextLayer?.isSpeechBubble
                    ? "bg-sky-600/20 border-sky-500/40 text-sky-300"
                    : "bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200"
                )}
                title="Convert this text layer to/from a speech dialogue bubble style"
              >
                {activeTextLayer?.isSpeechBubble ? "Is Bubble" : "Make Bubble"}
              </button>

              {/* Dialogue Bubble options: visible when the active layer is a speech bubble */}
              {/* Dialogue Bubble options: visible when the active layer is a speech bubble */}
              {activeTextLayer?.isSpeechBubble && (
                <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2 shrink-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                    <span className="text-[9px] text-sky-400 font-extrabold uppercase">Style:</span>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1 bg-slate-900 border border-slate-700 rounded p-0.5">
                      {(['speech', 'thought', 'narration'] as const).map((bType) => {
                        const labelMap = {
                          speech: 'Talk',
                          thought: 'Think',
                          narration: 'Desc'
                        };
                        return (
                          <button
                            key={bType}
                            onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleType: bType, isBold: bType === 'narration' ? true : activeTextLayer.isBold, isItalic: bType === 'thought' ? true : activeTextLayer.isItalic }, true)}
                            className={cn(
                              "px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[8px] font-extrabold uppercase rounded cursor-pointer transition-all",
                              (activeTextLayer.bubbleType || 'speech') === bType 
                                ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white" 
                                : "text-neutral-400 hover:text-neutral-200"
                            )}
                            title={`Set style to ${bType}`}
                          >
                            {labelMap[bType]}
                          </button>
                        );
                      })}
                    </div>

                    {activeTextLayer.bubbleType !== 'narration' && (
                      <>
                        <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-500 font-bold ml-1">Tail:</span>
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 bg-slate-900 border border-slate-700 rounded p-0.5">
                          {(['left', 'center', 'right'] as const).map((align) => (
                            <button
                              key={align}
                              onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleTailAlign: align }, true)}
                              className={cn(
                                "px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[8px] font-extrabold uppercase rounded cursor-pointer transition-all",
                                (activeTextLayer.bubbleTailAlign || 'center') === align 
                                  ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white" 
                                  : "text-neutral-400 hover:text-neutral-200"
                              )}
                              title={`Tail pointer alignment ${align}`}
                            >
                              {align}
                            </button>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      </>
                    )}

                    {(activeTextLayer.bubbleTailLength !== undefined || (activeTextLayer.bubbleType || 'speech') === 'speech') && (activeTextLayer.bubbleType || 'speech') === 'speech' && (
                      <>
                        <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-500 font-bold ml-1">Quote:</span>
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 bg-slate-900 border border-slate-700 rounded p-0.5">
                          {(['short', 'medium', 'long'] as const).map((len) => (
                            <button
                              key={len}
                              onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleTailLength: len }, true)}
                              className={cn(
                                "px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[8px] font-extrabold uppercase rounded cursor-pointer transition-all",
                                (activeTextLayer.bubbleTailLength || 'medium') === len 
                                  ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white" 
                                  : "text-neutral-400 hover:text-neutral-200"
                              )}
                              title={`Tail quote bar length ${len}`}
                            >
                              {len}
                            </button>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      </>
                    )}

                    {/* Bubble Background Color Picker */}
                    <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-500 font-bold ml-1">Bg:</span>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1 bg-slate-900 border border-slate-700 rounded p-0.5">
                      {[
                        { value: '#ffffff', name: 'White' },
                        { value: '#fffdf2', name: 'Cream' },
                        { value: '#fef08a', name: 'Yellow' },
                        { value: '#bbf7d0', name: 'Green' },
                        { value: '#bae6fd', name: 'Blue' },
                        { value: '#e9d5ff', name: 'Purple' },
                        { value: '#fbcfe8', name: 'Pink' },
                      ].map((bgOpt) => (
                        <button
                          key={bgOpt.value}
                          onClick={() => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleBgColor: bgOpt.value }, true)}
                          className={cn(
                            "w-3.5 h-3.5 rounded border transition-all cursor-pointer",
                            (activeTextLayer.bubbleBgColor || (activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'thought' ? '#e8ecfb' : activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'narration' ? '#fffdf2' : '#ffffff')) === bgOpt.value
                              ? "border-violet-500 scale-110 shadow" 
                              : "border-slate-800 hover:scale-105"
                          )}
                          style={{ backgroundColor: bgOpt.value }}
                          title={bgOpt.name}
                        />
                      ))}
                      <input 
                        type="color" 
                        value={activeTextLayer.bubbleBgColor || (activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'thought' ? '#e8ecfb' : activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'narration' ? '#fffdf2' : '#ffffff')} 
                        onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ bubbleBgColor: e.target.value }, true)} 
                        className="w-4 h-4 rounded cursor-pointer bg-transparent border-0" 
                        title="Custom Bubble Background Color"
                      />
                    </div>

                    {/* Toggle button for Transform & Presets Panel (icon only) */}
                    <div className="h-4 w-px bg-slate-700/60 ml-1.5 shrink-0" />
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setShowBubbleStylePanel(!showBubbleStylePanel)}
                      className={cn(
                        "p-1 rounded transition-all cursor-pointer shrink-0 border",
                        showBubbleStylePanel 
                          ? "bg-violet-600 border-violet-500 text-white shadow shadow-violet-950/40" 
                          : "bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200"
                      )}
                      title="Toggle Transform Style & Presets Panel (Rotate, Skew, Tilt, Persp, Presets)"
                    >
                      <Sliders className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                    </button>
                  </div>

                  {/* Dedicated Style Panel: shown below the basic properties */}
                  {showBubbleStylePanel && (
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-slate-900 border border-violet-500/30 rounded p-1.5 mt-1 text-[9px] shrink-0">
                      {/* Rotate */}
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                        <span className="text-slate-500 font-bold" title="Rotate selected bubble layer">Rotate:</span>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-180} 
                          max={180} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.rotation !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.rotation : 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ rotation: Number(e.target.value) })} 
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-12 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                        />
                        <span className="text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                          {activeTextLayer.rotation !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.rotation : 0}°
                        </span>
                      </div>

                      {/* Skew X */}
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 border-l border-slate-700 pl-1.5">
                        <span className="text-slate-500 font-bold" title="Skew X (Shear)">Skew X:</span>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-60} 
                          max={60} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.skewX || 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ skewX: Number(e.target.value) })} 
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-12 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                        />
                        <span className="text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                          {activeTextLayer.skewX || 0}°
                        </span>
                      </div>

                      {/* Skew Y */}
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 border-l border-slate-700 pl-1.5">
                        <span className="text-slate-500 font-bold" title="Skew Y (Shear)">Skew Y:</span>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-60} 
                          max={60} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.skewY || 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ skewY: Number(e.target.value) })} 
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-12 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                        />
                        <span className="text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                          {activeTextLayer.skewY || 0}°
                        </span>
                      </div>

                      {/* Tilt X */}
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 border-l border-slate-700 pl-1.5">
                        <span className="text-slate-500 font-bold" title="Tilt X (3D rotation)">Tilt X:</span>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-80} 
                          max={80} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.rotateX || 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ rotateX: Number(e.target.value) })} 
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-12 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                        />
                        <span className="text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                          {activeTextLayer.rotateX || 0}°
                        </span>
                      </div>

                      {/* Tilt Y */}
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 border-l border-slate-700 pl-1.5">
                        <span className="text-slate-500 font-bold" title="Tilt Y (3D rotation)">Tilt Y:</span>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={-80} 
                          max={80} 
                          value={activeTextLayer.rotateY || 0} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ rotateY: Number(e.target.value) })} 
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-12 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                        />
                        <span className="text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                          {activeTextLayer.rotateY || 0}°
                        </span>
                      </div>

                      {/* Perspective */}
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 border-l border-slate-700 pl-1.5">
                        <span className="text-slate-500 font-bold" title="3D perspective focal depth">Persp:</span>
                        <input 
                          type="range" 
                          min={100} 
                          max={2000} 
                          step={50}
                          value={activeTextLayer.perspective || 1000} 
                          onChange={e => updateSelectedTextProps({ perspective: Number(e.target.value) })} 
                          onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                          className="w-12 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                        />
                        <span className="text-slate-400 font-mono w-8 text-right">
                          {activeTextLayer.perspective || 1000}px
                        </span>
                      </div>

                      {/* Dialogue Bubble Presets Selection & Save */}
                      <div className="h-4 w-px bg-slate-700 ml-1.5 shrink-0" />
                      <span className="text-violet-400 font-extrabold uppercase shrink-0">Presets:</span>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 bg-slate-950 border border-slate-800 rounded px-1 py-0.5 max-w-[150px] overflow-x-auto no-scrollbar shrink-0">
                        {bubblePresets.map((preset) => {
                          const isActive = activeTextLayer.bubbleType === preset.bubbleType &&
                            (activeTextLayer.bubbleBgColor || (activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'thought' ? '#e8ecfb' : activeTextLayer.bubbleType === 'narration' ? '#fffdf2' : '#ffffff')) === preset.bubbleBgColor &&
                            (activeTextLayer.bubbleTailLength || 'medium') === preset.bubbleTailLength &&
                            (activeTextLayer.bubbleTailAlign || 'center') === preset.bubbleTailAlign;
                          return (
                            <div key={preset.id} className="relative group/preset flex items-center shrink-0">
                              <button
                                onClick={() => applyPreset(preset)}
                                className={cn(
                                  "px-1 py-0.5 text-[8px] font-bold rounded cursor-pointer border transition-all truncate max-w-[70px] leading-none h-3.5 flex items-center",
                                  isActive
                                    ? "bg-violet-600/30 border-violet-500 text-violet-200"
                                    : "bg-slate-900 border-slate-800 text-slate-300 hover:text-white"
                                )}
                                style={{ borderLeftColor: preset.bubbleBgColor, borderLeftWidth: '3px' }}
                                title={`Apply preset: ${preset.name} (${preset.bubbleType})`}
                              >
                                {preset.name}
                              </button>
                              {!preset.isDefault && (
                                <button
                                  onClick={(e) => deletePreset(preset.id, e)}
                                  className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 flex items-center justify-center w-3 h-3 bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-500 text-white rounded-full text-[8px] font-extrabold cursor-pointer z-10"
                                  title="Delete preset"
                                >
                                  ×
                                </button>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          );
                        })}
                      </div>
                      <button
                        onClick={() => {
                          const name = prompt("Enter a name for your custom bubble preset:", `Bubble ${bubblePresets.length + 1}`);
                          if (name) {
                            saveCurrentPreset(name);
                          }
                        }}
                        className="px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-violet-600/20 border border-violet-500/40 text-violet-300 hover:bg-violet-600/30 hover:border-violet-500 rounded text-[8px] font-extrabold transition-all cursor-pointer shrink-0 leading-none"
                        title="Save current style as a preset"
                      >
                        + SAVE PRESET
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Rotation, horizontal scaling, and vertical scaling */}
              {!activeTextLayer?.isSpeechBubble && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold" title="Rotate selected layer">Rotate:</span>
                  <input 
                    type="range" 
                    min={-180} 
                    max={180} 
                    value={activeImageLayer ? (activeImageLayer.rotation !== undefined ? activeImageLayer.rotation : 0) : (activeTextLayer ? (activeTextLayer.rotation !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.rotation : 0) : textRotation)} 
                    onChange={e => {
                      const rot = Number(e.target.value);
                      if (activeImageLayer) {
                        setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, rotation: rot } : l));
                      } else if (activeTextLayer) {
                        updateSelectedTextProps({ rotation: rot });
                      } else {
                        setTextRotation(rot);
                      }
                    }} 
                    onMouseUp={() => {
                      if (activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
                    }}
                    onTouchEnd={() => {
                      if (activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
                    }}
                    className="w-14 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                  />
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-7 text-right">
                    {activeImageLayer ? (activeImageLayer.rotation !== undefined ? activeImageLayer.rotation : 0) : (activeTextLayer ? (activeTextLayer.rotation !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.rotation : 0) : textRotation)}°
                  </span>
                </div>
              )}

              <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold" title={activeImageLayer ? "Adjust Image absolute width" : "Independent text horizontal stretch scale"}>
                  {activeImageLayer ? "Width:" : "W-Scale:"}
                </span>
                <input 
                  type="range" 
                  min={activeImageLayer ? 10 : 0.2} 
                  max={activeImageLayer ? 1280 : 5.0} 
                  step={activeImageLayer ? 1 : 0.1}
                  value={activeImageLayer ? activeImageLayer.width : (activeTextLayer ? (activeTextLayer.scaleX !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.scaleX : 1) : textScaleX)} 
                  onChange={e => {
                    const val = Number(e.target.value);
                    if (activeImageLayer) {
                      setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, width: Math.round(val) } : l));
                    } else if (activeTextLayer) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ scaleX: val });
                    } else {
                      setTextScaleX(val);
                    }
                  }} 
                  onMouseUp={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
                  }}
                  onTouchEnd={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
                  }}
                  className="w-14 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                />
                <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-7 text-right">
                  {activeImageLayer ? `${activeImageLayer.width}px` : (activeTextLayer ? (activeTextLayer.scaleX !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.scaleX : 1).toFixed(1) + 'x' : textScaleX.toFixed(1) + 'x')}
                </span>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold" title={activeImageLayer ? "Adjust Image absolute height" : "Independent text vertical stretch scale"}>
                  {activeImageLayer ? "Height:" : "H-Scale:"}
                </span>
                <input 
                  type="range" 
                  min={activeImageLayer ? 10 : 0.2} 
                  max={activeImageLayer ? 720 : 5.0} 
                  step={activeImageLayer ? 1 : 0.1}
                  value={activeImageLayer ? activeImageLayer.height : (activeTextLayer ? (activeTextLayer.scaleY !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.scaleY : 1) : textScaleY)} 
                  onChange={e => {
                    const val = Number(e.target.value);
                    if (activeImageLayer) {
                      setImageLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === selectedImageId ? { ...l, height: Math.round(val) } : l));
                    } else if (activeTextLayer) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps({ scaleY: val });
                    } else {
                      setTextScaleY(val);
                    }
                  }} 
                  onMouseUp={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
                  }}
                  onTouchEnd={() => {
                    if (activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers);
                  }}
                  className="w-14 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                />
                <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-7 text-right">
                  {activeImageLayer ? `${activeImageLayer.height}px` : (activeTextLayer ? (activeTextLayer.scaleY !== undefined ? activeTextLayer.scaleY : 1).toFixed(1) + 'x' : textScaleY.toFixed(1) + 'x')}
                </span>
              </div>

              {(activeTextLayer || activeImageLayer) && (
                <>
                  {!activeTextLayer?.isSpeechBubble && (
                    <>
                      <div className="h-4 w-px bg-slate-700" />
                      <button 
                        onClick={() => setShow3DWarpBar(!show3DWarpBar)}
                        className={cn(
                          "flex items-center gap-1 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[9px] font-extrabold transition-all cursor-pointer border shrink-0",
                          show3DWarpBar 
                            ? 'bg-violet-600/20 border-violet-500/40 text-violet-300 shadow-md shadow-violet-950/10' 
                            : 'bg-slate-900 border-slate-800 text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300'
                        )}
                        title="Toggle 3D Distortion & Warp settings bar visibility"
                      >
                        {show3DWarpBar ? <Eye className="w-3 h-3 text-violet-400" /> : <EyeOff className="w-3 h-3 text-slate-500" />}
                        <span>3D Warp</span>
                      </button>
                    </>
                  )}

                  <div className="h-4 w-px bg-slate-700" />
                  <button 
                    onClick={() => {
                      if (activeTextLayer) {
                        const nextLayers = textLayers.filter(l => l.id !== selectedTextId);
                        setTextLayers(nextLayers);
                        setSelectedTextId(null);
                        pushHistory(nextLayers, imageLayers);
                      } else if (activeImageLayer) {
                        const nextLayers = imageLayers.filter(l => l.id !== selectedImageId);
                        setImageLayers(nextLayers);
                        setSelectedImageId(null);
                        pushHistory(textLayers, nextLayers);
                      }
                    }} 
                    className="p-1 hover:bg-slate-700/80 text-rose-400 hover:text-rose-300 rounded cursor-pointer"
                    title="Delete selected layer"
                  >
                    <Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                  </button>
                </>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Advanced Distortion, Perspective & 3D Warp Toolbar: visible only when a layer is selected and show3DWarpBar is enabled */}
            {(selectedTextId || selectedImageId) && !activeTextLayer?.isSpeechBubble && show3DWarpBar && (
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-slate-800/40 px-2.5 py-1 rounded border border-violet-500/30 shrink-0">
                <span className="text-[10px] text-violet-400 font-extrabold uppercase flex items-center gap-1">
                  <Sparkles className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-violet-400 animate-pulse" />
                  <span>3D Distortion & Warp:</span>
                </span>

                {/* Skew X */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold" title="Skew horizontally (shear)">Skew X:</span>
                  <input 
                    type="range" 
                    min={-60} 
                    max={60} 
                    value={
                      selectedImageId 
                        ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.skewX || 0) 
                        : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.skewX || 0)
                    } 
                    onChange={e => {
                      const val = Number(e.target.value);
                      if (selectedImageId) {
                        updateSelectedImageProps({ skewX: val });
                      } else if (selectedTextId) {
                        updateSelectedTextProps({ skewX: val });
                      }
                    }} 
                    onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    className="w-14 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                  />
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                    {selectedImageId 
                      ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.skewX || 0) 
                      : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.skewX || 0)}°
                  </span>
                </div>

                {/* Skew Y */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold" title="Skew vertically (shear)">Skew Y:</span>
                  <input 
                    type="range" 
                    min={-60} 
                    max={60} 
                    value={
                      selectedImageId 
                        ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.skewY || 0) 
                        : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.skewY || 0)
                    } 
                    onChange={e => {
                      const val = Number(e.target.value);
                      if (selectedImageId) {
                        updateSelectedImageProps({ skewY: val });
                      } else if (selectedTextId) {
                        updateSelectedTextProps({ skewY: val });
                      }
                    }} 
                    onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    className="w-14 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                  />
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                    {selectedImageId 
                      ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.skewY || 0) 
                      : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.skewY || 0)}°
                  </span>
                </div>

                {/* Rotate 3D X (Pitch) */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold" title="3D rotation around horizontal axis (Top/Bottom perspective tilt)">Tilt X:</span>
                  <input 
                    type="range" 
                    min={-80} 
                    max={80} 
                    value={
                      selectedImageId 
                        ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.rotateX || 0) 
                        : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.rotateX || 0)
                    } 
                    onChange={e => {
                      const val = Number(e.target.value);
                      if (selectedImageId) {
                        updateSelectedImageProps({ rotateX: val });
                      } else if (selectedTextId) {
                        updateSelectedTextProps({ rotateX: val });
                      }
                    }} 
                    onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    className="w-14 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                  />
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                    {selectedImageId 
                      ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.rotateX || 0) 
                      : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.rotateX || 0)}°
                  </span>
                </div>

                {/* Rotate 3D Y (Yaw) */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold" title="3D rotation around vertical axis (Left/Right perspective tilt)">Tilt Y:</span>
                  <input 
                    type="range" 
                    min={-80} 
                    max={80} 
                    value={
                      selectedImageId 
                        ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.rotateY || 0) 
                        : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.rotateY || 0)
                    } 
                    onChange={e => {
                      const val = Number(e.target.value);
                      if (selectedImageId) {
                        updateSelectedImageProps({ rotateY: val });
                      } else if (selectedTextId) {
                        updateSelectedTextProps({ rotateY: val });
                      }
                    }} 
                    onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    className="w-14 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                  />
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-6 text-right">
                    {selectedImageId 
                      ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.rotateY || 0) 
                      : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.rotateY || 0)}°
                  </span>
                </div>

                {/* 3D Perspective Depth */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-l border-slate-700/60 pl-2">
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold" title="3D Perspective focal depth (lower is more intense warp)">Persp:</span>
                  <input 
                    type="range" 
                    min={100} 
                    max={2000} 
                    step={50}
                    value={
                      selectedImageId 
                        ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.perspective || 1000) 
                        : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.perspective || 1000)
                    } 
                    onChange={e => {
                      const val = Number(e.target.value);
                      if (selectedImageId) {
                        updateSelectedImageProps({ perspective: val });
                      } else if (selectedTextId) {
                        updateSelectedTextProps({ perspective: val });
                      }
                    }} 
                    onMouseUp={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    onTouchEnd={() => pushHistory(textLayers, imageLayers)}
                    className="w-14 accent-violet-500 cursor-ew-resize" 
                  />
                  <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-400 font-mono w-10 text-right">
                    {selectedImageId 
                      ? (imageLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedImageId)?.perspective || 1000) 
                      : (textLayers.find(l => l.id === selectedTextId)?.perspective || 1000)}px
                  </span>
                </div>

                <div className="h-4 w-px bg-slate-700" />

                <button
                  onClick={() => {
                    const rPatch = { skewX: 0, skewY: 0, rotateX: 0, rotateY: 0, perspective: 1000 };
                    if (selectedImageId) {
                      updateSelectedImageProps(rPatch, true);
                    } else if (selectedTextId) {
                      updateSelectedTextProps(rPatch, true);
                    }
                  }}
                  className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-slate-900 hover:bg-slate-800 text-[9px] font-bold text-slate-300 rounded border border-slate-700 hover:text-white transition-colors cursor-pointer"
                  title="Reset 3D and Distortion Transforms back to default"
                >
                  Reset Warp
                </button>
              </div>
            )}
              </>
            )}

            {isCropping && (
              <>
                <div className="h-5 w-px bg-slate-800" />
                <span className="text-[10px] text-purple-400 font-bold">Crop selection ready</span>
                <button onClick={applyCrop} className="px-2.5 py-1 bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-500 text-white rounded text-[10px] font-extrabold flex items-center gap-1 transition-colors cursor-pointer"><Check className="w-3 h-3" /> Apply Crop</button>
                <button onClick={cancelCrop} className="px-2.5 py-1 bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200 rounded text-[10px] font-bold border border-slate-700 transition-colors cursor-pointer">Cancel</button>
              </>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

          <div ref={containerRef} className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center bg-slate-950 p-6 overflow-auto">
            <div className="relative shadow-2xl shadow-black/80 border border-slate-800 rounded-lg overflow-hidden checkerboard-bg" style={{ width: displayW, height: displayH }} onClick={() => { setSelectedTextId(null); setEditingTextInPlace(null); }}>
              <canvas 
                ref={canvasRef}
