                className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full" 
                style={{ 
                  imageRendering: 'auto',
                  filter: activeFilter === 'grayscale' ? 'grayscale(100%)' :
                          activeFilter === 'sepia' ? 'sepia(80%)' :
                          activeFilter === 'cinematic' ? 'contrast(120%) brightness(95%) saturate(85%)' :
                          activeFilter === 'warm' ? 'sepia(30%) saturate(140%) contrast(110%)' :
                          activeFilter === 'cold' ? 'saturate(85%) brightness(105%) contrast(95%)' :
                          activeFilter === 'high-contrast' ? 'contrast(150%)' :
                          activeFilter === 'invert' ? 'invert(100%)' : 'none'
                }} 
              />
              <canvas 
                ref={overlayRef} 
                className={cn("absolute inset-0 w-full h-full z-10", tool === 'move' ? (isPanning ? 'cursor-grabbing' : 'cursor-grab') : tool === 'select' ? 'cursor-default' : 'cursor-crosshair')} 
                onMouseDown={handlePointerDown} 
                onMouseMove={handlePointerMove} 
                onMouseUp={handlePointerUp} 
                onMouseLeave={handlePointerUp} 
                onTouchStart={handlePointerDown} 
                onTouchMove={handlePointerMove} 
                onTouchEnd={handlePointerUp} 
                onClick={(e) => {
                  if (justAddedTextRef.current) {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    justAddedTextRef.current = false;
                    return;
                  }
                  if (tool === 'select') {
                    setSelectedTextId(null);
                    setSelectedImageId(null);
                    setEditingTextInPlace(null);
                  } else {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                  }
                }}
              />

              <div className="absolute inset-0 z-20 pointer-events-none">
                {imageLayers.map((layer) => {
                  const isSelected = layer.id === selectedImageId;
                  const imageDisplayW = layer.width * displayScale;
                  const imageDisplayH = layer.height * displayScale;
                  return (
                    <div
                      key={layer.id}
                      style={{
                        position: 'absolute',
                        left: `${(layer.x / width) * 100}%`,
                        top: `${(layer.y / height) * 100}%`,
                        transform: `translate(-50%, -50%) rotate(${layer.rotation || 0}deg) skew(${layer.skewX || 0}deg, ${layer.skewY || 0}deg) perspective(${layer.perspective || 1000}px) rotateX(${layer.rotateX || 0}deg) rotateY(${layer.rotateY || 0}deg)`,
                        transformOrigin: 'center center',
                        pointerEvents: 'auto',
                        width: imageDisplayW,
                        height: imageDisplayH
                      }}
                      onMouseDown={(e) => handleImageMouseDown(e, layer)}
                      onTouchStart={(e) => handleImageTouchStart(e, layer)}
                      onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
                    >
                      <div
                        className={cn(
                          "w-full h-full relative select-none group border",
                          isSelected ? "ring-2 ring-sky-500/80 bg-slate-950/20 border-sky-500" : "hover:border-white/20 border-transparent"
                        )}
                      >
                        <img
                          src={layer.src}
                          alt=""
                          className="w-full h-full object-contain pointer-events-none"
                        />
                        {isSelected && (
                          <>
                            <div className="absolute -top-1 -left-1 w-2 h-2 bg-sky-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                            <div className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-2 h-2 bg-sky-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                            <div className="absolute -bottom-1 -left-1 w-2 h-2 bg-sky-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                            {/* Bottom-right interactive handle for resize dragging! */}
                            <div 
                              className="absolute -bottom-1 -right-1 w-3 h-3 bg-sky-400 hover:bg-sky-300 rounded-full border border-slate-950 cursor-se-resize pointer-events-auto shadow-md"
                              onMouseDown={(e) => handleImageResizeMouseDown(e, layer)}
                              onTouchStart={(e) => handleImageResizeTouchStart(e, layer)}
                              title="Drag to resize image"
                            />
                          </>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  );
                })}

                {!hideAllTextLayers && textLayers.map((layer) => {
                  const isSelected = layer.id === selectedTextId;
                  const isEditing = layer.id === editingTextInPlace;
                  const textDisplaySize = Math.max(10, layer.fontSize * displayScale);
                  const rot = layer.rotation || 0;
                  const sx = layer.scaleX !== undefined ? layer.scaleX : 1;
                  const sy = layer.scaleY !== undefined ? layer.scaleY : 1;
                  return (
                    <div 
                      key={layer.id} 
                      style={{ 
                        position: 'absolute', 
                        left: `${(layer.x / width) * 100}%`, 
                        top: `${(layer.y / height) * 100}%`, 
                        transform: `translate(-50%, -50%) rotate(${rot}deg) scale(${sx}, ${sy}) skew(${layer.skewX || 0}deg, ${layer.skewY || 0}deg) perspective(${layer.perspective || 1000}px) rotateX(${layer.rotateX || 0}deg) rotateY(${layer.rotateY || 0}deg)`, 
                        transformOrigin: 'center center',
                        pointerEvents: 'auto' 
                      }} 
                      onMouseDown={(e) => handleTextMouseDown(e, layer)} 
                      onTouchStart={(e) => handleTextTouchStart(e, layer)} 
                      onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
                      onDoubleClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setEditingTextInPlace(layer.id); setInPlaceInputValue(layer.text); }}
                    >
                      {layer.isSpeechBubble ? (
                        isEditing ? (
                          <textarea
                            value={inPlaceInputValue}
                            autoFocus
                            onMouseDown={e => e.stopPropagation()}
                            onTouchStart={e => e.stopPropagation()}
                            onChange={e => {
                              setInPlaceInputValue(e.target.value);
                              setTextLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === layer.id ? { ...l, text: e.target.value } : l));
                            }}
                            onBlur={() => { setEditingTextInPlace(null); pushHistory(); }}
                            onKeyDown={e => {
                              if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
                                  e.preventDefault();
                                  setEditingTextInPlace(null);
                                  pushHistory();
                                }
                                if (e.key === 'Escape') setEditingTextInPlace(null);
                              }}
                              className="border-2 border-violet-500 p-2 rounded-xl shadow-2xl outline-none text-center resize-none"
                              style={{
                                fontFamily: layer.fontFamily,
                                fontSize: `${textDisplaySize}px`,
                                fontWeight: layer.isBold ? 'bold' : 'normal',
                                fontStyle: layer.isItalic ? 'italic' : 'normal',
                                color: layer.color || '#000000',
                                width: `${(layer.bubbleWidth || 250) * displayScale}px`,
                                height: `${(layer.bubbleHeight || 120) * displayScale}px`,
                                backgroundColor: layer.bubbleBgColor || (layer.bubbleType === 'thought' ? '#e8ecfb' : layer.bubbleType === 'narration' ? '#fffdf2' : '#ffffff')
                              }}
                            />
                          ) : (
                            <div 
                              className={cn(
                                "select-none relative group text-center cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing flex items-center justify-center p-4 shadow-lg",
                                layer.bubbleType === 'narration' ? 'rounded-none border-[3px] border-black overflow-hidden' :
                                layer.bubbleType === 'thought' ? 'rounded-[50%] border-[3px] border-black outline outline-[4px] outline-[#8b5cf6] -outline-offset-[1px]' :
                                'rounded-[24px] border-[3px] border-black',
                                isSelected ? "ring-2 ring-violet-500 ring-offset-2 ring-offset-slate-900" : ""
                              )} 
                              style={{ 
                                fontFamily: layer.fontFamily, 
                                fontSize: `${textDisplaySize}px`, 
                                fontWeight: layer.isBold ? 'bold' : 'normal', 
                                fontStyle: layer.isItalic ? 'italic' : 'normal',
                                color: layer.color || '#000000',
                                width: `${(layer.bubbleWidth || 250) * displayScale}px`,
                                height: `${(layer.bubbleHeight || 120) * displayScale}px`,
                                whiteSpace: 'normal',
                                wordBreak: 'break-word',
                                lineHeight: '1.25',
                                backgroundColor: layer.bubbleBgColor || (layer.bubbleType === 'thought' ? '#e8ecfb' : layer.bubbleType === 'narration' ? '#fffdf2' : '#ffffff')
                              }}
                            >
                              {/* Narration Left Orange Accent Bar */}
                              {layer.bubbleType === 'narration' && (
                                <div className="absolute left-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-2.5 bg-[#f97316]" />
                              )}

                              <span className="relative z-10 leading-snug pl-2">{layer.text || <span className="opacity-50 italic">Empty bubble</span>}</span>
                              
                              {/* Downward Tail pointer for speech bubble */}
                              {(!layer.bubbleType || layer.bubbleType === 'speech') && (() => {
                                const tailStyle = layer.bubbleTailLength || 'medium';
                                let tailH = 16;
                                if (tailStyle === 'short') tailH = 8;
                                else if (tailStyle === 'long') tailH = 28;
                                const bgColor = layer.bubbleBgColor || '#ffffff';
                                return (
                                  <div 
                                    className="absolute top-full -mt-[3px] pointer-events-none"
                                    style={{
                                      left: layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'left' ? '25%' : layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'right' ? '75%' : '50%',
                                      transform: 'translateX(-50%)',
                                      width: '24px',
                                      height: `${tailH}px`
                                    }}
                                  >
                                    <svg viewBox={`0 0 24 ${tailH}`} className="w-full h-full filter drop-shadow-[0_1px_0_#000]" preserveAspectRatio="none">
                                      <path d={`M 4 0 L 12 ${tailH - 2} L 20 0 Z`} fill={bgColor} stroke="black" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinejoin="round" />
                                      <rect x="5" y="-2" width="14" height="5" fill={bgColor} />
                                    </svg>
                                  </div>
                                );
                              })()}

                              {/* Thought bubble trail circles */}
                              {layer.bubbleType === 'thought' && (() => {
                                const tailOffset = layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'left' ? '25%' : layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'right' ? '75%' : '50%';
                                const bgColor = layer.bubbleBgColor || '#e8ecfb';
                                return (
                                  <>
                                    <div className="absolute rounded-full border border-black outline outline-2 outline-[#8b5cf6] -outline-offset-[1px] pointer-events-none shadow" style={{ left: `calc(${tailOffset} - 6px)`, top: '100%', marginTop: '6px', width: '12px', height: '12px', backgroundColor: bgColor }} />
                                    <div className="absolute rounded-full border border-black outline outline-2 outline-[#8b5cf6] -outline-offset-[1px] pointer-events-none shadow" style={{ left: `calc(${tailOffset} + ${layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'left' ? '-14px' : layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'right' ? '6px' : '-4px'})`, top: '100%', marginTop: '16px', width: '8px', height: '8px', backgroundColor: bgColor }} />
                                    <div className="absolute rounded-full border border-black outline outline-1 outline-[#8b5cf6] -outline-offset-[1px] pointer-events-none shadow" style={{ left: `calc(${tailOffset} + ${layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'left' ? '-20px' : layer.bubbleTailAlign === 'right' ? '12px' : '-2px'})`, top: '100%', marginTop: '24px', width: '5px', height: '5px', backgroundColor: bgColor }} />
                                  </>
                                );
                              })()}

                              {isSelected && (
                                <>
                                  <div className="absolute -top-1 -left-1 w-2 h-2 bg-violet-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                                  <div className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-2 h-2 bg-violet-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                                  <div className="absolute -bottom-1 -left-1 w-2 h-2 bg-violet-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                                  {/* Bottom-right interactive handle for resize dragging! */}
                                  <div 
                                    className="absolute -bottom-1 -right-1 w-3 h-3 bg-violet-400 hover:bg-violet-300 rounded-full border border-slate-950 cursor-se-resize pointer-events-auto shadow-md z-20"
                                    onMouseDown={(e) => handleBubbleResizeMouseDown(e, layer)}
                                    onTouchStart={(e) => handleBubbleResizeTouchStart(e, layer)}
                                    title="Drag to scale speech bubble size"
                                  />
                                </>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          )
                      ) : (
                        isEditing ? (
                          <input type="text" value={inPlaceInputValue} autoFocus onMouseDown={e => e.stopPropagation()} onTouchStart={e => e.stopPropagation()} onChange={e => { setInPlaceInputValue(e.target.value); setTextLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.id === layer.id ? { ...l, text: e.target.value } : l)); }} onBlur={() => { setEditingTextInPlace(null); pushHistory(); }} onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') { setEditingTextInPlace(null); pushHistory(); } if (e.key === 'Escape') setEditingTextInPlace(null); }} className="bg-slate-900/95 border-2 border-violet-500 text-white px-2 py-1 rounded shadow-2xl outline-none" style={{ fontFamily: layer.fontFamily, fontSize: `${textDisplaySize}px`, fontWeight: layer.isBold ? 'bold' : 'normal', fontStyle: layer.isItalic ? 'italic' : 'normal', color: layer.color }} />
                        ) : (
                          <div className={cn("px-2.5 py-1.5 rounded transition-all select-none relative whitespace-nowrap group text-center cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing", isSelected ? "ring-2 ring-violet-500/80 bg-slate-950/70 border border-violet-500" : "hover:bg-white/5 border border-transparent")} style={{ fontFamily: layer.fontFamily, fontSize: `${textDisplaySize}px`, fontWeight: layer.isBold ? 'bold' : 'normal', fontStyle: layer.isItalic ? 'italic' : 'normal', color: layer.color, textShadow: layer.hasOutline ? `-2px -2px 0 #000, 2px -2px 0 #000, -2px 2px 0 #000, 2px 2px 0 #000, -1px -1px 0 #000, 1px -1px 0 #000, -1px 1px 0 #000, 1px 1px 0 #000` : 'none' }}>
                            {layer.text || <span className="opacity-50 italic">Empty text block</span>}
                            {isSelected && (
                              <>
                                <div className="absolute -top-1 -left-1 w-2 h-2 bg-violet-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                                <div className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-2 h-2 bg-violet-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                                <div className="absolute -bottom-1 -left-1 w-2 h-2 bg-violet-400 rounded-full border border-slate-950 pointer-events-none" />
                                {/* Bottom-right interactive handle for resize dragging! */}
                                <div 
                                  className="absolute -bottom-1 -right-1 w-3 h-3 bg-violet-400 hover:bg-violet-300 rounded-full border border-slate-950 cursor-se-resize pointer-events-auto shadow-md"
                                  onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeMouseDown(e, layer)}
                                  onTouchStart={(e) => handleResizeTouchStart(e, layer)}
                                  title="Drag to resize text font size"
                                />
                              </>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        )
                      )}
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>

            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {showAssetLibrary && (
          <div className="w-72 bg-[#121217] border-l border-neutral-800 flex flex-col shrink-0 z-20 overflow-hidden text-neutral-200">
            {/* Header */}
            <div className="p-3 border-b border-neutral-800 flex items-center justify-between bg-neutral-900/40">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                <FolderHeart className="w-4 h-4 text-pink-400" />
                <span className="text-xs font-black uppercase tracking-wider text-neutral-200">Asset Library</span>
              </div>
              <button 
                onClick={() => setShowAssetLibrary(false)}
                className="p-1 hover:bg-neutral-800 text-neutral-400 hover:text-white rounded transition-colors cursor-pointer"
              >
                <X className="w-4 h-4" />
              </button>
            </div>

            {/* Upload to Asset Library Button */}
            <div className="p-3 border-b border-neutral-800 flex flex-col gap-2">
              <button
                onClick={() => assetFileInputRef.current?.click()}
                className="w-full flex items-center justify-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white rounded text-xs font-bold transition-all cursor-pointer shadow"
              >
                <Upload className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                <span>Upload to Library</span>
              </button>
              <input
                type="file"
                ref={assetFileInputRef}
                onChange={handleLibraryAssetUpload}
                accept="image/*"
                className="hidden"
              />
              <p className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 text-center">Persists image sticker overlays to your Firestore DB library.</p>
            </div>

            {/* Filter and Search */}
            <div className="p-3 border-b border-neutral-800 flex flex-col gap-2">
              <div className="relative">
                <Search className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-neutral-500 absolute left-2 top-2" />
                <input
                  type="text"
                  placeholder="Search assets..."
                  value={searchQuery}
                  onChange={e => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                  className="w-full bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-800 rounded px-2 py-1 pl-7 text-[10px] text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-indigo-500"
                />
              </div>

              {/* Categories */}
              <div className="flex gap-1 overflow-x-auto pb-1 scrollbar-none">
                {['all', 'sticker', 'character', 'prop', 'bg'].map(cat => (
                  <button
                    key={cat}
                    onClick={() => setSelectedCategory(cat)}
                    className={cn(
                      "px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[9px] font-extrabold uppercase shrink-0 transition-colors cursor-pointer",
                      selectedCategory === cat 
                        ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white" 
                        : "bg-neutral-800 text-neutral-400 hover:bg-neutral-700 hover:text-white"
                    )}
                  >
                    {cat}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Asset List Grid */}
            <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-3 gap-2.5 grid grid-cols-2 auto-rows-max bg-neutral-950/20">
              {filteredAssets.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="col-span-2 py-8 text-center text-neutral-500 text-[11px] flex flex-col items-center gap-2">
                  <span>No assets found.</span>
                  {collageAssets.length === 0 && (
                    <button
                      onClick={handleSeedDefaultAssets}
                      className="px-2 py-1 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 hover:text-white border border-neutral-700 rounded text-[9px] font-bold flex items-center gap-1 transition-all cursor-pointer animate-pulse"
                    >
                      <Sparkles className="w-3 h-3 text-amber-400" />
                      <span>Seed Default Assets</span>
                    </button>
                  )}
                </div>
              ) : (
                filteredAssets.map(asset => (
                  <div
                    key={asset.id}
                    onClick={() => handleLibraryAssetSelect(asset.imageUrl, asset.name)}
                    className="group relative bg-neutral-900/60 hover:bg-neutral-800/80 border border-neutral-800/80 hover:border-neutral-700 rounded-lg p-2 flex flex-col items-center justify-center cursor-pointer transition-all aspect-square text-center"
                    title={`Click to overlay "${asset.name}"`}
                  >
                    <img
                      src={asset.imageUrl}
                      alt={asset.name}
                      referrerPolicy="no-referrer"
                      className="max-h-16 max-w-full object-contain mb-1 transition-transform group-hover:scale-105"
                    />
                    <span className="text-[9px] text-neutral-400 font-bold truncate w-full px-1">{asset.name}</span>
                    <button
                      onClick={(e) => handleLibraryAssetDelete(asset.id, e)}
                      className="absolute top-1 right-1 p-1 bg-red-600/20 hover:bg-red-600 text-red-400 hover:text-white rounded opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-150 cursor-pointer"
                      title="Delete asset from database"
                    >
                      <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" />
                    </button>
                  </div>
                ))
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

=== FILE: src/components/ScreenplayWriter.tsx ===
import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { 
  FileText, Sparkles, RefreshCw, HelpCircle, Plus, Trash2, Link, 
  CheckCircle2, AlertCircle, BookOpen, Edit3, ArrowRightLeft, Camera, Layers,
  Maximize2, Minimize2, MessageSquare, Eye, EyeOff
} from 'lucide-react';
import { Slide } from '../types';

interface ScreenplayWriterProps {
  slides: Slide[];
  onUpdateSlides: (newSlides: Slide[]) => void;
  folderName: string;
  activeSlideId: string | null;
  onSelectSlideId: (id: string | null) => void;
  isFullScreen?: boolean;
  onToggleFullScreen?: () => void;
  onOpenFrameEditorWithTextLayers?: (index: number, initialTextLayers: any[]) => void;
}

export interface ScriptParagraph {
  type: 'scene-heading' | 'action' | 'character' | 'dialogue' | 'parenthetical' | 'transition' | 'frame-tag' | 'empty';
  text: string;
  sceneNo?: number;
  shotNo?: number;
}

// Client-side parser for Screenplay (Fountain-light format)
export function parseSubjects(text: string) {
  const regex = /\[(\d+)\]([^\n\[]+)/g;
  const subjects: { id: string; text: string }[] = [];
  let match;
  while ((match = regex.exec(text)) !== null) {
    let subjectText = match[2].trim();
    subjectText = subjectText.replace(/^[\,\.\s]+|[\,\.\s]+$/g, '');
    subjects.push({ id: match[1], text: subjectText });
  }
  return subjects;
}

export function parseScreenplay(text: string): ScriptParagraph[] {
  const lines = text.split('\n');
  const paragraphs: ScriptParagraph[] = [];
  
  for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    const line = lines[i].trim();
    if (!line) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'empty', text: '' });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for frame tags: [Frame: Scene X, Shot Y] or [Frame: Sc X, Sh Y]
    const frameMatch = line.match(/\[Frame:\s*(?:Scene|Sc)?\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*(?:Shot|Sh)?\s*(\d+)\]/i);
    if (frameMatch) {
      paragraphs.push({
        type: 'frame-tag',
        text: line,
        sceneNo: parseInt(frameMatch[1], 10),
        shotNo: parseInt(frameMatch[2], 10)
      });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for scene heading
    if (line.match(/^(?:INT|EXT|INT\/EXT|EXT\/INT|I\/E)\.?\s+/i)) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'scene-heading', text: line.toUpperCase() });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for transitions
    if (line.match(/^(?:FADE IN|FADE OUT|CUT TO|DISSOLVE TO|FADE TO BLACK|FADE TO)\s*:/i) || line.toUpperCase().endsWith('TO:')) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'transition', text: line.toUpperCase() });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for Character / Dialogue sequence
    const isAllCaps = line === line.toUpperCase() && /[A-Z]/.test(line);
    if (isAllCaps) {
      // Look ahead to see if there is dialogue
      let nextLine = '';
      for (let j = i + 1; j < lines.length; j++) {
        const testLine = lines[j].trim();
        if (testLine) {
          nextLine = testLine;
          break;
        }
      }
      
      if (nextLine) {
        paragraphs.push({ type: 'character', text: line });
        continue;
      }
    }
    
    // Check for parenthetical
    if (line.startsWith('(') && line.endsWith(')')) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'parenthetical', text: line });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Default is dialogue if previous was character or parenthetical
    const prevParagraph = paragraphs[paragraphs.length - 1];
    if (prevParagraph && (prevParagraph.type === 'character' || prevParagraph.type === 'parenthetical' || (prevParagraph.type === 'empty' && paragraphs[paragraphs.length - 2] && (paragraphs[paragraphs.length - 2].type === 'character' || paragraphs[paragraphs.length - 2].type === 'parenthetical')))) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'dialogue', text: line });
    } else {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'action', text: line });
    }
  }
  
  return paragraphs;
}

export default function ScreenplayWriter({
  slides,
  onUpdateSlides,
  folderName,
  activeSlideId,
  onSelectSlideId,
  isFullScreen = false,
  onToggleFullScreen,
  onOpenFrameEditorWithTextLayers
}: ScreenplayWriterProps) {
  const [scriptText, setScriptText] = useState<string>(() => {
    return localStorage.getItem('storyboard_screenplay_text') || '';
  });
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<'edit' | 'preview'>('edit');
  const [isGenerating, setIsGenerating] = useState(false);
  const [isExtracting, setIsExtracting] = useState(false);
  const [errorMsg, setErrorMsg] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [infoMsg, setInfoMsg] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showHelp, setShowHelp] = useState(false);
  const [highlightedFrameKey, setHighlightedFrameKey] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [isAIEnabled, setIsAIEnabled] = useState(false);
  const [complexity, setComplexity] = useState<'quick' | 'objects' | 'full'>('quick');
  const [isDescribingFrame, setIsDescribingFrame] = useState(false);
  const textareaRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null);

  const [showActiveFrame, setShowActiveFrame] = useState<boolean>(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('storyboard_show_active_frame');
    return saved !== null ? saved === 'true' : true;
  });
  const [showStoryDeckLink, setShowStoryDeckLink] = useState<boolean>(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('storyboard_show_story_deck_link');
    return saved !== null ? saved === 'true' : true;
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('storyboard_show_active_frame', String(showActiveFrame));
  }, [showActiveFrame]);

  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('storyboard_show_story_deck_link', String(showStoryDeckLink));
  }, [showStoryDeckLink]);

  // Save changes to local storage
  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('storyboard_screenplay_text', scriptText);
  }, [scriptText]);

  // Sync highlighting from selected Storyboard frame
  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeSlideId) {
      const slide = slides.find(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
      if (slide) {
        const key = `${slide.sceneNo}-${slide.shotNo}`;
        setHighlightedFrameKey(key);
        // Automatically set info message
        setInfoMsg(`Correlated to Scene ${slide.sceneNo}, Shot ${slide.shotNo}`);
        setTimeout(() => setInfoMsg(null), 3000);
      }
    } else {
      setHighlightedFrameKey(null);
    }
  }, [activeSlideId, slides]);

  // AI: Generate Screenplay based on current slides
  const handleAIGenerateScript = async () => {
    if (slides.length === 0) {
      setErrorMsg('Add at least one storyboard slide to generate a screenplay.');
      return;
    }
    
    setIsGenerating(true);
    setErrorMsg(null);
    setInfoMsg(null);

    try {
      const simplifiedSlides = slides.map(s => ({
        sceneNo: s.sceneNo,
        shotNo: s.shotNo,
        shotType: s.shotType || 'MS',
        action: s.action || '',
        dialogue: s.dialogue || '',
        notes: s.notes || '',
        duration: s.duration || 3000
      }));

      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/generate-script', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ slides: simplifiedSlides, folderName })
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to generate script');
      }

      if (data.script) {
        setScriptText(data.script);
        setInfoMsg('AI Screenplay Generated successfully!');
        setActiveTab('preview');
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error(err);
      setErrorMsg(err.message || 'AI generation failed. Check your API key configuration.');
    } finally {
      setIsGenerating(false);
    }
  };

  // AI: Describe active frame
  
  const handleApplyBubbles = async () => {
    const activeSlide = slides.find(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
    if (!activeSlide || !activeSlide.captions || activeSlide.captions.length === 0) return;

    const img = new Image();
    img.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
    img.src = activeSlide.imageUrl;
    
    await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      img.onload = resolve;
      img.onerror = reject;
    });

    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    canvas.width = img.width;
    canvas.height = img.height;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    if (!ctx) return;

    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);

    activeSlide.captions.forEach((caption, index) => {
      const text = caption.text;
      ctx.font = "bold 24px sans-serif";
      
      const maxWidth = canvas.width * 0.4;
      const words = text.split(' ');
      let line = '';
      const lines = [];
      for (let n = 0; n < words.length; n++) {
        const testLine = line + words[n] + ' ';
        const metrics = ctx.measureText(testLine);
        if (metrics.width > maxWidth && n > 0) {
          lines.push(line);
          line = words[n] + ' ';
        } else {
          line = testLine;
        }
      }
      lines.push(line);
      
      const lineHeight = 30;
      const textHeight = lines.length * lineHeight;
      const padding = 20;
      const bubbleWidth = Math.max(...lines.map(l => ctx.measureText(l).width)) + padding * 2;
      const bubbleHeight = textHeight + padding * 2;
      
      const x = index % 2 === 0 ? canvas.width * 0.05 : canvas.width * 0.95 - bubbleWidth;
      const y = canvas.height * 0.05 + Math.floor(index / 2) * (bubbleHeight + 50);

      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
      ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
      ctx.lineWidth = 4;
      
      ctx.beginPath();
      if (typeof ctx.roundRect === 'function') {
        ctx.roundRect(x, y, bubbleWidth, bubbleHeight, 15);
      } else {
        ctx.rect(x, y, bubbleWidth, bubbleHeight);
      }
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.stroke();

      ctx.beginPath();
      if (index % 2 === 0) {
        ctx.moveTo(x + bubbleWidth * 0.8, y + bubbleHeight);
        ctx.lineTo(x + bubbleWidth * 0.9, y + bubbleHeight + 40);
        ctx.lineTo(x + bubbleWidth * 0.6, y + bubbleHeight);
      } else {
        ctx.moveTo(x + bubbleWidth * 0.2, y + bubbleHeight);
        ctx.lineTo(x + bubbleWidth * 0.1, y + bubbleHeight + 40);
        ctx.lineTo(x + bubbleWidth * 0.4, y + bubbleHeight);
      }
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.stroke();

      ctx.fillStyle = '#000000';
      lines.forEach((l, i) => {
        ctx.fillText(l.trim(), x + padding, y + padding + 24 + i * lineHeight);
      });
    });

    const newImageUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.9);
    
    const newSlide = {
      ...activeSlide,
      id: "slide-" + Date.now(),
      shotNo: activeSlide.shotNo + 1,
      imageUrl: newImageUrl,
      action: activeSlide.action + " (Bubbles Applied)",
      captions: [],
    };
    
    const newSlides = [...slides];
    const idx = newSlides.findIndex(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
    newSlides.splice(idx + 1, 0, newSlide);
    onUpdateSlides(newSlides);
    onSelectSlideId(newSlide.id);
  };

  const handleDescribeFrame = async (slide: Slide) => {
    setIsDescribingFrame(true);
    setErrorMsg(null);
    setInfoMsg(null);
    try {
      const [header, base64Data] = slide.imageUrl.split(",");
      const mimeType = header.split(":")[1].split(";")[0];
      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/describe-frame', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ base64Data, mimeType })
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to describe frame');
      
      const description = data.description;
      const subjects = parseSubjects(description);
      
      const newSlides = [...slides];
      const slideIndex = newSlides.findIndex(s => s.id === slide.id);
      if (slideIndex !== -1) {
        newSlides[slideIndex] = { ...newSlides[slideIndex], description, subjects };
        onUpdateSlides(newSlides);
      }
      setInfoMsg('Frame fully described & subjects enumerated!');
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error(err);
      setErrorMsg(err.message || 'Failed to describe frame');
    } finally {
      setIsDescribingFrame(false);
    }
  };

  // AI: Extract slides from current script text
  const handleAIExtractFrames = async () => {
    if (!scriptText.trim()) {
      setErrorMsg('Please write or generate a screenplay script first.');
      return;
    }

    setIsExtracting(true);
    setErrorMsg(null);
    setInfoMsg(null);

    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/extract-frames', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ scriptText, complexity })
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to extract frames');
      }

      if (data.frames && Array.isArray(data.frames)) {
        // Map the extracted JSON blocks to slides
        const newSlides: Slide[] = data.frames.map((f: any, idx: number) => ({
          id: `extracted-${Date.now()}-${idx}`,
          sceneNo: Number(f.sceneNo) || 1,
          shotNo: Number(f.shotNo) || (idx + 1),
          shotType: f.shotType || 'MS',
          duration: Number(f.duration) || 3000,
          action: f.action || '',
          dialogue: f.dialogue || '',
          notes: f.notes || '',
          imageUrl: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1536440136628-849c177e76a1?w=800&auto=format&fit=crop&q=60', // placeholder cinematic image
          imageScale: 1,
          fitMode: 'cover'
        }));

        if (confirm(`AI extracted ${newSlides.length} visual shots from the screenplay. Do you want to append them to your Storyboard deck?`)) {
          const merged = [...slides, ...newSlides];
          onUpdateSlides(merged);
          setInfoMsg(`Successfully appended ${newSlides.length} cinematic frames!`);
        }
      } else {
        throw new Error('AI response was invalid or contained no frames.');
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error(err);
      setErrorMsg(err.message || 'AI extraction failed. Check your API key.');
    } finally {
      setIsExtracting(false);
    }
  };

  // Link slide to current cursor position inside script
  const handleInsertFrameTag = (slide: Slide) => {
    if (!textareaRef.current) return;
    
    const textarea = textareaRef.current;
    const start = textarea.selectionStart;
    const end = textarea.selectionEnd;
    const text = textarea.value;
    
    const tag = `\n[Frame: Scene ${slide.sceneNo}, Shot ${slide.shotNo}]\n`;
    const newText = text.substring(0, start) + tag + text.substring(end);
    
    setScriptText(newText);
    
    // Reset cursor
    setTimeout(() => {
      textarea.focus();
      textarea.setSelectionRange(start + tag.length, start + tag.length);
    }, 100);
    
    setInfoMsg(`Inserted tag [Scene ${slide.sceneNo}, Shot ${slide.shotNo}]`);
    setTimeout(() => setInfoMsg(null), 3000);
  };

  // Sync narrative action/dialogues from Screenplay back to Storyboard slides!
  const handleSyncToStoryboard = () => {
    const paragraphs = parseScreenplay(scriptText);
    let updatedCount = 0;
    const newSlides = [...slides];

    for (let i = 0; i < paragraphs.length; i++) {
      const p = paragraphs[i];
      if (p.type === 'frame-tag' && p.sceneNo !== undefined && p.shotNo !== undefined) {
        // Find matching slide in storyboard
        const slideIndex = newSlides.findIndex(s => s.sceneNo === p.sceneNo && s.shotNo === p.shotNo);
        if (slideIndex !== -1) {
          // Gather succeeding action & dialogue paragraphs until the next frame tag or scene heading
          let accumulatedAction = '';
          let accumulatedDialogue = '';
          
          for (let j = i + 1; j < paragraphs.length; j++) {
            const nextP = paragraphs[j];
            if (nextP.type === 'frame-tag' || nextP.type === 'scene-heading') {
              break;
            }
            if (nextP.type === 'action' && nextP.text) {
              accumulatedAction += (accumulatedAction ? ' ' : '') + nextP.text;
            }
            if (nextP.type === 'dialogue' && nextP.text) {
              accumulatedDialogue += (accumulatedDialogue ? ' ' : '') + nextP.text;
            }
          }

          // Update slide if we found matching text
          let changed = false;
          if (accumulatedAction && newSlides[slideIndex].action !== accumulatedAction) {
            newSlides[slideIndex].action = accumulatedAction;
            changed = true;
          }
          if (accumulatedDialogue && newSlides[slideIndex].dialogue !== accumulatedDialogue) {
            newSlides[slideIndex].dialogue = accumulatedDialogue;
            changed = true;
          }
          
          if (changed) {
            updatedCount++;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (updatedCount > 0) {
      onUpdateSlides(newSlides);
      setInfoMsg(`Synced & updated visual cues in ${updatedCount} matching storyboard frames!`);
    } else {
      setInfoMsg('No updates found. Verify you have matching [Frame: Scene X, Shot Y] tags in your script.');
    }
    setTimeout(() => setInfoMsg(null), 5000);
  };

  // Interactive frame link click
  const handleFrameTagClick = (sceneNo: number, shotNo: number) => {
    const match = slides.find(s => s.sceneNo === sceneNo && s.shotNo === shotNo);
    if (match) {
      onSelectSlideId(match.id);
      setHighlightedFrameKey(`${sceneNo}-${shotNo}`);
      setInfoMsg(`Jumping to Storyboard Scene ${sceneNo}, Shot ${shotNo}`);
      setTimeout(() => setInfoMsg(null), 3000);
    } else {
      setErrorMsg(`No storyboard slide matches Scene ${sceneNo}, Shot ${shotNo}`);
      setTimeout(() => setErrorMsg(null), 4000);
    }
  };

  const parsedParagraphs = parseScreenplay(scriptText);

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full bg-[#0E0E12] bg-theme-panel border-l border-neutral-800 border-theme text-xs">
      {/* Sidebar Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-neutral-850 border-theme bg-neutral-900/40 bg-theme-badge shrink-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <FileText className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" />
          <h3 className="font-black text-white text-sm">Screenplay Suite</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
          {onToggleFullScreen && (
            <button
              onClick={onToggleFullScreen}
              className="p-1 text-neutral-400 hover:text-white hover:bg-neutral-800 rounded transition-colors mr-1 cursor-pointer"
              title={isFullScreen ? "Exit Fullscreen" : "Fullscreen Screenplay Mode"}
            >
              {isFullScreen ? <Minimize2 className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" /> : <Maximize2 className="w-4 h-4" />}
            </button>
          )}
          <button 
            onClick={() => setShowHelp(!showHelp)}
            className="p-1 text-neutral-400 hover:text-white hover:bg-neutral-800 rounded transition-colors cursor-pointer"
            title="Screenplay formatting help"
          >
            <HelpCircle className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Screenplay Formatting Guide banner */}
      {showHelp && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-indigo-950/20 border-b border-indigo-500/20 text-neutral-300 animate-fade-in shrink-0">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1.5">
            <span className="font-bold text-indigo-300 uppercase text-[9px] tracking-wider">Typewriter Guide</span>
            <button onClick={() => setShowHelp(false)} className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 hover:text-white font-black">Close</button>
          </div>
          <ul className="space-y-1 text-[11px] list-disc list-inside text-neutral-400">
            <li><strong className="text-white font-mono text-[10px]">INT. / EXT. COFFEE SHOP</strong> starts a Scene heading.</li>
            <li><strong className="text-white font-mono text-[10px]">CHARACTER (ALL CAPS)</strong> on its own line signals character.</li>
            <li>Indented dialogues and italicized parentheticals auto-format.</li>
            <li>Use <strong className="text-indigo-400 font-mono text-[10px]">[Frame: Scene 1, Shot 2]</strong> to link a visual slide.</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Alert Messaging area */}
      {errorMsg && (
        <div className="p-2 bg-rose-950/20 border-b border-rose-500/20 text-rose-400 text-[11px] flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0 animate-fade-in">
          <AlertCircle className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0" />
          <span className="truncate flex-1">{errorMsg}</span>
          <button onClick={() => setErrorMsg(null)} className="font-black text-[9px] px-1 hover:text-white">✕</button>
        </div>
      )}

      {infoMsg && (
        <div className="p-2 bg-emerald-950/20 border-b border-emerald-500/20 text-emerald-400 text-[11px] flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0 animate-fade-in">
          <CheckCircle2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 text-emerald-400" />
          <span className="truncate flex-1">{infoMsg}</span>
          <button onClick={() => setInfoMsg(null)} className="font-black text-[9px] px-1 hover:text-white">✕</button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Toolbar Options */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 bg-neutral-900/60 border-b border-neutral-850 shrink-0">
        {/* Toggle Mode */}
        <div className="flex bg-neutral-950 p-0.5 rounded-lg border border-neutral-850">
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('edit')}
            className={`px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md text-[10px] font-black uppercase transition-all flex items-center gap-1 ${
              activeTab === 'edit' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow-md' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Edit3 className="w-3 h-3" /> Typewriter
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('preview')}
            className={`px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md text-[10px] font-black uppercase transition-all flex items-center gap-1 ${
              activeTab === 'preview' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow-md' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <BookOpen className="w-3 h-3" /> Cinematic Preview
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Action button bar */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
          {/* Show/Hide Toggles */}
          <button
            onClick={() => setShowActiveFrame(!showActiveFrame)}
            className={`px-2 py-1 rounded text-[9px] font-bold uppercase transition-all border flex items-center gap-1 cursor-pointer shrink-0 ${
              showActiveFrame 
                ? 'bg-indigo-600/10 border-indigo-500/30 text-indigo-300' 
                : 'bg-neutral-800/40 border-neutral-700/20 text-neutral-500 hover:text-neutral-300'
            }`}
            title="Toggle Active Frame Panel Visibility"
          >
            {showActiveFrame ? <Eye className="w-3 h-3 text-indigo-400" /> : <EyeOff className="w-3 h-3 text-neutral-500" />}
            <span>Active Frame</span>
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={() => setShowStoryDeckLink(!showStoryDeckLink)}
            className={`px-2 py-1 rounded text-[9px] font-bold uppercase transition-all border flex items-center gap-1 cursor-pointer shrink-0 ${
              showStoryDeckLink 
                ? 'bg-indigo-600/10 border-indigo-500/30 text-indigo-300' 
                : 'bg-neutral-800/40 border-neutral-700/20 text-neutral-500 hover:text-neutral-300'
            }`}
            title="Toggle Story Deck Link Panel Visibility"
          >
            {showStoryDeckLink ? <Eye className="w-3 h-3 text-indigo-400" /> : <EyeOff className="w-3 h-3 text-neutral-500" />}
            <span>Deck Link</span>
          </button>

          <div className="h-4 w-px bg-neutral-800" />

          <button
            onClick={handleSyncToStoryboard}
            disabled={slides.length === 0 || !scriptText}
            className="flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 bg-indigo-950/40 hover:bg-indigo-950/60 text-indigo-400 border border-indigo-500/20 hover:border-indigo-500/40 rounded text-[10px] font-bold transition-all disabled:opacity-40 cursor-pointer shrink-0"
            title="Parse screenplay changes and push action/dialogue back to matching storyboard frames"
          >
            <ArrowRightLeft className="w-3 h-3 text-indigo-400" /> Sync to Board
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Primary Workstation Pane */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden relative flex flex-col">
        {activeTab === 'edit' ? (
          <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
            <textarea
              ref={textareaRef}
              value={scriptText}
              onChange={(e) => setScriptText(e.target.value)}
              placeholder={`Write your cinematic screenplay here...\n\nExample:\n\nFADE IN:\n\nINT. COFFEE SHOP - DAY\n\n[Frame: Scene 1, Shot 1]\nHERO sits nervously holding a warm mug. The steam rises gently.\n\nHERO\nIs there anyone else coming?`}
              className="flex-1 w-full bg-[#09090D] bg-theme-app text-neutral-200 text-theme-primary p-4 font-mono text-xs leading-relaxed outline-none border-none resize-none overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar"
              style={{ tabSize: 4 }}
            />
          </div>
        ) : (
          /* CINEMATIC PREVIEW TAB (Fountain styled screenplay) */
          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 bg-[#09090D] bg-theme-app text-neutral-300 text-theme-primary font-mono leading-loose custom-scrollbar selection:bg-indigo-600/30">
            {parsedParagraphs.length === 0 || (parsedParagraphs.length === 1 && parsedParagraphs[0].type === 'empty') ? (
              <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center p-4 text-neutral-500 text-theme-muted">
                <FileText className="w-8 h-8 text-neutral-600 mb-2" />
                <p className="text-xs">Your screenplay screenplay is empty.</p>
                <p className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 mt-1">Switch to typewriter mode to draft your cinematic project.</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="max-w-md mx-auto space-y-1 pb-16 text-[11.5px]">
                {parsedParagraphs.map((p, idx) => {
                  const isHighlighted = p.sceneNo !== undefined && p.shotNo !== undefined && highlightedFrameKey === `${p.sceneNo}-${p.shotNo}`;
                  
                  if (p.type === 'empty') {
                    return <div key={idx} className="h-4" />;
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'frame-tag') {
                    return (
                      <div 
                        key={idx} 
                        onClick={() => handleFrameTagClick(p.sceneNo!, p.shotNo!)}
                        className={`my-3 p-2 rounded-lg border flex items-center justify-between cursor-pointer transition-all ${
                          isHighlighted 
                            ? 'bg-indigo-600/15 border-indigo-500/55 text-indigo-400 shadow-md ring-1 ring-indigo-500/20' 
                            : 'bg-neutral-900/60 bg-theme-panel border-neutral-800 border-theme text-neutral-300 hover:border-indigo-500/50 hover:bg-neutral-900 text-theme-primary'
                        }`}
                      >
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 font-sans font-extrabold text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider">
                          <Camera className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 ${isHighlighted ? 'text-indigo-400' : 'text-neutral-500 text-theme-muted'}`} />
                          <span>Frame Visual: Scene {p.sceneNo}, Shot {p.shotNo}</span>
                        </div>
                        <span className="font-sans font-black text-[9px] uppercase tracking-widest px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-neutral-800/80 rounded hover:bg-indigo-600 hover:text-white transition-colors">Select Frame</span>
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'scene-heading') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="font-bold uppercase tracking-wider text-white pt-4 pb-1 border-b border-neutral-800 border-theme mb-2">
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'character') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="text-center font-bold text-indigo-400 uppercase pt-2" style={{ width: '80%', margin: '0 auto' }}>
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'parenthetical') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="text-center italic text-neutral-400 text-theme-muted" style={{ width: '60%', margin: '0 auto' }}>
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'dialogue') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="text-neutral-200 text-theme-primary" style={{ width: '70%', margin: '0 auto', textAlign: 'left', textIndent: '0' }}>
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'transition') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="text-right font-bold uppercase py-2 text-neutral-400 text-theme-muted">
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  // Default Action
                  return (
                    <div key={idx} className="text-neutral-300 text-theme-primary leading-relaxed text-justify">
                      {p.text}
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      
      {/* Active Slide Subject & Speech Editor */}
      {activeSlideId && showActiveFrame && (
        <div className="p-3 border-t border-neutral-850 bg-neutral-900/60 shrink-0 flex flex-col gap-2 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">
          {(() => {
            const activeSlide = slides.find(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
            if (!activeSlide) return null;
            return (
              <>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                  <span className="text-[10px] font-black text-indigo-400 uppercase tracking-widest">Active Frame (Scene {activeSlide.sceneNo}, Shot {activeSlide.shotNo})</span>
                  <button 
                    onClick={() => handleDescribeFrame(activeSlide)}
                    disabled={isDescribingFrame}
                    className="px-2 py-1 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-50 text-white rounded text-[9px] uppercase font-bold flex items-center gap-1"
                  >
                    {isDescribingFrame ? <RefreshCw className="w-3 h-3 animate-spin" /> : <Sparkles className="w-3 h-3" />}
                    Describe & Enumerate Objects
                  </button>
                </div>
                
                {activeSlide.description && (
                  <div className="text-[10px] text-neutral-400 bg-black/40 p-2 rounded border border-neutral-800">
                    <p className="font-bold text-neutral-300 mb-1">Scene Description:</p>
                    <p className="leading-relaxed">{activeSlide.description}</p>
                  </div>
                )}
                
                {activeSlide.subjects && activeSlide.subjects.length > 0 && (
                  <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-1">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                      <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-neutral-300 uppercase tracking-wider">Identified Subjects / Objects</span>
                      <button
                        onClick={() => {
                          const newSlides = [...slides];
                          const idx = newSlides.findIndex(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
                          const currentSubjects = newSlides[idx].subjects || [];
                          const maxId = currentSubjects.length > 0 ? Math.max(...currentSubjects.map(s => parseInt(s.id))) : 0;
                          newSlides[idx].subjects = [...currentSubjects, { id: String(maxId + 1), text: "New Subject" }];
                          onUpdateSlides(newSlides);
                        }}
                        className="text-[9px] text-indigo-400 hover:text-indigo-300 flex items-center gap-1"
                      >
                        <Plus className="w-3 h-3" /> Add
                      </button>
                    </div>
                    {activeSlide.subjects.map(sub => (
                      <div key={sub.id} className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 bg-black/20 p-2 rounded border border-neutral-800/60">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <span className="text-[10px] font-mono bg-neutral-800 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-neutral-400">[{sub.id}]</span>
                          <input 
                            type="text"
                            value={sub.text}
                            onChange={(e) => {
                              const newSlides = [...slides];
                              const idx = newSlides.findIndex(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
                              const newSubjects = [...(newSlides[idx].subjects || [])];
                              const subIdx = newSubjects.findIndex(s => s.id === sub.id);
                              if (subIdx !== -1) {
                                newSubjects[subIdx].text = e.target.value;
                                newSlides[idx].subjects = newSubjects;
                                onUpdateSlides(newSlides);
                              }
                            }}
                            className="flex-1 bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-800 rounded px-2 py-1 text-[10px] text-neutral-300 focus:border-indigo-500 outline-none"
                          />
                          <button
                            onClick={() => {
                              const newSlides = [...slides];
                              const idx = newSlides.findIndex(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
                              newSlides[idx].subjects = (newSlides[idx].subjects || []).filter(s => s.id !== sub.id);
                              // Also remove any captions for this subject
                              newSlides[idx].captions = (newSlides[idx].captions || []).filter(c => c.speaker !== `Subject [${sub.id}]`);
                              onUpdateSlides(newSlides);
                            }}
                            className="p-1 text-neutral-500 hover:text-red-400"
                          >
                            <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" />
                          </button>
                        </div>
                        
                        {/* Speech Caption Assignment */}
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 ml-7">
                           <MessageSquare className="w-3 h-3 text-emerald-500" />
                           <input
                             type="text"
                             placeholder="Assign speech bubble..."
                             value={activeSlide.captions?.find(c => c.speaker === `Subject [${sub.id}]`)?.text || ''}
                             onChange={(e) => {
                               const newSlides = [...slides];
                               const idx = newSlides.findIndex(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
                               let newCaptions = [...(newSlides[idx].captions || [])];
                               const capIdx = newCaptions.findIndex(c => c.speaker === `Subject [${sub.id}]`);
                               if (e.target.value) {
                                 if (capIdx !== -1) {
                                   newCaptions[capIdx].text = e.target.value;
                                 } else {
                                   newCaptions.push({ speaker: `Subject [${sub.id}]`, text: e.target.value });
                                 }
                               } else {
                                 if (capIdx !== -1) newCaptions.splice(capIdx, 1);
                               }
                               newSlides[idx].captions = newCaptions;
                               onUpdateSlides(newSlides);
                             }}
                             className="flex-1 bg-neutral-900/50 border border-neutral-800/50 rounded px-2 py-1 text-[10px] text-emerald-400 placeholder:text-neutral-600 focus:border-emerald-500 outline-none"
                           />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}

                  {activeSlide.captions && activeSlide.captions.length > 0 && (
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-2">
                      {onOpenFrameEditorWithTextLayers && (
                        <button
                          onClick={() => {
                            const globalIndex = slides.findIndex(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
                            if (globalIndex === -1) return;
                            
                            const canvasW = 1280;
                            const canvasH = 720;
                            const layers = activeSlide.captions.map((caption, index) => {
                              const text = caption.text;
                              const bubbleW = Math.min(350, Math.max(200, text.length * 8 + 60));
                              const bubbleH = Math.min(220, Math.max(100, Math.ceil(text.length / 25) * 28 + 40));
                              
                              const x = index % 2 === 0 ? canvasW * 0.25 : canvasW * 0.75;
                              const y = canvasH * 0.25 + Math.floor(index / 2) * (bubbleH + 60);

                              return {
                                id: "bubble-" + Date.now() + "-" + index,
                                text: text,
                                x: x,
                                y: y,
                                fontSize: 24,
                                fontFamily: "sans-serif",
                                color: "#000000",
                                isBold: true,
                                isItalic: false,
                                hasOutline: false,
                                rotation: 0,
                                scaleX: 1,
                                scaleY: 1,
                                isSpeechBubble: true,
                                bubbleWidth: bubbleW,
                                bubbleHeight: bubbleH,
                                bubbleTailAlign: index % 2 === 0 ? 'left' : 'right'
                              };
                            });
                            
                            onOpenFrameEditorWithTextLayers(globalIndex, layers);
                          }}
                          className="w-full py-2.5 bg-gradient-to-r from-indigo-600 to-violet-600 hover:from-indigo-500 hover:to-violet-500 text-white rounded text-[10px] uppercase font-black flex items-center justify-center gap-2 transition-all shadow-lg ring-2 ring-violet-500/50 hover:scale-[1.02] active:scale-[0.98] cursor-pointer"
                        >
                          <Layers className="w-4 h-4" />
                          Send to FrameEditor Studio
                        </button>
                      )}
                      
                      <button
                        onClick={handleApplyBubbles}
                        className="w-full py-2 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 rounded text-[10px] uppercase font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 transition-colors border border-neutral-700/50 cursor-pointer"
                      >
                        <CheckCircle2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-emerald-400" />
                        Directly Bake Bubbles to Frame
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  )}
              </>
            );
          })()}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Frame Insertion Panel (bottom) */}
      {showStoryDeckLink && (
        <div className="p-3 border-t border-neutral-850 bg-neutral-900/50 shrink-0">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-[10px] font-black text-neutral-400 uppercase tracking-widest">Story Deck Link</span>
            <span className="text-[9px] font-mono text-neutral-600">{slides.length} Frames Available</span>
          </div>
          
          {slides.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="p-3 border border-dashed border-neutral-800 rounded-lg text-center text-neutral-500 text-[11px]">
              No storyboard slides available.
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="flex gap-2 overflow-x-auto pb-1.5 custom-scrollbar">
              {slides.map((s, index) => {
                const isSelected = s.id === activeSlideId;
                return (
                  <button
                    key={s.id}
                    onClick={() => {
                      onSelectSlideId(s.id);
                      handleInsertFrameTag(s);
                    }}
                    className={`flex-none w-16 group relative border rounded-lg overflow-hidden bg-black transition-all cursor-pointer ${
                      isSelected ? 'border-indigo-500 scale-[1.02]' : 'border-neutral-800 hover:border-neutral-600'
                    }`}
                    title={`Insert [Frame: Scene ${s.sceneNo}, Shot ${s.shotNo}] tag at cursor`}
                  >
                    <div className="aspect-video w-full overflow-hidden relative bg-neutral-900">
                      <img src={s.imageUrl} alt="" className="w-full h-full object-cover" />
                      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/40 group-hover:bg-black/15 transition-all" />
                      <div className="absolute bottom-1 left-1 px-1 bg-black/70 rounded text-[8px] font-mono font-black text-white">
                        S{s.sceneNo}.H{s.shotNo}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="py-0.5 text-center text-[8px] font-extrabold uppercase bg-neutral-950 text-neutral-400 group-hover:text-white truncate">
                      + Insert
                    </div>
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Enhanced Screenplay Writer (AI Writer) toggle */}
      <div className="px-3 py-2 border-t border-neutral-850 bg-neutral-950/90 shrink-0 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <Sparkles className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 ${isAIEnabled ? "text-indigo-400 animate-pulse" : "text-neutral-500"}`} />
          <div className="flex flex-col">
            <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-neutral-300 uppercase tracking-wider">Enhanced AI Screenplay</span>
            <span className="text-[8px] font-medium text-neutral-500">Enable automated AI drafting & shot extraction</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => setIsAIEnabled(!isAIEnabled)}
          className={`relative inline-flex h-4 w-8 shrink-0 cursor-pointer rounded-full border-2 border-transparent transition-colors duration-200 ease-in-out outline-none ${
            isAIEnabled ? "bg-indigo-600" : "bg-neutral-800"
          }`}
          title={isAIEnabled ? "Disable AI Assistant" : "Enable AI Assistant"}
        >
          <span
            className={`pointer-events-none inline-block h-3 w-3 transform rounded-full bg-white shadow ring-0 transition duration-200 ease-in-out ${
              isAIEnabled ? "translate-x-4" : "translate-x-0"
            }`}
          />
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* AI Complexity Level Option (Cycle Button) */}
      {isAIEnabled && (
        <div className="px-3 py-1.5 border-t border-neutral-850 bg-neutral-950/50 shrink-0 flex items-center justify-between text-[11px]">
          <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-neutral-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Detail Level</span>
          <button
            onClick={() => {
              setComplexity(prev => {
                if (prev === 'quick') return 'objects';
                if (prev === 'objects') return 'full';
                return 'quick';
              });
            }}
            className="px-2.5 py-1 bg-neutral-900 hover:bg-neutral-800 text-indigo-400 border border-neutral-800 hover:border-neutral-700 rounded text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-wider transition-colors cursor-pointer flex items-center gap-1.5"
            title="Cycle through detail levels for extraction"
          >
            <RefreshCw className="w-3 h-3 text-neutral-500" />
            <span>
              {complexity === 'quick' && 'quick'}
              {complexity === 'objects' && 'main objects only'}
              {complexity === 'full' && 'full'}
            </span>
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* AI Assistant footer actions */}
      <div className="p-3 border-t border-neutral-850 bg-neutral-950 shrink-0 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
        <button
          onClick={handleAIGenerateScript}
          disabled={!isAIEnabled || isGenerating || slides.length === 0}
          className={`flex items-center justify-center gap-1 py-2 rounded-lg text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider transition-all cursor-pointer shadow-md ${
            isAIEnabled 
              ? "bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white" 
              : "bg-neutral-900 text-neutral-500 border border-neutral-850/60 opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed"
          }`}
          title={!isAIEnabled ? "Toggle Enhanced AI Writer above to enable" : "AI Write Script"}
        >
          {isGenerating ? (
            <RefreshCw className="w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin" />
          ) : (
            <Sparkles className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          )}
          <span>{isGenerating ? 'Writing...' : 'AI Write Script'}</span>
        </button>

        <button
          onClick={handleAIExtractFrames}
          disabled={!isAIEnabled || isExtracting || !scriptText.trim()}
          className={`flex items-center justify-center gap-1 py-2 rounded-lg text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider transition-all cursor-pointer border ${
            isAIEnabled 
              ? "bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-200 border-neutral-700" 
              : "bg-neutral-900 text-neutral-500 border border-neutral-850/60 opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed"
          }`}
          title={!isAIEnabled ? "Toggle Enhanced AI Writer above to enable" : "Use AI to parse script and extract sequential storyboard shots"}
        >
          {isExtracting ? (
            <RefreshCw className="w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin" />
          ) : (
            <Layers className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-indigo-400" />
          )}
          <span>{isExtracting ? 'Extracting...' : 'AI Extract Shots'}</span>
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
-e

export default function App() {
  const [currentThemeId, setCurrentThemeId] = useState<string>(() => {
    return localStorage.getItem('storyboard_theme') || 'cinema';
  });

  const handleSetTheme = (themeId: string) => {
    setCurrentThemeId(themeId);
    localStorage.setItem('storyboard_theme', themeId);
  };

  const [customBgColor, setCustomBgColor] = useState<string>(() => {
    return localStorage.getItem('storyboard_custom_bg') || '';
  });
  const [customTextColor, setCustomTextColor] = useState<string>(() => {
    return localStorage.getItem('storyboard_custom_text') || '#10b981';
  });
  const [showSettingsDropdown, setShowSettingsDropdown] = useState(false);

  const handleSetCustomBgColor = (color: string) => {
    setCustomBgColor(color);
    if (color) {
      localStorage.setItem('storyboard_custom_bg', color);
    } else {
      localStorage.removeItem('storyboard_custom_bg');
    }
  };

  const handleSetCustomTextColor = (color: string) => {
    setCustomTextColor(color);
    if (color) {
      localStorage.setItem('storyboard_custom_text', color);
    } else {
      localStorage.removeItem('storyboard_custom_text');
    }
  };

  const [slides, setSlides] = useState<Slide[]>([]);
  const [showUpload, setShowUpload] = useState(false);
  
  // Image Studio States
  const [showImageStudio, setShowImageStudio] = useState(false);
  const [imageStudioTab, setImageStudioTab] = useState<'enhance' | 'textToImage' | 'sequence'>('enhance');

  // Enhancer States
  const [enhanceImgBase64, setEnhanceImgBase64] = useState<string>('');
  const [enhanceImgMimeType, setEnhanceImgMimeType] = useState<string>('');
  const [enhanceStyle, setEnhanceStyle] = useState<string>('cinematic');
  const [enhanceScaleSize, setEnhanceScaleSize] = useState<string>('2K');
  const [enhancedResultUrl, setEnhancedResultUrl] = useState<string>('');
  const [isEnhancing, setIsEnhancing] = useState(false);

  // Text to Image States
  const [t2iPrompt, setT2iPrompt] = useState('');
  const [t2iAspectRatio, setT2iAspectRatio] = useState('16:9');
  const [t2iImageSize, setT2iImageSize] = useState('1K');
  const [t2iResultUrl, setT2iResultUrl] = useState('');
  const [isGeneratingT2i, setIsGeneratingT2i] = useState(false);

  // Image to Sequence States
  const [seqImgBase64, setSeqImgBase64] = useState<string>('');
  const [seqImgMimeType, setSeqImgMimeType] = useState<string>('');
  const [seqMovementType, setSeqMovementType] = useState<string>('dolly_in');
  const [suggestedSequenceFrames, setSuggestedSequenceFrames] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [isGeneratingSequence, setIsGeneratingSequence] = useState(false);
  const [sequenceFrameVisuals, setSequenceFrameVisuals] = useState<Record<number, string>>({}); // maps shotNo to image URL
  const [isGeneratingFrameVisual, setIsGeneratingFrameVisual] = useState<Record<number, boolean>>({});

  const [editingFrame, setEditingFrame] = useState<{imageUrl: string; index: number; initialTextLayers?: any[]} | null>(null);
  const [editingGridFrame, setEditingGridFrame] = useState<{imageUrl: string; index: number} | null>(null);
  const [showVectorEditOnPanels, setShowVectorEditOnPanels] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [folderName, setFolderName] = useState('My-Storyboard');
  const [storyboardId] = useState('default-storyboard');

  // Density & Screenplay States
  const [viewDensity, setViewDensity] = useState<'full' | 'compact' | 'strip' | 'icon' | 'grid-storyboard'>('strip');
  const [videoDownloadUrlExtension, setVideoDownloadUrlExtension] = useState<string>('mp4');
  const [showScriptEditor, setShowScriptEditor] = useState<boolean>(() => {
    return localStorage.getItem('storyboard_show_script') === 'true';
  });
  const [scriptWriterFullScreen, setScriptWriterFullScreen] = useState(false);
  const [activeSlideId, setActiveSlideId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [currentSlideIndex, setCurrentSlideIndex] = useState(0);

  const handleSelectSlide = (id: string | null) => {
    setActiveSlideId(id);
    if (id) {
      const idx = slides.findIndex(s => s.id === id);
      if (idx !== -1) {
        setCurrentSlideIndex(idx);
      }
    }
  };

  // Sync active slide and current indices unidirectionally to avoid circular resets
  useEffect(() => {
    if (slides.length > 0) {
      let indexToUse = currentSlideIndex;
      if (indexToUse < 0 || indexToUse >= slides.length) {
        indexToUse = 0;
        setCurrentSlideIndex(0);
      }
      const targetId = slides[indexToUse]?.id || null;
      if (targetId && targetId !== activeSlideId) {
        setActiveSlideId(targetId);
      }
    } else {
      if (activeSlideId !== null) {
        setActiveSlideId(null);
      }
    }
  }, [currentSlideIndex, slides, activeSlideId]);

  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('storyboard_density', viewDensity);
  }, [viewDensity]);

  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('storyboard_show_script', String(showScriptEditor));
  }, [showScriptEditor]);

  const [headerDisplayMode, setHeaderDisplayMode] = useState<'icons' | 'text' | 'both'>(() => {
    return (localStorage.getItem('storyboard_header_display_mode') as 'icons' | 'text' | 'both') || 'icons';
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('storyboard_header_display_mode', headerDisplayMode);
  }, [headerDisplayMode]);

  // Sequencer Playback & View States
  const [isPlaying, setIsPlaying] = useState(false);
  const [transitionStyle, setTransitionStyle] = useState<TransitionStyle>('none');
  const [activeLayout, setActiveLayout] = useState<'grid' | 'spreadsheet' | 'player'>('grid');
  const [selectedAspectRatio, setSelectedAspectRatio] = useState<AspectRatioKey>('16:9');
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
  const [colorFilter, setColorFilter] = useState<string>('all');
  const [enableBeeps, setEnableBeeps] = useState(true);
  const [isLooping, setIsLooping] = useState(false);
  const [showFilmstrip, setShowFilmstrip] = useState(true);
  const [showAddBlankDropdown, setShowAddBlankDropdown] = useState(false);
  const [fullscreenPlayer, setFullscreenPlayer] = useState(false);
  const [sidebarTab, setSidebarTab] = useState<'filmstrip' | 'tracks'>('filmstrip');
  const [activePlaybackTrackId, setActivePlaybackTrackId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [enableTransitionSpeed, setEnableTransitionSpeed] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [playbackTimingMode, setPlaybackTimingMode] = useState<'duration' | 'fps'>('fps');
  const [playbackFps, setPlaybackFps] = useState<number>(30);

  // Selection & Drag/Drop states for List Sequencer
  const [selectedSlideIds, setSelectedSlideIds] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [draggedIndex, setDraggedIndex] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const [dragOverIndex, setDragOverIndex] = useState<number | null>(null);

  // Triple Zoom Variations
  const [zoomVariationsSource, setZoomVariationsSource] = useState<Slide | null>(null);
  const [zoomRatios, setZoomRatios] = useState<[number, number, number]>([1.2, 1.8, 2.5]);
  const [zoomPanOffsets, setZoomPanOffsets] = useState<Array<{ x: number; y: number }>>([{ x: 0, y: 0 }, { x: 0, y: 0 }, { x: 0, y: 0 }]);
  const [draggingIdx, setDraggingIdx] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const dragStartRef = useRef<{ x: number; y: number } | null>(null);
  const panStartRef = useRef<{ x: number; y: number } | null>(null);

  // Print / PDF Export states
  const [showPrintPreview, setShowPrintPreview] = useState(false);
  const [printTitle, setPrintTitle] = useState('');
  const [printAuthor, setPrintAuthor] = useState('');
  const [printLayout, setPrintLayout] = useState<'grid' | 'list'>('grid');
